{1 pratijñāsūtra PJS}

    1. viśuddhajñānadehāya trivedīdivyacakṣuṣe |
    2. śreyaḥprāptinimittāya namaḥ somārdhadhāriṇe ||
    1. abhivandya gurūnādau śiṣyadhīpadminīravīn |
    2. tatprasādāt kariṣye 'haṃ mīmāṃsāślokavārttikaṃ ||
    1. tadvidvāṃso 'nugṛhṇantu cittaśrotraiḥ prasādibhiḥ |
    2. santaḥ praṇayivākyāni gṛhṇanti hy anasūyavaḥ ||
    1. na cātrātiva kartavyaṃ doṣadṛṣṭiparaṃ manaḥ |
    2. doṣo hy avidyamāno 'pi taccittānāṃ prakāśate ||
    1. kuto vā gṛhṇate doṣaṃ sūrayo madvidhoktiṣu |
    2. neṣyate yaḥ parastho 'pi sa svayaṃ gṛhyate katham ||
    1. nirdoṣatvaikavākyatvaṃ kva vā lokasya dṛśyate |
    2. sāpavādā yataḥ ke cin mokṣasvargāv api prati ||
    1. āgamapravaṇaś cāhaṃ nāpavādyaḥ skhaliteṣv apy apodyate |
    2. na hi sadvartmanā gacchan skhaliteṣv apy apodyate ||
    1. yathā kathañ cid ārabdhā trayīmārgānusāriṇī |
    2. vāgvṛttir alpasārāpi śraddadhānasya śobhate ||
    1. mīmāṃsāśāstratejobhir viśeṣeṇoj jvalīkṛte |
    2. vedārthajñānaratne me tṛṣṇātīva vijṛmbhate ||
    1. prāyenaiva hi mīmāṃsā loke lokāyatīkṛtā |
    2. tāmāstikapathe kartum ayaṃ yatnaḥ kṛto mayā ||
    1. athāto dharmajijñāsā sūtram ādyam idaṃ kṛtam |
    2. dharmākhyaṃ viṣayaṃ vaktuṃ mīmāṃsāyāḥ prayojanam ||
    1. sarvasyaiva hi śāstrasya karmaṇo vāpi kasya cit |
    2. yāvat prayojanaṃ noktaṃ tāvat tat kena gṛhyate ||
    1. mīmāṃsākhyā tu vidyeyaṃ bahuvidyāntarāśritā |
    2. na śuśrūṣayituṃ śakyā prāganuktvā prayojanam ||
    1. vidyāntareṣu nāpy etad yady abhīṣṭaṃ prayojanam |
    2. anarthaprāpaṇaṃ tāvat tebhyo nāśaṅkyate kva cit ||
    1. mīmāṃsāyāṃ tv ihājñāte durjñāte vāvivekataḥ |
    2. nyāyamārge mahān doṣa iti yatnopacaryatā ||
    1. tasmāt prayojanaṃ pūrvam uktaṃ sūtrakṛtā svayam |
    2. yat svenoktaṃ vadeyus tad bhāṣyakārādayaḥ katham ||
    1. siddhārthaṃ jñātasambandhaṃ śrotuṃ śrotā pravartate |
    2. śāstrādau tena vaktavyaḥ sambandhaḥ saprayojanaḥ ||
    1. śāstraṃ prayojanaṃ caiva sambandhasyāśrayāv ubhau |
    2. taduktyantargatas tasmād bhinno noktaḥ prayojanāt ||
    1. siddhiḥ śrotṛpravṛttīnāṃ sambandhakathanād yataḥ |
    2. tasmāt sarveṣu śāstreṣu sambandhaḥ pūrvam ucyate ||
    1. yāvat prayojanenāsya sambandho nābhidhīyate |
    2. asambaddhapralāpitvād bhavet tāvad asaṃgatiḥ ||
    1. iha tv ākṣipya sambandhaṃ bhāṣya evābhidhāsyate |
    2. dharmaprasiddhyasiddhibhyāṃ, tasmān nānyo 'bhidhīyate ||
    1. na cāpy atrāthaśabdena śāstrasambandha ucyate |
    2. sambandhaṃ kriyayor hy eṣa brūte śāstrāc ca te pṛthak ||
    1. yo 'py ayaṃ śāstrasambandho varṇyate kaiś cid āditaḥ |
    2. kriyānantaryarūpo vā guruparvakramo 'pi vā ||
    1. sadasadbhāvayos tasya viśeṣo nopalabhyate |
    2. śrotuvidhau niṣedhe vā jñāne vā śāstragocare ||
    1. tasmād vyākhyāṅgam icchadbhiḥ sahetuḥ saprayojanaḥ |
    2. śāstrāvatārasambandho vācyo nānyas tu niṣphalaḥ ||
    1. loke ityādibhāṣyasya ṣaḍarthān sampracakṣate |
    2. bhāṣyakārānusāreṇa, prayuktasyāditaḥ pṛthak ||
    1. sarvavyākhyām upālambhaṃ pratyākhyānaṃ tathā pare |
    2. parisaṃkhyās tutī kecithaśabdasya dūṣaṇam ||
    1. sādhāraṇī viśiṣṭā ca sūtravyākhyā dvidhā matā |
    2. viśiṣṭā pratisūtraṃ yā sarvārthā tv iyam ucyate ||
    1. pravṛttis tu padeṣv eva nivṛttiḥ sūtrasaṃśrayā |
    2. vedavākyāviruddheṣu na tu sarveṣu keṣu cit ||
    1. adhyāhārasya vākyeṣu vyatyāsasya ca sambhavāt |
    2. tenaiṣām iti sūtrāṇāṃ pārārthye saty api grahaḥ ||
    1. evaśabdo 'lpavācyatvād, asyāvṛttau tu gauravam |
    2. prasiddhatvād avācyaṃ cet, na doṣaḥ puṅgirām ayam ||
    1. vyākhyāṅgatvābhimānena yo 'dhyāhārādyapekṣate |
    2. svasaṃjñāṃ vāpi tasyedaṃ śāstrarūpaṃ nirūpyate ||
    1. vṛtyantareṣu keṣāñ cil laukikārthavyatikramaḥ |
    2. śabdānāṃ dṛśyate teṣam upālambho 'yam ucyate ||
    1. athāta ity ayaṃ loke nānantarye prayujyate |
    2. tasmāt tādarthyam etasya paribhāṣādibhir bhavet ||
    1. prasiddhahāniḥ śabdānām aprasiddhe ca kalpanā |
    2. na kāryā vṛttikāreṇa sati siddhārthasambhave ||
    1. sūtrārthe kliśyataś caivaṃ dūre vedārthanirṇayaḥ |
    2. tatra yatnasya bhāratvaṃ vaktṛśrotroḥ prasajyate ||
    1. na vyākhyāsyati sūtrāṇi codanārthaparatvataḥ |
    2. yat tasya parihāro 'yaṃ pratyākhyānena cocyate ||
    1. prayāso vedavākyeṣu kāryaḥ sūtreṣv anena kim |
    2. phalavattvāphalatvābhyām, ebhiḥ karaṇasammataiḥ ||
    1. codanārtha upetavyaḥ, nobhayaṃ yatnagauravāt |
    2. padārthānāṃ prasiddhatvāt vyākhyeyaṃ nāvaśiṣyate ||
    1. evaṃśabdādiko granthaḥ pakṣe cāsmin samarthyate |
    2. padacchedadādyabhāvena pratyākhyānamatis tv iyam ||
    1. brabīty eva hi sūtrārtham, atiriktādi ceṣyate |
    2. nanv aśaktam idaṃ sūtraṃ samyak sūtritam ity api ||
    1. sūtre cāgamakatvādi pratyākhyāne virudhyate |
    2. na copāyānabhijñena śakyopeyāvadhāraṇā ||
    1. nānyato vedavidbhyaś ca sūtravṛttikriyeṣyate |
    2. pratyākhyānasya hetuś ca padārthānāṃ prasiddhatā ||
    1. yoktā sā vedavākyānaṃ tulyārthatvān nivārayet |
    2. vākyārthe tatra sandehād vyākhyānaṃ cet pravartate ||
    1. sūtreṣv api samānatvāt pratyākhyānaṃ na yujyate |
    2. na vyākhyātavyam ityevaṃ pratyākhyāne ca sidhyati ||
    1. duṣṭavyākhyā niṣedhena tadapetā na vāryate |
    2. asya dṛṣṭaviruddhatvāt phalgutvāc cāpi parvayoḥ ||
    1. madhyame cātidaurjanyāt parisaṃkhyaiva yujyate |
    2. vaidikaṃ jaiminīyaṃ ca yatra vākyaṃ virudhyate ||
    1. yathāśrutagṛhīte 'rthe tatredam upadiśyate |
    2. adhyāhārādibhiḥ sūtraṃ vaidikaṃ tu yathāśrutam ||
    1. neyam, virodhe 'nyonyasya vaidikānāṃ bhavantu te |
    2. yathā dharmāvabodhasya pramāṇaṃ vaidikaṃ vacaḥ ||
    1. tadarthanirṇaye hetur jaiminīyaṃ tathaiva naḥ |
    2. vākyasāmarthyatulyatvāt tathā padatadarthayoḥ ||
    1. adhyāhārādibhir muktā vyākhyā sarvatra yujyate |
    2. asambhavād avaśyaṃ yā virodhe 'nyatarasya tu ||
    1. anyāyyakalpanā sāpi vikalpena prasajyate |
    2. prāthamyenāvaruddhatvād upāyavaśato 'tha vā ||
    1. yathāśrutena sūtreṇa nyāyyāṃ bādheta codanām |
    2. tena vedāviruddhasya sati sambhava ity ayam ||
    1. vidhīyate 'rthaḥ, śeṣaṃ tu yathāprāptam anūdyate |
    2. śeṣabhājāṃ bhavel lopa ity adhyāhārakalpanā ||
    1. viprakarṣāt paśoś ceti vibhaktiḥ pariṇamyate |
    2. padena vyavadhānaṃ tu loke saṃniyamād iti ||
    1. sūtreṇa vyavadhānaṃ tu pānavyāpadi kalpitam |
    2. paśusāmānyavidhyādau sūtram evānyathā kṛtam ||
    1. agnayaś ca svakālatvād deyadharmāpayātanam |
    2. vyākhyānaṃ vākyabhedena, guṇakalpās tv amī kṛtāḥ ||
    1. autpattikas tu gavyasya tathoṣṇikkakubhor iti |
    2. darśanāc ca viśeṣasya tathābhyudaya ity api ||
    1. sūtrakārapraśaṃsā vā loka ityādinocyate |
    2. prasiddhair abhidhānād dhi na śiṣyāḥ kleśitā yataḥ ||
    1. bhavitavyaṃ tu teneti prāgasmād ekavākyatā |
    2. vedādhyayanavākyād vā tenāthety asya dūṣaṇam ||
    1. prasiddhārthapadaiḥ śakyaḥ sūtrair vedārthanirṇayaḥ |
    2. na ca so 'sty athaśabdasya vinā te pūrvakarmaṇā ||
    1. prasiddhārthaṃ padaṃ yuktaṃ tac ca nāstīti dūṣaṇam |
    2. prasiddho 'py athaśabdādeḥ kiṃpadārtho 'tra varṇyate ||
    1. pradarśanārtham ity eke, ke cin nānārthavācinaḥ |
    2. samudāyād avacchidya bhavadāsena kalpitāt ||
    1. śaktito 'vayavaṃ caiva varṇayantyaṣṭamādivat |
    2. na cātra codanāvyākhyā gauravaṃ tatra coditam ||
    1. yad vākṣepo yathoktasya vṛttābhāvād asambhavāt |
    2. yadi lokaprasiddhārthagrahaṇaṃ kriyate pade ||
    1. sa nāsty atrāthaśabdasyety adhyāhārādikalpanam |
    2. vedādhyayanavṛttatvaṃ snānasyotkarṣakalpanā ||
    1. nāvyākhyāte 'thaśabdārthe jñāyate tena varṇyate |
    2. anarthake 'tha vānyārthe prasiddhir bādhyate dhruvam ||
    1. tasmāc chrutārthasiddhyarthaṃ vṛttaṃ kim api gamyate |
    2. viśiṣṭaliṅgavijñānād viśiṣṭe liṅginīkṣite ||
    1. sūtreṇāsambhavaṃ matvā naitad ity abravīt paraḥ |
    2. ānantaryopadeśena taddṛṣṭārthatayāpi ca ||
    1. vedādhyayanam ākṣiptaṃ kim asūtritacodanā |
    2. yena vṛttena jijñāsā vinā naivopapadyate ||
    1. tadānantaryam uktaṃ hi dṛṣṭārtham avakalpate |
    2. kriyamāṇā ca jijñāsā niyamād yasya kasya cit ||
    1. kriyetānantaraiveti vyarthaṃ tadupadeśanam |
    2. saṅkalpādibhir apy eṣā vinā satyaṃ na sidhyati ||
    1. sādhāraṇyāt tu te 'py atra nopadeśyāḥ kathañ cana |
    2. tasmād dharmabubhutsāyām asādhāraṇakāraṇam ||
    1. nirvṛttaṃ sūtrakāreṣṭaṃ tac ca nākhyayanād ṛte |
    2. anyasyāpīty anenaiva vedapāṭhe prabādhite ||
    1. prāg apīti hi vaktavyaṃ tatrāpy anyasya sambhavāt |
    2. pūrveṇaiva hi labdhārthe tādṛśīṃ tv ity anena kim ||
    1. vakṣyamāṇam anālocya sambhavet paricodanā |
    2. na tāvat sādhyate 'dyāpi codanā dharmasādhanam ||
    1. iha vā kāni vākyāni vivariṣyati jaiminiḥ |
    2. dharmamātrābhidhānād dhi buddhādivacanāny api ||
    1. paṭhitvā dharmajijñāsety anyasyāpīti codanā |
    2. yad vā bhavatu nāmedṛk sūtraṃ vedam adhītya tu ||
    1. jijñāsānantaraṃ kāryety atrāpi dvayam īpsitam |
    2. nānadhītya na cāpy anyat kṛtvety etan na labhyate ||
    1. vakṣyamāṇavacobhaṅgyor vākyabhedaprasaṅgataḥ |
    2. adhītyaiveti hi vidhau snānāder apy anantarā ||
    1. bhaved dharmasya jijñāsā nānantaryavidhis tadā |
    2. ānantaryavidhāne tu yā vedādhyayane kṛte ||
    1. ity evam anuvādatvāt prāg apy eṣā prasajyate |
    2. buddhavākyādipāṭhasya tādṛśīṃ tv ity apākriyā ||
    1. prāg apīti ca codyasya, sāmarthyād vedalābhataḥ |
    2. naivaitayor vacobhaṅgyor eko 'py artho vidhīyate ||
    1. api cetyādikenoktam, kin tv ityetad vidhīyate |
    2. ānantaryaṃ parastāc ca nāpi śiṃṣma itīha tu ||
    1. ke cid adhyāharanti, asya sūtrasyānyaparatvataḥ |
    2. na vāryate 'nadhītatvaṃ nānantaryaṃ vidhīyate ||
    1. sāmarthyāsiddhyadṛṣṭārthaprasaṅgāt tena lakṣaṇā |
    2. ānantaryavacovyaktir āśritaivātra lakṣyate ||
    1. śrutārthaṃ tv aparityajya lakṣaṇārtho vidhīyate |
    2. pratītā dharmajiñāsā vedādhyāyād anantarā ||
    1. tatkālasyāvaruddhatvāt snānābhāvaṃ hi lakṣayet |
    2. virodho yugapatprāpteḥ, daurbalyaṃ vedabādhanāt ||
    1. snānasya tena bādhaḥ syād dharmajijñāsayā balāt |
    2. dṛṣṭārthatvādisaṃyuktaṃ vākyaṃ lakṣaṇayā tv iti ||
    1. punaruktyā gatārthatvāt tyaktaṃ kaiś cit, tad ucyate |
    2. yady apy asya bhaved vācyam ānantaryam asaṃśayam ||
    1. tathāpi pūrvatāmātraṃ lakṣayed avirodhataḥ |
    2. granthagrahaṇamātre ca kṛte snānaṃ virudhyate ||
    1. adhītyetyadhigamyeti vyākhyāne tv avirodhitā |
    2. yas tv evamavirodhitvaṃ kurvannāplavanaṃ vadet ||
    1. adṛṣṭāyātha vāpy anyaḥ saṃskāraṃ tasya cottaram |
    2. ihāsnānādiniyamo yaḥ kṛto brahmacāriṇaḥ ||
    1. avidhitvam anāśritya so 'vasānam apekṣate |
    2. tato 'pekṣāvaśāt snānam asnānādinivartanam ||
    1. virodhasāhacaryābhyāṃ dṛṣṭārthatvena lakṣayet |
    2. tasmād adhyayanasnānajijñāsākramavācinām ||
    1. dṛṣṭārthatvāya śabdānām evaṃ vyākhyeyam āśritā |
    2. snātvā jijñāsamāno 'pi nanu vedaṃ na bādhate ||
    1. tenāvirodhitā tasya, ityevaṃ vadata uttaram |
    2. yathaivādhyayanāt snānaṃ smaryate samanantaram ||
    1. tathā tataḥ paro 'py anyaḥ padārtho 'nyaḥ paras tataḥ |
    2. tataś cāvaśyakartavye bādhe smārtasya kasya cit ||
    1. yogyatvād āgate kāle prāthamyāt snānabādhanam |
    2. so 'yaṃ pāṭhakramasyārthād bādha ity avagamyate ||
    1. guṇapradhānayor vāpi virodhād guṇabādhanam |
    2. snānopalakṣitā cātra nivṛttir guruveśmanaḥ ||
    1. virodhitvena bādhyeta na tu madhvādibhakṣaṇam |
    2. tasmād gurukule tiṣṭhanmadhumāṃsādyavarjayan ||
    1. jijñāsetāviruddhatvād dharmam ity avagamyate |
    2. gurugehanivṛttyaṃśo yāvac ca na samāpyate ||
    1. tāvat sakalavācitvān na snānaṃ paryavasyati |
    2. gurugehādanāvṛttaḥ snātako hi na kathyate ||
    1. tatparatvavidhānāc ca na tāvad dārasaṅgrahaḥ |
    2. vyākhyāya kīrtitā cātra snāyād iti punaḥ smṛtiḥ ||
    1. smāvartiṣṭa metyādi smṛter yady apy anantaram |
    2. viparītārtham ity asmāt tadvākyād apanīyate ||
    1. athaśabdena yo bādhaḥ purastād upavarṇitaḥ |
    2. tanmātrasyaiva bādho 'tra dṛṣṭārthatvāt pradarśitaḥ ||
    1. smṛtiprāptam idānīṃ tu madhumāṃsādyavarjanam |
    2. pratiṣedhann adṛṣṭārthaṃ sūtrakāro na śobhate ||
    1. nivṛttya gurugehāc ca jijñāsārthaḥ punar bhavet |
    2. praveśaḥ so 'py adṛṣṭārtha iti naiveha sūtritaḥ ||
    1. nirgamo hi kṛtārthasya dṛṣṭārtho guruveśmanaḥ |
    2. smaryate tasya nārthaḥ syād akṛtārthasya nirgame ||
    1. athaśabdaprasiddhyaiva vedagrahaṇahetutā |
    2. ānantaryopadeśitvād ataḥ śabdena kiṃ punaḥ ||
    1. yogyatvam athaśabdena yady api pratipāditam |
    2. tad eva hetur atreti nātaḥśabdād vinā bhavet ||
    1. lakṣaṇaṃ puruṣasyaiva tadā tad dhi prasajyate |
    2. jijñāsāyāś ca hetutve phalārthatvādi sambhavet ||
    1. ataḥśabdagṛhītaṃ vā tatrādhyayanam āśritam |
    2. hetāvakathyamāne hi maṅgalādy apy asau vadet ||
    1. snānabādhasya vā hetur ata ity ucyate punaḥ |
    2. yogyasyādhītavedatvān nāvasthātuṃ hi labhyate ||
    1. sanvācyecchāntaraṃ karma jñānaṃ vyāpnoti tāvatā |
    2. jñānopasarjanā saiva na tu vidhyādi gamyate ||
    1. iṣes tu karma bāhyaḥ syād dharmaḥ sā vātha vā dvayam |
    2. samānakartṛkatvaṃ tu tumunoktaṃ liṅā vidhiḥ ||
    1. evaṃ viṣayanānātvān na kā cit punaruktatā |
    2. sūtritecchābhinirvṛttyai dvitīyecchātra sūtritā ||
    1. prakṛtyā vikṛtir yasmāc caturthyantā samasyate |
    2. tādarthye yūpadārvādau tenāsminn asamāsatā ||
    1. sa hi tasyety anenokto dharmasyety eṣa vigrahaḥ |
    2. dharmāyeti tu tādarthye ṣaṣṭhī vṛtteti kathyate ||
    1. prāpnoty atra caturthy eva viśeṣaś ced vivakṣitaḥ |
    2. sāmānyasya vivakṣāyāṃ tādṛśaṃ kathyate katham ||
    1. sambandhamātra evaiṣā ṣaṣṭhyutpannā tathāpi tu |
    2. viśeṣaniṣṭhatā tasyā bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇyate ||
    1. sādhanābhāsatā cātra pūrvapakṣārthagocarā |
    2. anyasādhanam anyasya sādhanābhāsa ucyate ||
    1. kratvarthaṃ puruṣārthasya tadarthaṃ ca krator iti |
    2. śeṣalakṣaṇaśabdaś ca kṛtsnaśāstravivakṣayā ||
    1. prasiddhaḥ śakyate jñātum prasiddhatvāt tu neṣyate |
    2. aprasiddhas tv aśakyatvānnatarām ity ato 'bravīt ||
    1. jijñāsyaḥ saṃśayād dharmaḥ śreyaskaratayāpi ca |
    2. asandigdho hy ajijñāsyo yo vā syān niṣprayojanaḥ ||
    1. svarūpādiṣu dharmasya dvidhā vipratipadyate |
    2. pūrvaṃ pramāṇarūpābhyām, pādenādyasya nirṇayaḥ ||
    1. sthite vedapramāṇatve punar vākyārthanirṇaye |
    2. matir bahuvidāṃ puṃsāṃ saṃśayān nopajāyate ||
    1. ke cid āhur asāv arthaḥ, ke cin nāsāv ayaṃ tv iti |
    2. tannirṇayārtham apy etat paraṃ śāstraṃ praṇīyate ||

{2 codanāsūtra CDS}

    1. dharme sāmānyataḥ siddhe pramāṇaṃ codanocyate |
    2. svarūpādes tataḥ siddhaḥ, svarūpaṃ ceha sūtryate ||
    1. dvayam ekena sūtreṇa śrutyarthābhyāṃ nirūpyate |
    2. svarūpe 'pi hi tasyokte pramāṇaṃ kathyate 'rthataḥ ||
    1. kimādyapekṣitaiḥ pūrṇaḥ samarthaḥ pratyayo vidhau |
    2. tena pravartakaṃ vākyaṃ śāstre 'smin codanocyate ||
    1. codanaiva pramāṇaṃ cetyetaddharme 'vadhāritam |
    2. sākāṅkṣam iti manvāno yuktileśaṃ dvaye 'spṛśat ||
    1. sambhāvyate pramāṇatvaṃ śabdasyaivaṃvidheṣv api |
    2. indriyāder asāmarthyaṃ vakṣyamāṇamadīdiśat ||
    1. atyantāsaty api jñānam arthe śabdaḥ karoti hi |
    2. tenotsarge sthite tasya doṣābhāvāt pramāṇatā ||
    1. codanety abravīc cātra śabdamātravivakṣayā |
    2. na hi bhūtādiviṣayaḥ kaś cid asti vidhāyakaḥ ||
    1. indriyādivyudāsena śabdo yāvan na sādhyate |
    2. tāvac ca tadviśeṣasya kuto vāvasaro bhavet ||
    1. nimittamātraṃ vocyeta pramāṇaṃ ceha lakṣaṇam |
    2. pramāṇaṃ tv api śabdo vā tajjñānaṃ vā nirūpyate |
    1. padārthas tanmatir vā syād vākyārthādhigamo 'pi vā |
    2. pūrveṣāṃ tu pramāṇatve phalatvaṃ tasya gamyate ||
    1. jñāne lakṣaṇaśabdo 'yaṃ yadi nāma prayujyate |
    2. codanoktis tadā kāryaṃ tatkāryaṃ cāpi lakṣayet ||
    1. nimittamātre śabde ca pramāṇe mukhyavṛttayoḥ |
    2. sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ syāc codanālakṣaṇatvayoḥ ||
    1. dravyakriyāguṇādīnāṃ dharmatvaṃ sthāpayiṣyate |
    2. teṣām aindriyakatve 'pi na tādrūpyeṇa dharmatā ||
    1. śreyaḥsādhanatā hy eṣāṃ nityaṃ vedāt pratīyate |
    2. tādrūpyeṇa ca dharmatvaṃ tasmān nendriyagocaraḥ ||
    1. pradarśanārtham atroktam indriyaṃ sūtrakāravat |
    2. nānyat kiñ ceti vācchedaḥ sāmānyārthaḥ prayujyate ||
    1. tadasāmarthyasiddhyai ca punar indriyakīrtanam |
    2. kiñ ceti madhyam acchedo hetupraśne prayujyate ||
    1. yady api tv anumānasyāpy evamādau samarthatā |
    2. vinā sambandhabodhena na tu tasyodbhavaḥ kva cit |
    1. na sāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ dharmasambandhadarśanam |
    2. liṅgasya kasya cit siddhaṃ yena syād anumānatā ||
    1. nanu śabdo 'pi sambandhabodhānnarte pravarttate |
    2. padaṃ tat, na ca tadvācyo dharmaḥ, vākyārtha eva saḥ ||
    1. vākyasyāvācakatvaṃ ca, padārthānāṃ ca hetutā |
    2. sambandhasyānapekṣāṇāṃ vākyārthe sthāpayiṣyate ||
    1. nityatvāder asiddhatvād, abhyupetyocyate 'tha vā |
    2. sutarām apramāṇatvaṃ vaktṛprāmāṇyavarjanāt ||
    1. pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭaṃ hi śabdo 'rthaṃ prāpayet sadā |
    2. smṛtivac ca svayaṃ tasya prāmāṇyaṃ nopapadyate ||
    1. nūnaṃ tatrānubhūto 'sāvityāptoktinibandhanā |
    2. buddhiḥ sākṣād adṛṣṭe 'pi yuktārthe puruṣoktitaḥ ||
    1. nātmīyād anyadīyād vā pratyakṣāder vinā kva cit |
    2. vacasaḥ satyatā dṛṣṭā tathā syāc codanāsv api ||
    1. tena saty api vijñāne pratijñāder yathaiva hi |
    2. svātantryān na pramāṇatvaṃ tathā vede 'pi dṛśyatām ||
    1. svargayāgādisambandhaviṣayā codanā mṛṣā |
    2. pratyakṣādyagatārthatvādīdṛgbuddhādivākyavat ||
    1. yad vāptenāpraṇītatvād bālonmattādivākyavat |
    2. vyomādivac ca nityatvāt prāmāṇyasya nirākṛtiḥ ||
    1. yadi vā puruṣādhīnaprāmāṇyāḥ sarvacodanāḥ |
    2. svato vā na pramāṇaṃ syur vākyatvāt puruṣoktivat ||
    1. prāmāṇyaṃ vā narāpekṣaṃ sarvaśabdeṣu gamyatām |
    2. śabdaiḥ sambandhyamānatvād apramāṇyaṃ tathaiva hi |
    1. na syād vaktṛguṇānāṃ ced vacaḥ prāmāṇyahetutā |
    2. taddoṣair apramāṇatvaṃ kim ity asya bhaviṣyati ||
    1. evaṃ sthite tu vedasya sati vāsati vā nare |
    2. prāmāṇyaṃ durlabhaṃ matvā nanv ity etadacūcudat |
    1. tatra vipratiṣiddhatvaṃ buddhavākye 'pi yujyate |
    2. tato 'pi pratyayotpattes tasmāj jātyuttaraṃ tv idam ||
    1. sarvavijñānaviṣayam idaṃ tāvat parīkṣyatām |
    2. pramāṇatvāpramāṇatve svataḥ kiṃ parato 'tha vā ||
    1. svato 'satām asādhyatvāt ke cid āhur dvayaṃ svataḥ |
    2. apare kāraṇotpannaguṇadoṣāvadhāraṇāt ||
    1. svatas tāvad dvayaṃ nāsti, virodhāt, parato na ca |
    2. niḥsvabhāvatvam evaṃ hi jñānarūpe prasajyate |
    1. kathaṃ hy anyānapekṣasya viparītātmasambhavaḥ |
    2. kimātmakaṃ bhavet tac ca svabhāvadvayavarjitam |
    1. vijñānavyaktibhedena bhavec ced aviruddhatā |
    2. tathāpy anyānapekṣatve kiṃ kveti na nirūpyate ||
    1. tasmāt svābhāvikaṃ teṣām apramāṇatvam iṣyatām |
    2. prāmāṇyañ ca parāpekṣam, atra nyāyo 'bhidhīyate ||
    1. aprāmānyam avastutvān na syāt kāraṇadoṣataḥ |
    2. vastutvāt tu guṇais teṣāṃ prāmāṇyam upajanyate ||
    1. prāmāṇyaṃ hi yadotsargāt tadabhāvo 'tha kṛtrimaḥ |
    2. tadā svapnādibodhe 'pi prāmāṇyaṃ kena vāryate ||
    1. matpakṣe kāraṇābhāvāt prāmānyaṃ nopajāyate |
    2. hetumattvaprasaṅgo 'to na bhaviṣyaty avastunaḥ ||
    1. indriyādiguṇāś cāsya kāraṇam, tadasad dvidhā |
    2. duṣṭatvād indriyādīnām abhāve 'nyatamasya vā |
    1. ata eva ca vo bhrāntir doṣair mithyātvadhīr iti |
    2. tadvyāptes tu guṇābhāvas tatkṛtā hy apramāṇatā ||
    1. tasmāt kāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ jñānaprāmāṇyakāraṇam |
    2. svabhāvato 'pramāṇatvaṃ tadabhāvena lakṣyate |
    1. anvayavyatirekābhyām aprāmāṇyaṃ na doṣataḥ |
    2. nājñāne dṛśyate hy etatkāraṇābhāvahetuke ||
    1. tataś ca puruṣābhāvāt sati vā śuddhyasambhavāt |
    2. nirmūlatvāt pramāṇatvaṃ codanāyāṃ na yujyate ||
    1. svataḥ sarvapramāṇānāṃ prāmāṇyam iti gamyatām |
    2. na hi svato 'satī śaktiḥ kartum anyena śakyate ||
    1. ātmalābhe ca bhāvānāṃ kāraṇāpekṣatā bhavet |
    2. labdhātmanāṃ svakāryeṣu pravṛttiḥ svayam eva tu |
    1. jāte 'pi yadi vijñāne tāvan nārtho 'vadhāryate |
    2. yāvatkāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ na pramāṇāntarād bhavet ||
    1. tatra jñānāntarotpādaḥ pratīkṣyaḥ kāraṇāntarāt |
    2. yāvad dhi na paricchinnā śuddhis tāvad asatsamā ||
    1. tasyāpi kāraṇe śuddhe tajjñāne syāt pramāṇatā |
    2. tasyāpy evam itīcchaś ca na kva cid vyavatiṣṭhate ||
    1. yadā svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ tadānyan naiva gṛhyate |
    2. nivarttatte hi mithyātvaṃ doṣājñānād ayatnataḥ ||
    1. tasmād bodhātmakatvena prāptā buddheḥ pramāṇatā |
    2. arthānyathātvahetūtthadoṣajñānād apodyate ||
    1. aprāmāṇyaṃ tridhā bhinnaṃ mithyātvājñānasaṃśayaiḥ |
    2. vastutvād dvividhasyātra sambhavo duṣṭakāraṇāt ||
    1. avijñāne tu doṣāṇāṃ vyāpāro naiva kalpyate |
    2. kāraṇābhāvatas tv eva tatsiddhaṃ nastvaduktivat ||
    1. doṣataś cāpramāṇatve svataḥprāmāṇyavādinām |
    2. guṇajñānānavasthāvan na doṣeṣu prasajyate ||
    1. sākṣād viparyayajñānāl laghvyeva tv apramāṇatā |
    2. pūrvābādhena notpattir uttarasya hi sidhyati ||
    1. duṣṭakāraṇabodhe tu siddhe 'pi viṣayāntare |
    2. arthāt tulyārthatāṃ prāpya bādho godohanādivat ||
    1. tatra doṣāntarajñānaṃ bādhadhīr vā parā na cet |
    2. tadudbhūtau dvitīyasya mithyātvād ādyamānatā ||
    1. svata eva hi tatrāpi doṣājñānāt pramāṇatā |
    2. doṣajñāne tv anutpanne na śaṅkyā niṣpramāṇatā ||
    1. evaṃ tricaturajñānajanmano nādhikā matiḥ |
    2. prārthyate tāvataivaikaṃ svataḥ prāmāṇyam aśnute ||
    1. śabde doṣodbhavas tāvad vaktradhīna iti sthitiḥ |
    2. tadabhāvaḥ kva cit tāvad guṇavadvaktṛkatvataḥ |
    1. tadguṇair apakṛṣṭānāṃ śabde saṃkrāntyasambhavāt |
    2. yadā vaktur abhāvena na syur doṣā nirāśrayāḥ |
    1. pauruṣeye dvayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ doṣābhāvo guṇās tathā |
    2. prāmāṇyaṃ tatra guṇato naiva syād ity udāhṛtam ||
    1. tasmād guṇebhyo doṣāṇām abhāvas tadabhāvataḥ |
    2. aprāmāṇyadvayāsattvaṃ tenotsargo 'napoditaḥ ||
    1. pratyayotpattihetutvāt prāmāṇyaṃ nāpanīyate |
    2. doṣābhāvo guṇebhyaś cen nanu saivāsthitir bhavet ||
    1. tadā tu vyāpriyante hi jñāyamānatayā guṇāḥ |
    2. doṣābhāve tu vijñeye sattāmātropakāriṇaḥ ||
    1. tatrāpavādanirmuktir vaktrabhāvāl laghīyasī |
    2. vede tenāpramāṇatvaṃ nāśaṅkām api gacchati ||
    1. ato vaktranadhīnatvāt prāmāṇye tadupāsanam |
    2. na yuktam, apramāṇatve kalpye tatprārthanā bhavet ||
    1. tataś cāptāpraṇītatvaṃ na doṣāyātra jāyate |
    2. prayogāṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ vakṣyāmaḥ pratisādhanam ||
    1. pauruṣeye tu vacane pramāṇāntaramūlatā |
    2. tadabhāve hi tad duṣyeditaran na kadā cana |
    1. tenetaraiḥ pramāṇair yā codanānām asaṅgatiḥ |
    2. tayaiva syāt pramāṇatvam anuvādatvam anyathā ||
    1. anyasyāpi pramāṇatve saṅgatir naiva kāraṇam |
    2. tulyārthānāṃ vikalpyatvād ekaṃ tatra hi bodhakam ||
    1. yatrāpi syāt paricchedaḥ pramāṇair uttaraiḥ punaḥ |
    2. nūnaṃ tatrāpi pūrveṇa so 'rtho nāvadhṛtas tathā ||
    1. saṅgatyā yadi ceṣyeta pūrvapūrvapramāṇatā |
    2. pramāṇāntaram icchanto na vyavasthāṃ labhemahi |
    1. kasya cit tu yadīṣyeta svata eva pramāṇatā |
    2. prathamasya tathābhāve pradveṣaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ ||
    1. śrotradhīś cāpramāṇaṃ syād itarābhir asaṅgateḥ |
    2. syāc cet tajjanitenaiva jñānenānyena saṅgatiḥ ||
    1. vede 'pi śatakṛtvaḥ syād buddhir uccāraṇānugā |
    2. sādhanāntarajanyā tu buddhir nāsti dvayor api ||
    1. yathā tv ekendriyādhīnajñānāntaranibandhanā |
    2. saṅgatiḥ kāraṇaṃ prāptā tathā vede 'pi kalpyatām ||
    1. tasmād dṛḍhaṃ yadutpannaṃ nāpi saṃvādamṛcchati |
    2. jñānāntareṇa vijñānaṃ tatpramāṇaṃ pratīyatām ||
    1. na cānumānataḥ sādhyā śabdādīnāṃ pramāṇatā |
    2. sarvasyaiva hi mā prāpat pramāṇāntarasādhyatā ||
    1. nanu pramāṇam ityevaṃ pratyakṣādi na gṛhyate |
    2. na cetthamagṛhītena vyavahāro 'vakalpate ||
    1. prāmāṇyaṃ grahaṇāt pūrvaṃ svarūpeṇaiva saṃsthitam |
    2. nirapekṣaṃ svakāryeṣu gṛhyate pratyayāntaraiḥ ||
    1. tenāsya jñāyamānatvaṃ prāmāṇye nopayujyate |
    2. viṣayānubhāvo hy atra pūrvasmād eva labhyate |
    1. apramāṇaṃ punaḥ svārthagrāhakaṃ syāt svarūpataḥ |
    2. nivṛttis tasya mithyātve nāgṛhīte parair bhavet ||
    1. na hy arthasyātathābhāvaḥ pūrveṇārthas tathātvavat |
    2. tatrāpy arthānyathābhāve dhīr yad vā duṣṭakāraṇe ||
    1. tāvataiva ca mithyātvaṃ gṛhyate nānyahetukam |
    2. utpattyavasthaṃ caivedaṃ pramāṇam iti mīyate ||
    1. ato yatrāpi mithyātvaṃ parebhyaḥ pratipādyate |
    2. tatrāpy etad dvayaṃ vācyaṃ na tu sādharmyamātrakam ||
    1. codanārthānyathābhāvaṃ kurvataś cānumānataḥ |
    2. tajjñānenaiva yo bādhaḥ sa kathaṃ vinivāryate ||
    1. tanmithyātvād abādhaś cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam |
    2. nānumānād ato 'nyad dhi bādhakaṃ kiñ cid asti te ||
    1. na cānyair agrahe 'rthasya syād abhāvo rasādivat |
    2. teṣāṃ jihvādibhir yasmān niyamo grahaṇe 'sti hi ||
    1. taddhiyaivārthabodhaś cet, tādṛgdharme bhaviṣyati |
    2. mamāsiddham idaṃ kin tu vedāj jāte 'vabodhane |
    1. vaktuṃ na dveṣamātreṇa yujyate satyavādinā |
    2. dveṣād asammatatvād vā na ca syād apramāṇatā ||
    1. na cātmecchābhyanujñābhyāṃ prāmāṇyam avakalpate |
    2. agnidāhādiduḥkhasya na hy apratyakṣateṣyate ||
    1. na cābhilāpikaṃ jñānaṃ prāmāṇyenāvadhāryate |
    2. tasmād ālokavad vede sarvasādhāraṇe sati ||
    1. naivaṃ vipratipattavyam, bauddhāder vakṣyate 'ntaram |
    2. puruṣāśaktitas tatra sāpavādatvasambhavaḥ ||
    1. vedasyāpauruṣeyatve siddhā tv evaṃ pramāṇatā |
    2. kartṛmattve tu vedasya samyaṅmithyātvavādibhiḥ ||
    1. kartā guṇāś ca doṣāś ca mahājanaparigrahaḥ |
    2. evamādi vinā yuktyā kalpyam, mīmāṃsakaiḥ punaḥ ||
    1. idānīm iva sarvatra dṛṣṭān nādhikam iṣyate |
    2. evambhūtasya vedasya jñānotpattiṃ prakurvataḥ ||
    1. svarūpaviparītatvasaṃśayau bhāṣyavāritau |
    2. nivārayiṣyate cāpi duṣṭakāraṇakalpanā ||
    1. puruṣābhāvatas tena taddvāreṇāpy aśaṅkitau |
    2. tathā satyatathābhāvo buddhyanutpattim āśritaḥ ||
    1. tatra vipratiṣiddhatvaṃ bravītītyevamādinā |
    2. yathādṛṣṭārthavāditvaṃ tac cet pratyayitāditi ||
    1. indriyeti tu mūlaṃ ced asyāstītyevam abravīt |
    2. draṣṭṛtvasatyavāditve tac cet pratyayitāditi ||
    1. dṛśyamānārthavāditve syād anāptoktisatyatā |
    2. evaṃ tv ekāṅgavaikalyāt pratyudāharaṇasthitiḥ ||
    1. ekaikābhāvamātre syād āptatvaindriyakatvayoḥ |
    2. apratyayitapakṣe syād aindriyasyāpy asatyatā ||
    1. anindriyatvapakṣe vā satpratyayitabhāṣitam |
    2. vyāhatagranthataivaṃ syāt, tasmāt pūrveṇa satyatā ||
    1. pareṇa mūlasadbhāva indriyeṇa tu darśitaḥ |
    2. aprāmāṇyanivṛttyarthaṃ doṣābhāvopavarṇanam ||
    1. guṇāt prāmāṇyam ityevaṃ tatpūrvaṃ sunirākṛtam |
    2. pūrvatra pratiṣiddhatvān naitat prāmāṇyakāraṇam ||
    1. samuccayārtho vāśabdaḥ pūrvasmin, uttaratra ca |
    2. vikalpenobhayor āha pratyudāharaṇe pṛthak ||
    1. śakye 'py asatye mithyātvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ satye 'py aśaktike |
    2. nānena vacaneneha sarvajñatvanirākriyā ||
    1. vacanād ṛta ityevam apavādo hi saṃśritaḥ |
    2. yadi ṣaḍbhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ syāt sarvajñaḥ kena vāryate ||
    1. ekena tu pramāṇena sarvajño yena kalpyate |
    2. nūnaṃ sa cakṣuṣā sarvān rasādīn pratipadyate ||
    1. yajjātīyaiḥ pramāṇais tu yajjātīyārthadarśanam |
    2. bhaved idānīṃ lokasya tathā kālāntare 'py abhūt |
    1. yatrāpy atiśayo dṛṣṭaḥ sa svārthānatilaṅghanāt |
    2. dūrasūkṣmādidṛṣṭau syān na rūpe śrotravṛttitā ||
    1. bhaviṣyati na dṛṣṭaṃ ca pratyakṣasya manāgapi |
    2. sāmarthyam, nānumānāder liṅgādirahite kva cit ||
    1. sarvajñakalpanānyais tu vede cāpauruṣeyatā |
    2. tulyatā kalpitā yena tenedaṃ sampradhāryatām ||
    1. sarvajño dṛśyate tāvan nedānīm asmadādibhiḥ |
    2. nirākaraṇavacchakyā na cāsīd iti kalpanā ||
    1. na cāgamena sarvajñaḥ, tadīye 'nyonyasaṃśrayāt |
    2. narāntarapraṇītasya prāmāṇyaṃ gamyate katham ||
    1. na cāpy evamparo nityaḥ śakyo labdhum ihāgamaḥ |
    2. nityaś ced arthavādatvaṃ tatpare syād anityatā ||
    1. āgamasya ca nityatve siddhe tatkalpanā vṛthā |
    2. yatas taṃ pratipadyante dharmam eva tato narāḥ ||
    1. yo 'pīndriyārthasambandhaviṣaye satyavāditām |
    2. dṛṣṭvā tadvacanatvena śraddheye 'rthe 'pi kalpayet ||
    1. tenāpi pāratantryeṇa bādhitā syāt pramāṇatā |
    2. prāmāṇyaṃ cet svayaṃ tasya kāpekṣānyendriyādiṣu ||
    1. yathaivātrendriyādibhyaḥ paricchedāt pramāṇatā |
    2. śraddheye 'pi tathaiva syān na svātantryeṇa labhyate |
    1. yathā ca teṣāṃ satyatvaṃ sidhyaty etena hetunā |
    2. tathānyānavabuddhārthaprāmāṇyābhāvasādhanam |
    1. aśraddheyārthasatyatvaṃ śraddheye cāpy asatyatā |
    2. pūrvajñānānuvāditvaṃ dṛṣṭāntavad iheṣyatām ||
    1. api cālaukikārthatve sati puṃvākyahetukam |
    2. mithyātvaṃ bauddhavākyānāṃ syād anyonyaṃ sapakṣataḥ ||
    1. dharmādharmātiriktārthe prāmāṇyaṃ ca prasajyate |
    2. sāṃkhyādiṣu ca jīvatsu dṛṣṭānto durlabho 'sya ca |
    1. alaukikārthavācitvaṃ nṛvākyatve satīti ca |
    2. parasparam apekṣyaiva bauddhādeḥ syān mṛṣārthatā ||
    1. vaded evaṃ ca yo nāma vādī prathamasaṅgataḥ |
    2. tasyāpi hetuḥ syād eṣa bhavantaṃ pratyasaṃśayam ||
    1. buddhādīnām asarvajñam iti satyaṃ vaco mama |
    2. maduktatvād yathaivāgnir uṣṇo bhāsvara ity api ||
    1. pratyakṣaṃ ca maduktatvaṃ tvayā sādhyā taduktatā |
    2. tena hetur madīyaḥ syāt sandigdhāsiddhatā tava ||
    1. pratyakṣādyavisaṃvādi prameyatvādi yasya ca |
    2. sadbhāvavāraṇe śaktaṃ ko nu taṃ kalpayiṣyati ||
    1. na cāpi smṛtyavicchedāt sarvajñaḥ parikalpyate |
    2. vigānāt, chinnamūlatvāt, kaiś cid eva parigrahāt ||
    1. sarvajño 'sāv iti hy eva tatkāle tu bubhutsubhiḥ |
    2. tajjñānajñeyavijñānarahitair gamyate katham ||
    1. kalpanīyāś ca sarvajñā bhaveyur bahavas tava |
    2. ya eva syād asarvajñaḥ sa sarvajñaṃ na budhyate ||
    1. sarvajño 'navabuddhaś ca yenaiva syān na taṃ prati |
    2. tadvākyānāṃ pramāṇatvaṃ mūlājñāne 'nyavākyavat ||
    1. rāgādirahite cāsmin nirvyāpāre vyavasthite |
    2. deśanānyapraṇītaiva syād ṛte pratyavekṣaṇāt ||
    1. sānnidhyamātratas tasya puṃsaścintāmaṇer iva |
    2. niḥsaranti yathākāmaṃ kuḍyādibhyo 'pi deśanāḥ ||
    1. evamādyucyamānaṃ tu śraddadhānasya śobhate |
    2. kuḍyādiniḥsṛtatvāc ca nāśvāso deśanāsu naḥ ||
    1. kin nu buddhapraṇītāḥ syuḥ kimu kaiś cid durātmabhiḥ |
    2. adṛśyair vipralambhārthaṃ piśācādibhir īritāḥ ||
    1. evaṃ yaiḥ kevalaṃ jñānam indriyādyanapekṣiṇaḥ |
    2. sūkṣmātītādiviṣayaṃ jīvasya parikalpitam ||
    1. narte tadāgamāt sidhyen na ca tenāgamo vinā |
    2. dṛṣṭānto 'pi na tasyānyo nṛṣu kaś cit pravartate ||
    1. nityāgamāvabodho 'pi pratyākhyeyo 'nayā diśā |
    2. na hi tatrāpi visrambho dṛṣṭo 'nena kṛto 'tha vā ||
    1. sarvadā cāpi puruṣāḥ prāyeṇānṛtavādinaḥ |
    2. yathādyatve na visrambhas tathātītārthakīrtane ||
    1. svapnādijñānavac cāpi pratyayo 'syāgamārthayoḥ |
    2. bhaved iti saśaṅkānāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ gamyate katham ||
    1. puruṣātiśayaś ceṣṭaḥ saiva cāgamanityatā |
    2. kalpitaṃ smaraṇaṃ cāsya janmāntaranibandhanam ||
    1. grāhyatve cāgamasyaivaṃ dveṣo 'rthagrahaṇe vṛthā |
    2. yo hy anuccāritaṃ śabdaṃ gahṇātyarthe 'sya kā kathā |
    1. pumāṃs tāvat svatantraḥ syād arthagrahaṇavādinām |
    2. āgamapratibhāne tu pāratantryaṃ dvayor api ||
    1. anekapuruṣasthatvād ekatraiva ca janmani |
    2. grahaṇasmaraṇād vede na svātantryaṃ vihanyate ||
    1. anyathākaraṇe cāsya bahubhyaḥ syān nivāraṇam |
    2. ekasya pratibhānaṃ tu kṛtakān na viśiṣyate ||
    1. ataś ca sampradāye ca naikaḥ puruṣa iṣyate |
    2. bahavaḥ paratantrāḥ syuḥ sarve hy adyatvavannarāḥ ||
    1. evaṃ ca kalpayantyanye yāvadāgamasiddhaye |
    2. tāvan na kalpayaty etat samatvaṃ jaimineḥ paraiḥ ||
    1. na hi dṛṣṭādhikaṃ kiñ cit prāmāṇye tena kalpyate |
    2. aprāmāṇyanimitteṣu parasyādṛṣṭakalpanā ||
    1. dṛṣṭaprāmāṇyabādhaś ca nāstikasya prasajyate |
    2. utpanne sati vijñāne balād bādhaprakalpanā ||
    1. sādhite puruṣābhāve nirdoṣajñānajanmanaḥ |
    2. pratyakṣān nāstikair vācyo viśeṣaś codanādhiyaḥ ||
    1. upadeśo 'nyathā na syād atīndriyanidandhanaḥ |
    2. tasya kartrā na ced dṛṣṭaḥ so 'rtha ity arthakalpanā ||
    1. yad vānumānam evedam upadeśitvam ucyate |
    2. dṛṣṭārthapūrvatāvyāptam, vyatireko 'sya nanv iti ||
    1. anyathāpy upapannatvaṃ vyāmohād iti kathyate |
    2. liṅgasya vyabhicāro vā bālavākyanidarśanāt |
    1. vedāj jñātvopadiṣṭaṃ ced ityevaṃ siddhasādhanam |
    2. vedād apītyanenoktam, manvādeś caitad iṣyate ||
    1. anyathā saṃvidāno 'pi vivakṣaty anyathā yataḥ |
    2. tasmād ekāntato nāsti puṃvākyāt taddhiyāṃ gatiḥ ||
    1. bhrāntasyānyavivakṣāyām anyad vākyaṃ ca dṛśyate |
    2. yathāvivakṣam apy etat tasmān naiva pravartate ||
    1. vaktṛdhīr āptavākyeṣu gamyate, anyatra viplutiḥ |
    2. tenotsargāpavādābhyāṃ vacasaḥ śaktir ucyate ||
    1. padārtharacanāyatto vākyārthapratyayodbhavaḥ |
    2. vivakṣāpūrvavijñānavaśāc ca racanākṛtiḥ ||
    1. vivakṣāntarayuktā hi kurvāṇā racanāntaram |
    2. āvāpodvāpabhedena dṛśyante 'rtheṣu mānavāḥ |
    1. tenārthapratyayotpāde śroturjāte 'pi vākyataḥ |
    2. jñāto nūnam aneneti vakturjñāne matir bhavet ||
    1. āptoktikāraṇaṃ kañ cid anuyuṅkte naraṃ yadā |
    2. tadā ca nirdiśatyāptaṃ sa jānātyetad ityasau ||
    1. tajjñānāntaritatvāc ca śabdās tāvad udāsate |
    2. prāmāṇyasthāpanaṃ tu syād vaktṛdhīhetusambhavāt ||
    1. arthe pūrvapratīte 'pi niścayo hi tadāśrayaḥ |
    2. tenārthajñānagamyāpi prāmāṇye saiva pūrvabhāk |
    1. ato 'tra puṃnimittatvād upapannā mṛṣārthatā |
    2. na tu syāt tatsvabhāvatvaṃ vede vakturabhāvataḥ |
    1. tadbuddhyantarayor nāstīty artho 'rthaiś ca pratīyate |
    2. ato na jñānapūrvatvam apekṣyaṃ nāyathārthatā ||
    1. apramāṇatvasiddhau vā dṛṣṭānto ya udāhṛtaḥ |
    2. buddhādivacanaṃ tasya sādhyenāsaṅgatocyate ||
    1. teṣām api hi yat kāryaṃ pūrvatra pratipāditam |
    2. tatra samyaktvam arthe tu vyāpāro naiva vidyate ||
    1. svavyāpārātirikte 'rthe vedasyāpi mṛṣārthatā |
    2. pūrvapakṣārthavattvena prasaktā siddhasādhyatā ||
    1. ajñātvaivamabhiprāyaṃ kṛtakākṛtakatvayoḥ |
    2. satyamithyātvahetūktimātrajñānāt paro 'bravīt ||
    1. nanu sāmānyatodṛṣṭam, nānyatvād ityadūṣaṇam |
    2. anyatvād eva dṛṣṭānto na hi pakṣe sapakṣatā ||
    1. tasmād ayam abhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasya varṇyate |
    2. abhyupetyārthaviṣayaṃ vākyavyāpāram ucyate |
    1. yadi syād vyavadhāne 'pi vākyārthāpekṣayānṛtam |
    2. dṛṣṭānto nṛvaco 'trāpi hetuḥ sādhāraṇo bhavet ||
    1. satyeṣv api hi dṛṣṭaiva paurṣeyeṣu vākyatā |
    2. atīndriye 'pi kiñ cid dhi satyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yadṛcchayā ||
    1. nānyatvād iti cānena paroktād anyatocyate |
    2. anyo hy eṣa tadābhāsaḥ, vipakṣaṃ vānyam abravīt |
    1. yad vānyasmād visaṃvādān mithyātvaṃ tatra na tv iha |
    2. viṣayasyāpi cānyatvāt sādhanāsaṅgataiva sā ||
    1. na hy anyasyeti naikasmin mṛṣārthe 'nyamṛṣārthatā |
    2. vivakṣāyā mṛṣārthatve na ca vākye mṛṣārthatā ||
    1. śyāmatve puṃstvavac caitat sādhāraṇye nidarśanam |
    2. parokter vāpi duṣṭatvād vikalpasamam ucyate ||
    1. yad vā pramāṇam evedaṃ samyaktve 'nyatvam ucyate |
    2. dhiruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ bādho vāpy anumānataḥ |
    1. codanājanitā buddhiḥ pramāṇaṃ doṣavarjitaiḥ |
    2. kāraṇair janyamānatvāl liṅgāptoktyakṣabuddhivat |
    1. tathānāptāpraṇītoktijanyatvād bādhavarjanāt |
    2. deśakālādibhedādau cāptoktipratyayo yathā ||
    1. akartṛkatvasiddhyā ca hetutvaṃ sādhayiṣyate |
    2. evamādyavabudhyāyaṃ nānyatvād ity avocata |
    1. pratyakṣas tv iti dārḍhyaṃ vā prāthamyaṃ vāpi lakṣayet |
    2. svarūpataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ mithyātvaṃ pararūpataḥ ||
    1. jñānābhāvaś ca mithyātvaṃ dvayasyāsambhavād yadi |
    2. pratyakṣaṃ tatpareṣāṃ ca siddham asyānumānataḥ ||
    1. yathā ca tava mithyātvaṃ sādhanaṃ sādhayed idam |
    2. tathā ca bādhakādhīnaṃ mithyātvam api sādhayet ||
    1. dharma ity upasaṃhārye yacchreyaskarabhāṣaṇam |
    2. taddharmapadavācyārthanirūpaṇavivakṣayā ||
    1. śreyo hi puruṣaprītiḥ sā dravyaguṇakarmabhiḥ |
    2. codanālakṣaṇaiḥ sādhyā tasmāt teṣv eva dharmatā ||
    1. anyat sādhyam adṛṣṭvaiva yāgādīnanuniṣṭhataḥ |
    2. dhārmikatvasamākhyānaṃ tadyogād iti gamyate ||
    1. paśvādīni ca dharmasya phalānīti vyavasthitam |
    2. citrāgodohanādīnāṃ tāny uktāni phalāni ca ||
    1. tasmāt teṣv eva dharmatvam, dhrmāṇīti ca darśanāt |
    2. liṅgasaṃkhyāvinirmukto dharmaśabdo nidarśanam |
    1. antaḥkaraṇavṛttau vā vāsanāyāṃ ca cetasaḥ |
    2. pudgaleṣu ca puṇyeṣu nṛguṇe 'pūrvajanmani ||
    1. prayogo dharmaśabdasya na dṛṣṭaḥ, na ca sādhanam |
    2. puruṣārthasya te jñātuṃ śakyante codanādibhiḥ ||
    1. na ca vastvantaraṃ śakyam apūrvaṃ svargayāgayoḥ |
    2. jñātuṃ sādhanabhūtaṃ vā sādhyaṃ vā nāpy ato 'nyathā |
    1. śrutasādhanasādhyatvatyāgenāśrutakalpanā |
    2. prasajyetāsya tādrūpye vyatireke tv arūpatā ||
    1. tasmāt phale pravṛttasya yāgādeḥ śaktimātrakam |
    2. utpattau vāpi paśvāder apūrvaṃ na tataḥ pṛthak ||
    1. śaktayaḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ bhāvaśabdair viśeṣataḥ |
    2. nopākhyāyanta ityevaṃ nāpūrvaṃ dharmaśabdatā |
    1. purastāc codanāśabdo vidhāv eva vyavasthitaḥ |
    2. na ca tallakṣaṇā hiṃsā pratyudāharaṇaṃ katham ||
    1. codanālakṣaṇo yaś ca śyenādir hi gamyate |
    2. niṣedhābhāvatas tasya kathaṃ brūyād anarthatā ||
    1. yady api syād vidhispṛṣṭe niṣedho naiva tādṛśaḥ |
    2. vijñāyate hy anarthatvaṃ ṣoḍaśigrahaṇādivat ||
    1. codanālakṣaṇaṃ coktvā niṣiddhatvād virudhyate |
    2. śyenādāv upadiṣṭe ca hiṃsā hīti na yujyate ||
    1. hiṃsā hi phalam eteṣāṃ bhinnā tebhyaḥ svarūpataḥ |
    2. sā hi prāṇaviyogātmā śyenas tatrāsivatpṛthak ||
    1. upadeśābhidhānaṃ ca nāvidheye 'vakalpate |
    2. śyenāder avidhāne ca kasyānyasya vidheyatā ||
    1. sarvatrāvasthito nyāyo bhāvanāṃśadvaye vidhiḥ |
    2. sa bādhyeta, iha ye cāmī jyotiṣṭomādayo matāḥ ||
    1. dharmatvena na te 'pi syur hiṃsāsādhanakā hi te |
    2. na cāvidhīyamānasya phalatatsādhanāṅgatā ||
    1. sādhanatvena vihitaṃ na cāvihitam ucyate |
    2. sādhyatvena vidhānaṃ tu naiveṣṭaṃ lokavedayoḥ ||
    1. tenaivamarthaśabdasya prayojanam ihocyate |
    2. pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yā śabdaśravaṇena dhīḥ |
    1. sā codaneti sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hṛdaye sthitam |
    2. pravartakagṛhītis tu syād udāharaṇārthatā ||
    1. tātparye hy arthaśabdasya neyaṃ vyākhyopapadyate |
    2. arthagrahaṇalabhyaṃ vā tatpravartakabhāṣaṇam |
    1. dharme pramāṇabhūtāyās tad vā lakṣaṇam uktavān |
    2. evaṃ sati vidhibhyaḥ syād vidheyārthāvadhāraṇam ||
    1. niṣedhebhyo niṣedhyānām anarthatvena nirṇayaḥ |
    2. tenārthagrahaṇenoktā vidheyasyeha dharmatā ||
    1. niṣedhyānām anarthatvam arthasiddhaṃ na sūtritam |
    2. tasmād ubhayam ityatra vidheyapratiṣedhyayoḥ ||
    1. yāgādibrahmahatyādivargayoḥ syān nidarśanam |
    2. śyenādīnāṃ vidheyatvādiṣṭasyāpi ca sādhanāt ||
    1. upacārād anarthatvaṃ phaladvāreṇa varṇyate |
    2. pratiṣiddhā hi setyatra sphuṭam etat kariṣyate ||
    1. hiṃsā hīti ca yac cāpi brūte nābhicared iti |
    2. śyenādīnāṃ svarūpe tu nottaragranthasaṅgatiḥ ||
    1. vihitatvān niṣedhasya pravṛttis teṣu durlabhā |
    2. yadā tu codanāśabdo vidhāveva vyavasthitaḥ |
    1. tadobhayādiko granthaḥ sadhyasādhanasaṃśritaḥ |
    2. sādhyasādhanasambandhe vidhinā pratipādite ||
    1. lakṣyamāṇatvam ubhayoḥ, dvividhaṃ ca phalaṃ kratoḥ |
    2. svargādi prāpyate tatra pratiṣedhānatikramāt ||
    1. atikrameṇa hiṃsādi, śāstrāntaranirīkṣayā |
    2. phalāṃśe bhāvanāyāś ca pratyayo na vidhāyakaḥ ||
    1. vakṣyate, jaiminiś cāha tasya lipsārthalakṣaṇā |
    2. tena sāmānyataḥ prāpto vidhinā na nivāritaḥ ||
    1. phalāṃśopanipātinyā hiṃsāyāḥ pratiṣedhakaḥ |
    2. anarthaprāptihetutvaṃ bodhyate tatra yady api ||
    1. śyenasvarūpaṃ nānarthas tatphalasya tv anarthatā |
    2. parastūbhayam ityādeḥ phalasyāpi vidheyatām ||
    1. bhāvanāntargatatvād vā matvānarthatvam ākṣipat |
    2. naivetyetāvatā cāsya vidheyatvanirākriyā ||
    1. kiṃ vidheyam idānīṃ syād āha śyenādayas tv iti |
    2. praśnāpākaraṇe cātra tavyo vidhivivakṣayā ||
    1. prayukto na tu sādhye 'rthe, dvaye 'py anupayogataḥ |
    2. anarthasyāpi sādhyatvam avidheyasya hīṣyate ||
    1. sādhyatvarahite ceṣṭā vidheye nityam arthatā |
    2. śatuś ca lakṣaṇārthatvaṃ teṣāṃ cāpy upadeśanam ||
    1. bruvan sphuṭīkarotīṣṭam upadeśo hi nānyathā |
    2. vidhitvamādiśabdāt syād itikartavyatāsv api |
    1. tasmāt phalāṃśe yā hiṃsā vaidikī sā niṣidhyate |
    2. aṃśadvaye tu yā nāma tanniṣedhābhidhāyinām ||
    1. aviśeṣeṇa yacchāstraṃ śirovad iti cottaram |
    2. niṣedhenānavaṣṭabdhe viṣaye na hy anarthatā |
    1. pratyakṣāder aśakyatvāt kalpyate niṣpramāṇikā |
    2. na hi hiṃsādyanuṣṭhāne tadānīṃ doṣadarśanam ||
    1. bāhye 'pi vicikitsā tu śāstrādevopajāyate |
    2. hiṃsyamānasya duḥkhitvaṃ dṛśyate yan na tāvatā ||
    1. karturduḥkhānumānaṃ syāt, tadānīṃ tadviparyayaḥ |
    2. viṣaye 'syāḥ phalaṃ yādṛk pretya krtus tathāvidham ||
    1. hiṃsā kriyāviśeṣatvāt sūte śāstroktadānavat |
    2. ya evamāha, tasyāpi gurustrīgamanādibhiḥ ||
    1. surāpānādibhiś cāpi vipakṣair vyabhicāritā |
    2. viruddhatā ca, yādṛgdhi dānais tādṛk phalaṃ bhavet ||
    1. vidhigamyaphalāvāptiḥ, aduḥkhātmakatā tathā |
    2. na ca yā sampradānasya prītis tādṛk phalaṃ śrutam ||
    1. dātus tena hi dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhyahīnaḥ pratīyate |
    2. sampradānaṃ ca dāne te viṣayaḥ karma hiṃsane ||
    1. vaiṣamyam, sampradāne tu pakṣe tv etadviruddhatā |
    2. prīyate sampradānaṃ hi devateti mataṃ tava ||
    1. dṛṣṭānte karma dānaṃ cet, tasya kīdṛk phalaṃ bhavet |
    2. japahomādidṛṣṭāntāt parapīḍādivarjanāt ||
    1. coditatvasya hetutvād viruddhāvyabhicāritā |
    2. vihitapratiṣiddhatve muktvānyan na ca kāraṇam ||
    1. dharmādharmāvabodhasya tenāyuktānumānagīḥ |
    2. anugrahāc ca dharmatvaṃ pīḍātaś cāpy adharmatām ||
    1. vadato japasīdhvādipānādau nobhayaṃ bhavet |
    2. krośatā hṛdayenāpi gurudārābhigāminām ||
    1. bhūyān dharmaḥ prasajyeta bhūyasī hy upakāritā |
    2. anumānapradhānasya pratiṣedhānapekṣiṇaḥ ||
    1. hṛdayakrośanaṃ kasmād dṛṣṭāṃ pīḍām apaśyataḥ |
    2. poḍātaś cāpy adharmatvaṃ tathā pīḍām adharmataḥ ||
    1. anyonyāśrayam āpnoti vinā śāstreṇa sādhayan |
    2. evamādāv aśāstrajñomleccho nodvijate kva cit ||
    1. tasya nādharmayogaḥ syāt pūrvoktā yadi kalpanā |
    2. tasmād anugrahaṃ pīḍāṃ tadabhāvam apāsya ca |
    1. dharmādharmārthibhir nityaṃ mṛgyau vidhiniṣedhakau |
    2. kva cid asyā niṣiddhatvāc chaktiḥ śāstreṇa bodhitā ||
    1. pratyavāyanimittatve vidhinā nāpagacchati |
    2. śāstreṇa na hi śaktīnām āvāpodvāpanakriyāḥ ||
    1. vidyamānā hi kathyante śaktayo dravyakarmaṇām |
    2. tad eva cedaṃ karmeti śāstram evānudhāvatā ||
    1. hiṃsādīnām adharmatvaṃ kathyate nānumānataḥ |
    2. evaṃ ye nipuṇaṃ prāhus tair apy etat parīkṣyatām ||
    1. surāpānādibhiḥ śūdraḥ kiṃ yāti narakaṃ kṛtaiḥ |
    2. vaiśyastomena vā kiṃ syād viprarājanyayoḥ phalam ||
    1. pañcamyām iṣṭikaraṇānmadhyāhne cāgnihotrataḥ |
    2. tasmād yady ādṛśaṃ karma yatphalotpattiśaktikam ||
    1. śāstreṇa gamyate tasya tādṛśasyaiva tat phalam |
    2. hiṃsā cāṃśadvayādanyā yā tasyāḥ pratiṣedhajam ||
    1. pratyavāyārthatājñānam, vidhinānyatra vāryate |
    2. jñānam eva ca śaktīnāṃ nāvāpodvāpanakriyāḥ ||
    1. jñāyante śāstratas tāstu kriyābhedavyavasthitāḥ |
    2. vyavasthāḥ śaktibhedānāṃ dṛṣṭārtheṣv api karmasu ||
    1. abhinnatve 'pi dṛśyante bhujeḥ svasthātur eṣv api |
    2. rūpābhede 'pi hiṃsāder bhedo 'ṅgānaṅgakāritaḥ ||
    1. tathāpy ekaphalatvaṃ cet kriyātvāt sarvasaṅkaraḥ |
    2. yajitvādyaviśeṣāc ca citrādiphalatulyatā ||
    1. bhedāt tatra vyavasthā ced ihāpyevaṃ bhaviṣyati |
    2. vidhīnāṃ vāpi sarveṣāṃ sākṣād vyavahito 'pi vā ||
    1. puruṣārthaḥ phalaṃ tena nānartho 'taḥ pratīyate |
    2. na caiṣu śrūyate 'narthaḥ, niṣedhān na ca kalpyate ||
    1. na ca prakaraṇasthatvāt puruṣārthaḥ phalaṃ bhavet |
    2. karmopakāraḥ kalpyas tu dṛṣṭo 'dṛṣṭo 'tha vā punaḥ ||
    1. kalpanāvasaras tatra nānarthasyānapekṣaṇāt |
    2. kratvarthaś cāpi saṃskāraḥ paśor nārādupakriyā ||
    1. dṛṣṭaiva tv avadānānāṃ niṣpattiḥ kratvapekṣitā |
    2. abhicāre 'py upāyasthā hiṃsā nādharma ucyate |
    1. tasmād anaṅgabhūtāyāṃ hiṃsāyām etad ucyate |
    2. uddeśāc ca phalatvena śyenādau na vidhīyate ||
    1. bhāvanāvidhir apy eva phalāṃśād vinivartate |
    2. ataḥ svato na dharmatvaṃ śyenāder nāpy adharmatā ||
    1. phalānarthānubandhitvāt taddvāreṇopacaryate |
    2. nirākāṅkṣasya caikena śyenasya na phaladvayam ||
    1. tasmāt kriyāntarād eva hiṃsāto 'nartha ucyate |
    2. phalato 'pi ca yatkarma nānarthenānubadhyate ||
    1. kevalaprītihetutvāt taddharmatvena hīṣyate |
    2. nanu ceṣṭābhyupāyatvāt śyenāder dharmatā bhavet ||
    1. phalaṃ tāvad adharmo 'sya śyenādeḥ sampradhāryate |
    2. yadi yeneṣṭasiddhiḥ syād anuṣṭhānānubandhinī ||
    1. tasya dharmatvam ucyeta tataḥ śyenādivarjanam |
    2. yadā tu codanāgamyaḥ kāryākāryānapekṣayā ||
    1. dharmaḥ prītinimittaṃ syāt tadā śyene 'pi dharmatā |
    2. yadi tv aprītihetur yaḥ sākṣād vyavahito 'pi vā ||
    1. so 'dharmaś codanārthaḥ syāt tadā śyene 'py adharmatā |
    2. yas tu hiṃsātvasādharmyād bāhyavaccodanāsv api ||
    1. vaded anarthahetutvaṃ tasyāpy āgamabādhanam |
    2. tam anādṛtya yo brūyād yāgāder apy asau vadet ||
    1. svargādisādhanāśaktiṃ kriyātvād bhojanādivat |
    2. gītāmantrārthavādair yā kalpyate 'narthahetutā ||
    1. pratyakṣaśrutibādhyatvāt sānyārthatvena nīyate |
    2. śiṣyān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt sūtravaidikavākyayoḥ ||
    1. aśakteś cobhayoḥ sāmyān na sūtreṣv ity anuttaram |
    2. prāguktaparisaṃkhyāyāḥ phalam etat prakāśyate ||
    1. sūtreṣu hy anayā yuktyā gatir eṣāpi yujyate |
    2. tasmād āvartate sūtram, tantraṃ vā śaktibhedataḥ ||
    1. ekadeśānumānād vā dve sūtre parikalpite |
    2. itaretarasāmīpyād etāv eva parasparam ||
    1. kalpyete vākyaśeṣāya nānyāvayavakalpanā |
    2. viśiṣṭārthānuvāditvād atha vety api bhāṣite ||
    1. vākyabhedaḥ sa eveti saṃjñātantratvam uttaram |
    2. arthaṃ vā pratyupādānāt saṃjñālakṣaṇaśabdayoḥ |
    1. tantraṃ lakṣaṇaśabdo vā vācyo dharmārthaśabdayoḥ |
    2. dharme sāmānyataḥ siddhe pramāṇaṃ kathyate yadā ||
    1. vṛttam eva tadārthatvaṃ kimarthaṃ punarucyate |
    2. codanālakṣaṇatvasya dharmaṃ prati vidheyatā ||
    1. labhyate 'rthānuvādena saṃśayo hy anyathā bhavet |
    2. tathā ca ye 'py anarthasya sādhanatvena kalpitāḥ ||
    1. niṣedhais te 'pi dharmāḥ syuś codanālakṣaṇatvataḥ |
    2. tasmād arthāparityāgād ekārthagrahaṇaṃ yathā ||
    1. labhyate vacanavyaktyā sā syād arthānuvādataḥ |
    2. viśeṣaṇād vinā caitadarthasāmarthyakāritam ||
    1. kathyate bhāṣyakāreṇa phalaṃ hiṃsādivarjanam ||

{3 nimittasūtra NMS}

    1. pratijñāvyatirekeṇa bhāṣyakāreṇa yady api |
    2. vakṣyamāṇā svapakṣasya yuktiḥ pūrvaṃ nidarśitā ||
    1. pratijñāmātram ityetajjaiminer matam ucyate |
    2. vṛttikāro 'dhikaṃ vāpi bhūtādi dvāram abravīt ||

{4 pratyakṣasūtra PAS}

    1. varṇyate sūtrabhedena yena pratyakṣalakṣaṇam |
    2. tena sūtrasya sambandho vācyaḥ pūrvapratijñayā ||
    1. lakṣaṇasyābhidhānaṃ tu kenāṃśenopayujyate |
    2. kimarthaṃ cānumānāder lakṣaṇaṃ nātra kathyate ||
    1. na tāvad apramāṇatvaṃ teṣāṃ nāpy akṣabuddhiṣu |
    2. śakyate 'ntargatir vaktuṃ na ca lakṣaṇatulyatā ||
    1. na cāpi siddhir eṣāṃ syād arthāt pratyakṣalakṣaṇāt |
    2. na hi tatpūrvakaṃ sarvaṃ pramāṇam iti niścitam ||
    1. pratyakṣalakṣaṇoktiś ca nānumānādilakṣaṇāt |
    2. vinā na sidhyatītyevamarthākṣepo na yujyate ||
    1. tadetatpūrvakatve dhīr na ca tallakṣaṇād bhavet |
    2. tadukter vānumānādi kiṃ na syāt tadapūrvakam ||
    1. na ca lakṣaṇabhedasya svarūpe yat tayor api |
    2. pratyakṣalakṣaṇād eṣāṃ kathañ cid avadhāraṇā ||
    1. prasiddhatvād avācyatvaṃ pratyakṣe 'pi prasajyate |
    2. tenānyaparisaṃkhyārthaṃ sūtraṃ mūḍhena vocyate ||
    1. na tv ekaṃ lakṣayed eṣu buddhipūrvaṃ kathañ cana |
    2. sambhavaty ekavākyatve vākyabhedaś ca neṣyate ||
    1. na cāpy etena sūtreṇa pratyakṣaṃ lakṣyate sphuṭam |
    2. tadābhāse 'pi tulyatvāt, svapnajñānaikavarjanāt ||
    1. taddhīndriyārthasambandhavyāpāreṇa vinā bhavet |
    2. kena cit samprayoge tu bhrāntyādi syān niyogataḥ ||
    1. grāhyeṇānyena vety etat kṛtaṃ naiva viśeṣaṇam |
    2. samprayogasya yena syād viśeṣo vakṣyamāṇavat ||
    1. asāmarthya ca matvāsya vṛttikāreṇa lakṣaṇe |
    2. tatsamprayoga ityevaṃ pāṭhāntaramṛdāhṛtam ||
    1. tenānyenāpi saṃyoge cakṣurāder yadutthitam |
    2. viṣayāntaravijñānaṃ tatpratyakṣaṃ prasajyate ||
    1. satsamprayoganirdeśo vyarthaś ced, etad eva hi |
    2. pratipādyaṃ parasyāpi lakṣaṇāsiddhir eva ca ||
    1. svapnādīnāṃ nivṛttir vā phalaṃ tasya bhaviṣyati |
    2. tasmād vidhyanuvāditvaṃ nānukte lakṣaṇe bhavet ||
    1. tena naiṣā vacovyaktir yatsatīndriyasaṅgame |
    2. vijñānaṃ jāyate tasya pratyakṣatvaṃ pratīyatām ||
    1. pratyakṣaṃ yajjane siddhaṃ tasyaivandharmakatvataḥ |
    2. vidyamānopalambhatvaṃ tena dharme nimittatā ||
    1. evaṃlakṣaṇatvaṃ ca na svarūpavivakṣayā |
    2. evaṃliṅgakam ityetad bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇyate ||
    1. yato 'sti tatra dharmo 'yaṃ vidyamānopalambhanam |
    2. tasmāt tena prasiddhena gamyatām animittatā ||
    1. pratyakṣatvamado hetuḥ śeṣaṃ hetuprasiddhaye |
    2. asmād ādau prasiddhatvād yogyartham abhidhīyate ||
    1. prakṛtena ca sambandhaḥ śeṣāprāmāṇyadarśanāt |
    2. tadaprāmāṇyasiddhiś ca sambandhāder anīkṣaṇāt ||
    1. śakyam anyāpramāṇatvam iti sūtrair na paṭhyate |
    2. na ca paryanuyogo 'tra lakṣaṇānupayogataḥ ||
    1. na ca nyūnātirekādiprasaṅgo lakṣaṇaṃ prati |
    2. sarvathā lokasiddhatvād dharmo 'yaṃ tāvad iṣyate ||
    1. tataś ca mṛgatṛṣṇādi na pratyakṣaṃ prasajyate |
    2. animittaprasaṅgas tu tasyāpi na nivāryate ||
    1. atītānāgate 'py arthe sūkṣme vyavahite 'pi ca |
    2. pratyakṣaṃ yoginām iṣṭaṃ kaiś cin muktātmanām api ||
    1. vidyamānopalambhatvam asiddhaṃ tatra tān prati |
    2. bhaviṣyattvasya vā hetor tadgrāhyair vyabhicāritā ||
    1. mā bhūtāmiti tenāha lokasiddhaṃ sad ity ayam |
    2. na lokavyatiriktaṃ hi pratyakṣaṃ yoginām api ||
    1. pratyakṣatvena tasyāpi vidyamānopalambhanam |
    2. satsamprayogajatvaṃ vāpy asmatpratyakṣavad bhavet ||
    1. teṣām avartamāne 'rthe vā nāmotpadyate matiḥ |
    2. pratyakṣaṃ sā tatas tv eva nābhilāṣasmṛtādivat ||
    1. loke cāpy aprasiddhatvāt pratyakṣatvapramāṇataḥ |
    2. pratibhāvad dvayāsattvaṃ sad ity etena kathyate ||
    1. laukikī pratibhā yadvat pratyakṣādyanapekṣiṇī |
    2. na niścayāya paryāptā tathā syād yoginām api ||
    1. avidyamānasaṃyogāt syāc cet pratyakṣadhīḥ kva cit |
    2. bhaviṣyaty api dharme syāc chaktety āha sad ity ayam ||
    1. pratyakṣaḥ prāganuṣṭhānān na dharmo 'nuṣṭhito 'pi vā |
    2. phalasādhanarūpeṇa tadānīṃ yena nāsty asau ||
    1. asmatpratyakṣavac cāpi vidyamānopalambhanam |
    2. pratyakṣaṃ dhyāyināṃ dharme pratyakṣatvāc ca neṣyate ||
    1. avidyamānasaṃyogāt pratyakṣatvanirākṛtiḥ |
    2. yogināṃ kena labhyeta neṣṭaṃ sadgrahaṇaṃ yadi ||
    1. saptamyāpi tu labhyeta sadarthaḥ, kalpanā punaḥ |
    2. pareṣāṃ vāraṇīyeti yatno jaimininā kṛtaḥ ||
    1. samyagarthe ca saṃśabdo duṣprayoganivāraṇaḥ |
    2. prayoga indriyāṇāṃ ca vyāpāro 'rtheṣu kathyate ||
    1. duṣṭatvāc chuktikāyogo vāryate, rajatekṣaṇāt |
    2. evaṃ saty anuvādatvaṃ lakṣaṇasyāpi sambhavet ||
    1. tataś cāprāpyakāritvād yad bauddhaiḥ śrotracakṣuṣoḥ |
    2. lakṣaṇāvyāptisiddhyarthaṃ saṃyogo neti kīrtyate ||
    1. prāpyagrahaṇapakṣe hi sāntarāgrahaṇaṃ kila |
    2. adhiṣṭānādhikaś cārtho na gṛhyeta tvagādivat ||
    1. vyāpāramātravācitvād aviruddhaṃ tad atra naḥ |
    2. yadi vārthārjavasthānaṃ samprayogo 'tra varṇyate ||
    1. yogyatālakṣaṇo vācyaḥ saṃyogaḥ kāryalakṣitaḥ |
    2. sāṃkhyādīn vā vinirjitya prāptipakṣo 'tra dūṣyatām ||
    1. tayoś ca prāpyakāritvam indriyatvāt tvagādivat |
    2. ke cit tayoḥ śarīrāc ca bahirvṛttiṃ pracakṣate ||
    1. cikitsādiprayogaś ca yo 'dhiṣṭhāne prayujyate |
    2. so 'pi tasyaiva saṃskāra ādheyasyopakārakaḥ ||
    1. taddeśaś cāpi saṃskāraḥ sarvavyāptyartha ucyate |
    2. cakṣurādyupakāraś ca pādādāv api dṛśyate ||
    1. tasmān naikāntataḥ śakyaṃ saṃskārāt tatra vartanam |
    2. bahirvṛttis tayoś ceṣṭā pṛthvagrā santatāpi ca ||
    1. adhiṣṭhānādhikaṃ tena gṛhyate yatra yādṛśam |
    2. pṛthutvaṃ vṛttibhāge syād, dūre 'pi grahaṇaṃ tathā ||
    1. dīpaprabhā yathā tasmin vinaśyati vinaśyati |
    2. tathā bahirgatāpy eṣā mūlacchedād vinaśyati ||
    1. adhiṣṭhānapidhāne tu saty apy ucchinnayatnayā |
    2. tayārtho 'nupanītatvād ātmanā nānubhūyate ||
    1. vicchinna iti buddhiḥ syād adhiṣṭhānam apekṣya ca |
    2. śabde tv ādhikyavicchedau bhrāntyaivoktāv asambhavāt ||
    1. puruṣendriyaśabdau ca vyavadhānena kalpitau |
    2. puruṣo laukiko vā syād yo vāsmin sādhayiṣyate ||
    1. vikriyā jñānarūpāsya na nityatve virotsyate |
    2. buddhijanmeti cāpy āha jāyamānapramāṇatām ||
    1. vyāpāraḥ kārakāṇāṃ hi dṛṣṭo janmātirekataḥ |
    2. pramāṇe 'pi tathā mā bhūd iti janma vivakṣyate ||
    1. na hi tat kṣaṇam apy āste, jāyate vāpramātmakam |
    2. yenārthagrahaṇe paścād vyāpriyetendriyādivat ||
    1. tena janmaiva viṣaye buddher vyāpāra iṣyate |
    2. tad eva ca pramārūpaṃ tadvatī karaṇaṃ ca dhīḥ ||
    1. janma cāvyatirekeṇa bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇitam |
    2. tac ca bhūtabhaviṣyattvāt kṛtaṃ buddher viśeṣaṇam ||
    1. yadāpy aulūkyasiddhāntāt samavāyasya janmatā |
    2. buddhis tatrendriyādhīnā tena pratyakṣamaśnute ||
    1. pramāṇaphalabhāvaś ca yayeṣṭaṃ parikalpyatām |
    2. sarvathāpy animittatvaṃ vidyamānopalambhanāt ||
    1. yadvendriyaṃ pramāṇaṃ syāt tasya vārthena saṅgatiḥ |
    2. manaso vendriyair yoga ātmanā sarva eva vā ||
    1. tadā jñānaṃ phalam, tatra vyāpārāc ca pramāṇatā |
    2. vyāpāro na yadā teṣāṃ tadā notpadyate phalam ||
    1. na ca sarvātmanākṣeṇa sambandho 'rthasya vidyate |
    2. yena sarvārthabodhaḥ syāt tatpramāṇābhidhāyinām ||
    1. prāptimātraṃ hi sambandho nendriyasyābhyupeyate |
    2. mā bhūt kāraṇamātreṇa tvacā rūpāvadhāraṇam ||
    1. yathā pramāṇaniṣpattau yogyatvād indriyārthayoḥ |
    2. niyatā saṅgatir hetuḥ phale 'py evaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
    1. yogasya dvyāśrayatve 'pi bhavatyanyatarāśrayaḥ |
    2. vyapadeśaḥ, atha vāpy akṣaṃ tatrāsādhāraṇaṃ bhavet ||
    1. saṃyoge tv ātmamanasoḥ syāc ced viṣayabhinnatā |
    2. pramāṇaphalayoḥ, nāsau, arthe hi vyāpṛtaṃ dvayam ||
    1. athāpy āśraya iṣṭas te na yogād viṣayāntaram |
    2. ātmasthatvena vijñānaṃ na bhinnaviṣayaṃ tataḥ ||
    1. prakṛṣṭasādhanatvāc ca pratyāsatteḥ sa eva naḥ |
    2. karaṇaṃ tena nānyatra kārake syāt pramāṇatā ||
    1. pramāṇe sarvasaṃyoge doṣo naiko 'pi vidyate |
    2. pramāṇaṃ tv indriyaṃ yasya tasyaiko viṣayaḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
    1. pramāṇaphalate buddhyor viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ |
    2. yadā tadāpi pūrvoktā bhinnārthatvanirākriyā ||
    1. viśeṣaṇe tu boddhavye yadālocanamātrakam |
    2. prasūte niścayaṃ paścāt tasya prāmāṇyakalpanā ||
    1. niścayas tu phalaṃ tatra, nāsāv ālocite tadā |
    2. tadā naiva pramāṇatvaṃ syād arthānavadhāraṇāt ||
    1. hānādibuddhiphalatā pramāṇaṃ ced viśeṣyadhīḥ |
    2. upakārādisaṃsmṛtyā vyavāyaś cet, iyaṃ phalam ||
    1. viṣayaikatvam icchaṃs tu yaḥ pramāṇaṃ phalaṃ vadet |
    2. sādhyasādhanayor bhedo laukikas tena bādhitaḥ ||
    1. chedane khadiraprāpte palāśe na cchidā yathā |
    2. tathaiva paraśor loke cchidayā saha naikatā ||
    1. bhavate bhedahānena rucitā viṣayaikatā |
    2. tattyāgena parebhyas tu bhedo rucim upāgataḥ ||
    1. karaṇatvopacāras tu phale cet kalpyate tvayā |
    2. kathañ cid viṣayaikatvaṃ parair vā kiṃ na kalpyate ||
    1. paricchedaphalatvena vṛttasyānantarasya naḥ |
    2. pramāṇatvaṃ bhavej jñāne pramāṇe tu paraṃ phalam ||
    1. svasaṃvittiphalatvaṃ tu tanniṣedhān na yujyate |
    2. pramāṇe viṣayākāre bhinnārthatvān na yujyate ||
    1. svākāraś ca svasaṃvittiṃ muktvā nānyaḥ pratīyate |
    2. prāmāṇyaṃ yasya kalpyeta svasaṃvittiphalaṃ prati ||
    1. svākārasya paricchedo na cākārāntarād vinā |
    2. tasyāpy evaṃ tathā ca syān nākārāntaḥ kadā cana ||
    1. na cāsañcetitaḥ sattāṃ svākāraḥ pratipadyate |
    2. grāhye ca viṣayākāre grāhako 'nyo na labhyate ||
    1. manasas tv indriyatvena pratyakṣā dhīḥ sukhādiṣu |
    2. manasā samprayukto hi tāny ātmā pratipadyate ||
    1. sambaddhaṃ vartamānaṃ ca grahyate cakṣurādinā |
    2. sāmānyaṃ vā viśeṣo vā grāhyaṃ nāto 'tra kalpyate ||
    1. lakṣaṇaṃ yac ca yair uktaṃ pratyakṣe laukike sati |
    2. vidyamānopalambhitvāt sarvasyaivānimittatā ||
    1. nirvikalpakapakṣe tu sutarām animittatā |
    2. sādhyasādhanasambandho nāvikalpya hi gṛhyate ||
    1. kathaṃ pratyakṣapūrvatvam anumānādi no bhavet |
    2. yadā smṛtyasamarthatvān nirvikalpendriyasya dhīḥ ||
    1. na cāvikalpya liṅgasya liṅgisambandhayos tathā |
    2. gṛhītiḥ, upamāne 'pi sādṛśyagrahaṇāt smṛteḥ ||
    1. arthāpattiḥ punaḥ prāyo nānyadṛṣṭe 'rtha iṣyate |
    2. pravartate ca yaṃ dṛṣṭvā so 'py arthaḥ savikalpakaḥ ||
    1. yatra cānumitaṃ liṅgaṃ sūryagatyādi liṅgi ca |
    2. tatra pratyakṣapūrvatvaṃ katham adhyavasīyate ||
    1. pratyakṣāvagate cārthe kutas teṣāṃ pramāṇatā |
    2. tair yadā sa pratīyeta tadā nākṣasya gocaraḥ ||
    1. atha kasya cid arthasya jñānāt tatpūrvatā bhavet |
    2. tadārthasya bhaviṣyattvaṃ na syād ajñānakāraṇam ||
    1. vartamāne hi kasmiṃś cid vijñāte 'rthe 'kṣabuddhibhiḥ |
    2. liṅgād avidyamāno 'pi dharmo gamyeta tais tadā ||
    1. pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā ca varṇān vede 'pi gṛhyate |
    2. prameyam iti so 'pi syāt tatpūrvatvād akāraṇam ||
    1. ke cit tatpūrvakatvaṃ tu hetur naiveti manvate |
    2. tatpūrvakatvād yat tāvat prāmāṇyaṃ tadasambhavaḥ ||
    1. pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā ca, liṅgādyanyatamaṃ dhruvam |
    2. pravṛttir anumānāder na ca dharme 'sti tādṛśam ||
    1. anumānānumānāder na cāpy astīha sambhavaḥ |
    2. sambandhaliṅgiliṅgānāṃ pūrvasiddher asambhavāt ||
    1. sattā ca nānumānena kasya cit pratipadyate |
    2. dharmeṇānyad viśeṣyaṃ cet, pakṣo 'siddhaviśeṣaṇaḥ ||
    1. tasmād adṛṣṭapūrvatvāt kena cid vastunā saha |
    2. dharmasya nānumeyatvam asādhāraṇavastuvat ||
    1. adṛṣṭasadṛśatvāc ca svyaṃ cānupalambhanāt |
    2. dharmasya nopameyatvam asādhāraṇavad bhavet ||
    1. nanv arthāpattir evaṃ syāj jagadvaicitryadarśanāt |
    2. sukhiduḥkhādibhedo hi nādṛṣṭāt kāraṇād ṛte ||
    1. dṛṣṭasya vyabhicāritvāt tadabhāve 'pi sambhavāt |
    2. sevāvyayanatulyatve dṛṣṭā ca phalabhinnatā ||
    1. syād evaṃ yadi śakyeta svābhāvikanivāraṇā |
    2. karmaśakteś ca vaicitrye hetur anyo bhaved yadi ||
    1. yathā ca phalavaicitrye karmaṇāṃ śaktatā svataḥ |
    2. tathā ca citratā loke svabhāvād upapatsyate ||
    1. adharme dharmarūpe vā hy avibhakte phalaṃ prati |
    2. kim apy astīti vijñānaṃ narāṇāṃ kvopayujyate ||
    1. kiṃ nu yāgād ito dukhaṃ hiṃsādeḥ kiṃ sukhodbhavaḥ |
    2. svargaputrādibhedaś ca kīdṛśāt karmabhedataḥ ||
    1. iti yāvad avijñānaṃ tāvan naiva pravartate |
    2. pravṛttyaṅgaṃ ca yajjñānaṃ tasya mūlaṃ pratīkṣyate ||
    1. tasmāt siddhe 'pi sāmānye viśeṣo nāgamād ṛte |
    2. viśeṣasya tu jijñāsā sūtrakāreṇa sūtritā ||
    1. gamyamāne viśeṣe ca tadantarbhāvakāritaḥ |
    2. sāmānyapratyayo 'pi syāc chāstrād evety akāraṇam ||
    1. yathārthāpattir evaṃ ca nānumānopameṣyate |
    2. śāstraṃ cet tadapekṣeta tasyaiva syāt pramāṇatā ||
    1. pratyakṣāgrahaṇaṃ yat tu liṅgāder avikalpanāt |
    2. tan na, iṣṭatvād vikalpasyāpy artharūpopakāriṇaḥ ||
    1. asti hy ālocanā jñānaṃ prathamaṃ nirvikapakam |
    2. bālamūkādivijñānasadṛśaṃ śuddhavastujam ||
    1. na viśeṣo na sāmānyaṃ tadānīmanubhūyate |
    2. tayor ādhārabhūtā tu, vyaktir evāvasīyate ||
    1. mahāsāmānyam anyais tu dravyaṃ sad iti cocyate |
    2. sāmānyaviṣayatvaṃ ca pratyakṣasyaivam āśritam ||
    1. viśeṣās tu pratīyante savikalpakabuddhibhiḥ |
    2. te ca ke cit pratidravyaṃ ke cid bahuṣu saṃśritāḥ ||
    1. tān akalpayad utpannaṃ vyāvṛttānugatātmanā |
    2. gavyaśve copajātaṃ tu pratyakṣaṃ na viśiṣyate ||
    1. tad ayuktam, pratidravyaṃ bhinnarūpopalambhanāt |
    2. na hy ākhyātum aśakyatvād bhedo nāstīti gamyate ||
    1. nirvikalpakabodhe 'pi dvyātmakasyāpi vastunaḥ |
    2. grahaṇam, lakṣaṇākhyeyaṃ jñātrā śuddhaṃ tu gṛhyate ||
    1. na cāsādhāraṇatvena paravyāvṛttyakalpanāt |
    2. viśeṣānugamākḷpteḥ sāmānyam iti nāpi tat ||
    1. tataḥ paraṃ punarvastudharmair jātyādibhir yayā |
    2. buddhyāvasīyate sāpi pratyakṣatvena sammatā ||
    1. karaṇaṃ cendriyaṃ buddher na tatra jñānam āhitam |
    2. tataḥ smṛtyasamarthatvād vikalpo 'to na vāryate ||
    1. ātmany eva sthitaṃ jñānam, sa hi boddhātra gamyate |
    2. smaraṇe cāsya sāmarthyaṃ sandhānādau ca vidyate ||
    1. tenendriyārthasambandhe vicyamāne smarann api |
    2. vikalpayan svadharmeṇa vastu pratyakṣavān naraḥ ||
    1. tac caitadindriyādhīnam iti tair vyapadiśyate |
    2. tadasambandhajātaṃ tu naiva pratyakṣam iṣyate ||
    1. punaḥ punarvikalpe 'pi satī jātiḥ pratīyate |
    2. tatsambandhānusāreṇa sarvaṃ pratyakṣam iṣyate ||
    1. na hi praviṣṭamātrāṇām uṣṇād garbhagṛhādiṣu |
    2. arthā na pratibhāntīti gṛhyante nendriyaiḥ punaḥ ||
    1. yathā tv ābhāsamātreṇa pūrvaṃ jñātvā svarūpataḥ |
    2. paścāt tatrāvabudhyante tathā jātyādidharmataḥ ||
    1. yadi tv ālocya saṃmīlya netre kaś cid vikalpayet |
    2. na syāt pratyakṣatā tasya sambandhānanusārataḥ ||
    1. asambaddhavikalpe 'pi tulyam ātmādi kāraṇam |
    2. tenāsādhāraṇatvaṃ syād atrākṣasyaiva kalpane ||
    1. nirvikalpakabodhe 'pi nākṣaṃ kevalakāraṇam |
    2. tatpāramparyajāte vā rūḍhiḥ syāt paṅkajādivat ||
    1. animittaiva vā rūḍhiḥ sutarāṃ savikalpakam |
    2. pratyakṣaṃ sammataṃ loke na tathā nirvikalpakam ||
    1. vṛddhaprayogagamyāś ca śabdārthāḥ sarva eva naḥ |
    2. tena yatra prayukto 'yaṃ na tasmād apanīyate ||
    1. siddhānugamamātraṃ hi kartuṃ yuktaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ |
    2. na sarvalokasiddhasya lakṣaṇena nivartanam ||
    1. kalpanāyāḥ svasaṃvittāv indriyādhīnatā katham |
    2. manas tatrendriyaṃ cet syād gotvādāv api tatsamam ||
    1. svasaṃvittau tad iṣṭaṃ cet, loko na hy evam icchati |
    2. tasmād rūḍhatvam eṣṭavyaṃ pāribhāṣikatāpi vā ||
    1. manasas tv indriyatvena sudhaduḥkhādibuddhiṣu |
    2. yathā pratyakṣataivaṃ nas tadadhīnā bhaviṣyati ||
    1. tadadhīnatvasāmye 'pi kalpanāpoḍhaśabdanāt |
    2. pratyakṣaṃ kiñ cid eveṣṭaṃ yathā tatra tathaiva naḥ ||
    1. liṅgādyabhāvataś cāpi nānumānādidhīr iyam |
    2. bādhakapratyayāsattvān nāprāmāṇyaṃ ca yujyate ||
    1. na ca parvamadṛṣṭatvāt smṛtitvam upapadyate |
    2. tasmāt pratyakṣam evedam, vyavahāras tathaiva ca ||
    1. jātyādyarthāntaraṃ yasmād atadrūpe 'pi vastuni |
    2. bhavaty adhyasya dhīs tasmān mṛgatṛṣṇādibhiḥ samā ||
    1. naitadaśvādibuddhīnām adhyāropādyasambhavāt |
    2. sthitaṃ naiva hi jātyādeḥ paratvaṃ vyaktito hi naḥ ||
    1. yadi hy ekāntato bhinnaṃ viśeṣyāt syād viśeṣaṇam |
    2. svānurūpāṃ sadā buddhiṃ viśeṣye janayet katham ||
    1. sphaṭikādau tu lākṣādisvarūpā yā matir bhavet |
    2. avyutpannasya sā mithyā vyutpannānāṃ hi bhedadhīḥ ||
    1. na tu jātyādinirmuktaṃ vastu dṛṣṭaṃ kadā cana |
    2. tadvimokena vā tāni lākṣādisphaṭikādivat ||
    1. tatrāpi cen na dṛśyeta bhedaḥ kaiś cit kadā cana |
    2. raktādibuddhisamyaktvaṃ vinivāryeta kena vā ||
    1. na cāpy ayutasiddhānāṃ sambandhitvena kalpanā |
    2. nāniṣpannasya sambandhaḥ, niṣpattau yutasiddhatā ||
    1. tathā ca sati sambandhe hetuḥ kaś cin na vidyate |
    2. tasmāc cāpi na sambandhaḥ padārthānāṃ pratīyate ||
    1. samavāyaviyogāc ca viśleṣaḥ syāt parasparam |
    2. tatkḷptāvavyavasthā syāt tasya tasyānyasaṅgateḥ ||
    1. atha tasyātmarūpatvān nānyasambandhakalpanā |
    2. abhedāt samavāyo 'stu svarūpaṃ dharmadharmiṇoḥ ||
    1. na hi sa vyatiriktaḥ san sambandhaṃ pratipadyate |
    2. tasmiṃs tābhyām abhinne tu na nānātvaṃ tayor bhavet ||
    1. nanu dharmātirekeṇa dharmiṇo 'nupalambhanāt |
    2. tatsaṅghamātra evāyaṃ gavādiḥ syād vanādivat ||
    1. āvirbhāvatirobhāvadharmakeṣv anuyāyi yat |
    2. taddharmi yatra vā jñānaṃ prāgdharmagrahaṇād bhavet ||
    1. ato jātyādirūpeṇa dharmi yad gṛhyate naiḥ |
    2. pārarūpyaṃ na tasyāstīty aprāmāṇyaṃ na yujyate ||
    1. yasyāpi vyatirekaḥ syād dharmebhyo dharmiṇaḥ sphuṭaḥ |
    2. nityaṃ tasyāpi tādrūpyān na mithyātvaṃ prasajyate ||
    1. yo hy asadrūpasaṃvedyaḥ saṃvedyetān yathā punaḥ |
    2. sa mithyā na tu tenaiva yo nityam avagamyate ||
    1. na cānekendriyagrāhyaṃ bhinnatāṃ pratipadyate |
    2. mā bhūd bhinnaśarīrasthagrāhyatvād bhinnarūpatā ||
    1. jātyabhedād abhedaś cet, indriyatvena tatsamam |
    2. tulyabuddher ato bhinnā na sattendriyabhedataḥ ||
    1. buddhibhedāc ca naikatvaṃ rūpādīnāṃ prasajyate |
    2. ekānekatvam iṣṭaṃ vā sattārūpādirūpataḥ ||
    1. kva cic ca saṅkarān nākṣam ekam ity avasīyate |
    2. dārḍhyadaurbalyabhedena vyavasthāpi yataḥ kva cit ||
    1. yathā hi manasaḥ sārdhaṃ rūpādau cakṣurādinā |
    2. pravṛttiḥ sukhaduḥkhādau kevalasyaiva dṛśyate ||
    1. na kva cit saṅkarābhāvāt sarvatraiva nivartate |
    2. kva cic ca saṅkaraṃ dṛṣṭvā saṅkaro 'nyatra kalpyate ||
    1. śrotrāder upaghāte 'pi śabdādismṛtidarśanāt |
    2. vartamānasya cājñānād vyavasthā sampratīyate ||
    1. ekaṃ yadi bhaved akṣaṃ sarvair gṛhyeta vā na vā |
    2. kalpyate śaktibhedaś cet, śaktir evendriyaṃ bhavet ||
    1. śṛṇuyād badhiraḥ śabdaṃ saṅkare cakṣurādinā |
    2. manaso vā svatantratve vartamānārthabuddhiṣu ||
    1. na smared badhiraḥ śabdaṃ śrotraṃ cet smṛtikāraṇam |
    2. smṛtivad vā bhaved asya vartamānārthadhīr api ||
    1. smṛtiś ca na bhavet paścād gṛhṇīyāt tan na cen manaḥ |
    2. śrotragrahaṇavelāyām, na cāsarvā smṛtir bhavet ||
    1. bodhātmakatayā puṃsaḥ sarvatra grahaṇaṃ bhavet |
    2. yugapadviṣaye 'py asya karaṇāpekṣitā na cet ||
    1. tasmāj jñānānusāreṇa vyavasthāsaṅkarau kva cit |
    2. grāhyagrāhakaśaktibhyaḥ kāryadvāreṇa kalpitau ||
    1. cakṣūrūpādibhedas tu pañcadhaiva vyavasthitaḥ |
    2. tena nīlādibhede 'pi nendriyānantyakalpanā ||
    1. tasmāt pañcabhir apy akṣair bodhaḥ sattāguṇatvayoḥ |
    2. dravyamūrtau punardvābhyāṃ rūpādāv ekaśaḥ sthitaḥ ||
    1. nanu jātyādirūpe 'pi śabdābhedopacārataḥ |
    2. pravartamānā mithya syād buddhī rūpeṣu buddhivat ||
    1. na śabdābhedarūpeṇa buddhir artheṣu jāyate |
    2. prāk śabdād yādṛśī buddhiḥ śabdād api hi tādṛśī ||
    1. nanu gotvādirūpeṇa gavākārādibuddhayaḥ |
    2. na prāk śabdārthasambandhajñānāt santi kadā cana ||
    1. jātyādes tatsvarūpaṃ ced aśabdajño 'pi lakṣayet |
    2. anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ śabdarūpatvaniścayaḥ ||
    1. yathā rūpādayo bhinnāḥ prāk śabdāt svātmanaiva tu |
    2. gamyante tadvad evaitat saṃjñitvaṃ kevalaṃ param ||
    1. na cāvikalpitaḥ śabdād iti vācyo na gṛhyate |
    2. tenāgṛhītaśabdo 'pi gotvādīn pratipadyate ||
    1. śrutisaṃsparśabodhe 'pi gotvādīn pratipadyate |
    2. vivekād arthaśabdānāṃ cakṣuḥ śrotradhiyā kṛtāt ||
    1. anantadharmake dharmiṇy ekadharmāvadhāraṇe |
    2. śabdo 'bhyupāyamātraṃ syān nātmādhyāropakāraṇam ||
    1. na copeye 'bhyupāyasya rūpādhyāsaḥ prasajyate |
    2. na hi dīpendriyādīnāṃ rūpādhyāropa iṣyate ||
    1. nityaṃ yadi ca gotvādi śabdarūpeṇa gṛhyate |
    2. rūpāntaraṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ ced bhedādhyāsau kuto nvimau ||
    1. yady abhedo na mithyātvam, bhedaś cet syāt svarūpataḥ |
    2. nādhyāropaprasaṅgaḥ syād bhrāntyā tv adhyāsakalpanā ||
    1. śabdenaiva ca nirdeśo gṛhīte 'rthe 'vakalpate |
    2. gaur ity eva ca nirdeśo vācyatadbuddhivādinām ||
    1. nirdeśatulyatāyāṃ ca śrotrā vaktṛsvarūpatā |
    2. śabdajñānaprameyeṣu vijñānasyāvasīyate ||
    1. bhrāntihetusamānatve 'py upāyatvānmatiśrutī |
    2. manyate 'rthe samadhyaste nārthādhyāsaṃ tayoḥ punaḥ ||
    1. gotve sāsnādimadrūpāṅgādirūpābhidhāyake |
    2. nirākārobhayajñāne saṃvittiḥ paramārthataḥ ||
    1. yadi cābhedarūpeṇa śabdenārthaḥ pratīyate |
    2. ekarūpatvam akṣādau devanādeḥ prasajyate ||
    1. syād anakṣanivṛtyā cet, na prāk śabdāt pratīyate |
    2. gavādiṣv api tulyaṃ cet, nekarūpasya darśanāt ||
    1. traye bibhītakādīnāṃ naikadharmānvayo 'sti hi |
    2. śabdaḥ sādhāraṇas teṣāṃ jātiśabdād vilakṣaṇaḥ ||
    1. parasparavibhinnaṃ tu jñāyate 'trākṛtitrayam |
    2. tadadhyāse na yujyeta tadrūpasyāvibhāgataḥ ||
    1. bhinnāḥ syur akṣaśabdāś cet, nārthe saṃśayadarśanāt |
    2. na sāmānyād ṛte sa syād, rūpābhedaś ca gamyate ||
    1. bhavatyādau ca bhinne 'pi nāmākhyātatvasaṃjñayā |
    2. rūpaikatvena cādhyāse tulyārthatvaṃ prasajyate ||
    1. śabdaniṣpattyabhedāc ca tiṅantārthasya sādhyatā |
    2. katham, kathaṃ ca mūrtārtho vācake mūrtivarjite ||
    1. gavāśvaśuklaśabdāder vācyarūpānapekṣaṇe |
    2. vācakatvavyavasthānaṃ kathaṃ jātiguṇādiṣu ||
    1. vṛkṣaplakṣādiśabdānāṃ tulye bhede ghaṭādibhiḥ |
    2. viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ katham arthānapekṣayā ||
    1. sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca na syad vācakabuddhivat |
    2. ekatra copasaṃhāro na buddhyor nirvikalpake ||
    1. vastumātre sa ced evaṃ sarveṣām ekavācyatā |
    2. bhaved gavādiśabdānāṃ sarvair vastu hi gamyate ||
    1. na cāsādhāraṇe bhede nīlotpalam itīṣyate |
    2. na hi śabdapravṛttiḥ syād anyatrānyatra ceṣyate ||
    1. na ca nīlotpalaṃ nāma vastvekaṃ kiñ cid iṣyate |
    2. śabdārthayor yato bhedo gamyate 'vayavānugaḥ ||
    1. śabdadvayasya cādhyāsaḥ paryāyeṣv api dṛśyate |
    2. ekādhikaraṇās tena syus te nīlotpalādivat ||
    1. na cānavagate pūrvaṃ padam arthe prayujyate |
    2. tatra sambandhavelāyāṃ kīdṛśo 'rthaḥ pratīyate ||
    1. tadānīṃ nārtharūpe hi śabdarūpasya sambhavaḥ |
    2. na cāsādhāraṇāṃśena sambandhānugamaḥ kva cit ||
    1. tatra pūrvānapekṣatve yadyātmādhyāsaśaktatā |
    2. śabdasya prathame 'pi syāc chravaṇe 'dhyastarūpatā ||
    1. mama vācyānabhijñatvān na bhavet smaraṇaṃ tataḥ |
    2. bhavatas tv artharūpasya vācakeṣv api darśanāt ||
    1. yathā tv ajñātaśabdānāṃ vācye taddhīr na jāyate |
    2. tathaivājñātavācyānām upalabdhe 'pi vācake ||
    1. tasmān nātīva vācyānāṃ vācakādhīnatā bhavet |
    2. smārakatvāc ca teṣv eva pāratantryaṃ pratīyate ||
    1. tena sambandhavelāyām arthātmā yo 'vasīyate |
    2. śabdād api sa eveti nārtharūpaṃ praṇaśyati ||
    1. pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yāṃ śabdaḥ kurute matim |
    2. tādātmyaṃ tasya śabdasya na kathañ cit pratīyate ||
    1. karahastādiśabdebhyaḥ śabdarūpasya bhedataḥ |
    2. bhinno 'rthaḥ sampratīyeta tadadhyāropakalpane ||
    1. ātmādhyāsas tu sādṛśyād uparāgāc ca dṛśyate |
    2. na tāvad arthasādṛśyaṃ śabdasyeha pratīyate ||
    1. na cānurāgaḥ śabdena bhinnadeśasya yujyate |
    2. dūrasthapratibimbaṃ ca nārūpasya pratīyate ||
    1. śabdasarvagatatvena yadyarthaprāptir ucyate |
    2. sarvārthānāṃ bhavec chabdaiḥ sarvair evānurañjanam ||
    1. na ca bhinnendriyagrāhyaṃ kiñ cid asty anurāgakṛt |
    2. na hi lākṣānurakte 'pi sphaṭike dhīs tvagādibhiḥ ||
    1. anumānāgamau mithyā syātāmadhyāsakalpane |
    2. nirūpaṇasya mithyātvāt sarvābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||
    1. tathās tv iti yadi brūyāt, mithyā svavacane sati |
    2. katham evaṃ vaded artho nānṛtād dhi pratīyate ||
    1. śūnyavādottarāccāpi yathārthaṃ buddhiśabdayoḥ |
    2. pravṛttir na tu tat tantram artharūpaṃ kadā cana ||
    1. tasmāt prāg api ye śabdād bhirnnaikatvādibuddhibhiḥ |
    2. gṛhyante sarvadā teṣāṃ paramārthastitā bhavet ||
    1. śabdābhyupāyake 'py arthe tadabhāve ca yady api |
    2. arthabuddhir na jāyeta nārthe rūpaṃ praṇaśyati ||
    1. cakṣurāder abhāve hi rūpādyātmā na gṛhyate |
    2. svarūpanāśo rūpādes tāvanmātreṇa neṣyate ||
    1. sambandhasya ca nityatvān nārethasya syād arūpatā |
    2. yugapanna hi sarveṣām anyākārārthavedanam ||
    1. tadākāre 'pi tadvac ced, dvaye sati parīkṣyatām |
    2. kiṃ nv arthasyātathābhāvo grahītuḥ kiṃ nv aśaktatā ||
    1. sadasadbhāvayor arthe virodhitvād asambhavaḥ |
    2. grahītṛbhedāc chaktatvam aśaktatvaṃ ca yujyate ||
    1. yathāndhānandhayoḥ pārśve rūpasyety abhidhāsyate |
    2. tenārthe dhvanyupāyasya tadhīrnānyasya jāyate ||
    1. devadattādiśabde tu sambandhādyatvadarśanāt |
    2. arthasyānityatāyāṃ ca tādrūpyasyāpy anityatā ||
    1. tatrāpy autpattikī śaktis tadrūpapratyayaṃ prati |
    2. grāhyagrāhakayor iṣṭā niyogasya tv anityatā ||
    1. tatra sarvair atādrūpyaṃ prāṅniyogāt pratīyate |
    2. teneṣṭam eva mithyātvaṃ kaiś cid adhyāsakalpane ||
    1. yadā tu yādṛśaḥ piṇḍaḥ pūrvaṃ śabdāt pratīyate |
    2. tādṛśasmaraṇe hetuḥ śabdas tatra yathārthatā ||
    1. niyogāt parato vāpi śabdena vyajyatām iyam |
    2. tadgrāhyaśaktir arthasya, pārarūpyaṃ na tāvatā ||
    1. sarvākāraparicchedyaśakte 'rthe vācake 'pi vā |
    2. sarvākārārthavijñānasamarthe niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ ||
    1. tatra śabdārthasambandhaṃ pramātuḥ smarato 'pi yā |
    2. buddhiḥ pūrvagṛhītārthasandhānād upajāyate ||
    1. cakṣuṣā sannikṛṣṭe 'rthe nāpratyakṣam asau bhavet |
    2. viviktā eva te 'py arthāḥ smṛtipratyakṣagocarāḥ ||
    1. smaryete śabdasambandhau mā bhūt pratyakṣatā tayoḥ |
    2. tadapratyakṣabhāvena na tv arthasyāpi vāryate ||
    1. gṛhītam api gotvādi smṛtispṛṣṭaṃ ca yady api |
    2. tathāpi vyatirekeṇa pūrvabodhāt pratīyate ||
    1. vyaktikālādibhedena tatrāsty avasaro miteḥ |
    2. yaḥ pūrvāvagato 'ṃśo 'tra sa na nāma pramīyate ||
    1. idānīn tanam astitvaṃ na hi pūrvadhiyā gatam |
    2. na hi smaraṇato yatprāk tat pratyakṣam itīdṛśam ||
    1. vacanaṃ rājakīyaṃ vā vaidikaṃ vāpi vidyate |
    2. na cāpi smaraṇāt paścād indriyasya pravartanam ||
    1. vāryate kena cin nātastat tadānīṃ praduṣyati |
    2. tenendriyārthasambandhāt prāgūrdhvaṃ vāpi yatsmṛteḥ ||
    1. vijñānaṃ jāyate sarvaṃ pratyakṣam iti gamyatām |
    2. vimanaskā yadā ke cit sambaddham api cendriyaiḥ ||
    1. na budhyante tathā cānye sādṛśyādivimohitāḥ |
    2. tatra yo 'rthaṃ vivekena kauśalāt sadṛśeṣv api ||
    1. sūkṣmaṃ vāpi prapadyeta tasya bhrāntirnaṃ tāvatā |
    2. yathā ṣaḍjādibhedena gāne laukikavaidike ||
    1. vivekenāvagacchanti yeṣāṃ tatsaṃskṛtā matiḥ |
    2. gānamātraṃ vijānanti tatrānadhikṛtās tu ye ||
    1. tadajñānān na mithyātvaṃ vaktuṃ śakyaṃ vivekinām |
    2. te hi ṣaḍjādiśabdebhyo vināpy eṣaṃ viviktatām ||
    1. yathāvadadhigacchanti, tadvad gotvādivas tv api |
    2. saṅkīrṇam arthamātraṃ tu budhyante 'bhyāsarvajitāḥ ||
    1. vivekaṃ pratipadyante ye śabdasmṛtisaṃskṛtāḥ |
    2. yathā rūpādimatyarthe yasyaivāsti yadindriyam ||
    1. sa tanmātraṃ gṛhītvānyan na gṛhṇātyanumānataḥ |
    2. tathā vivekahetūnāṃ yadā yaṃ pratipadyate ||
    1. tadupeye tadā jñānaṃ vartate tadanugrahāt |
    2. tena yāvat pramātāṇāṃ vivekopāyadarśanam ||
    1. na syāt tāvad bhavet teṣāṃ vijñānaṃ nirvikalpakam |
    2. tasmād yatra prakalpyeta vastu vastvantarātmanā ||
    1. pramāṇābhāsatā tatra na svadharmavikalpane |
    2. pratyakṣatvam ataḥ siddhaṃ sāmānyasya tathaiva ca ||
    1. sambandhasyeti tat pūrvam anumānādi jāyate |
    2. sarvaṃ cāpy anumānādi pratyakṣe nirvikalpake ||
    1. na pravartata ity etadanumāne 'bhidhāsyate |
    2. nanv evaṃ sati yāpy agner dūrād apy auṣṇyakalpanā ||
    1. sāpi pratyakṣam eva syād yathā gotvādibuddhayaḥ |
    2. pratyāsannataraṃ gotvaṃ pratyakṣatvena sammatam ||
    1. vijñānaṃ nānyad astīti pratyakṣam idam eva naḥ |
    2. tatrāpy akṣair asambandhaṃ manvānasyopajāyate ||
    1. yadā buddhiḥ, tadā naiva pratyakṣatvena kalpyate |
    2. sparśanena tu sambandhe pratyakṣatvena jāyate ||
    1. tasmād yadindriyaṃ yasya grāhakatvena kalpitam |
    2. tenaiva sati sambandhe pratyakṣaṃ nānyathā bhavet ||
    1. evaṃ samāne 'pi vikalpamārge yatrākṣasambandhaphalānusāraḥ |
    2. pratyakṣatā tasya tathā ca loke vināpyado lakṣaṇataḥ prasiddham ||

{5,1 vṛttikāragrantha VKG}

    1. pratyakṣādau niṣiddhe 'pi nanu lokaprasiddhitaḥ |
    2. dharmādharmau pramāsyete brāhmaṇādivivekavat ||
    1. dhārmikādhārmikatvābhyāṃ pīḍānugrahakāriṇau |
    2. prasiddhau hi, tathā cāha pārāśaryo 'tra vastuni ||
    1. idaṃ puṇyam idaṃ pāpam ity etasmin padadvaye |
    2. ācaṇḍālaṃ manuṣyāṇām alpaṃ śāstraprayojanam ||
    1. nirmūlāsambhavād atra pramāṇaiḥ saiva mṛgyate |
    2. kutaḥ punaḥ pravṛtteti, pratyakṣādi tu vāritam ||
    1. na caitāni parityajya pṛthag loke pramāṇatā |
    2. saṃsāramocakādeś ca hiṃsā puṇyatvasammatā ||
    1. na paścāt puṇyam icchanti ke cid evaṃ vigānataḥ |
    2. mlecchāryāṇāṃ prasiddhatvaṃ na dharmasyopapadyate ||
    1. na cāryāṇāṃ viśeṣo 'sti yāvacchāstram anāśritam |
    2. tanmūlārthaprasiddhis tu tatprāmāṇye sthite bhavet ||
    1. tasmād abhāvaktrasthau dharmādarmau na śaknuyāt |
    2. codanā cet samuddhartuṃ grastau tenaiva paśyatām ||
    1. upadeśo hi bhavati jñānaṃ tasyeti yojyate |
    2. jñāyate yena tajjñānam ekādhikaraṇatvataḥ ||
    1. autpattikagirā doṣaḥ kāraṇasya nivāryate |
    2. abādho 'nyatirekeṇa, svatas tena pramāṇatā ||
    1. sarvasyānupalabdhe 'rthe prāmāṇyaṃ smṛtir anyathā |
    2. codanā copadeśaś ca vidhiś caikārthavācinaḥ ||
    1. vākyāntare samarthe 'pi kimarthaṃ vidhir āśritaḥ |
    2. sādhyasādhanasambandhaḥ sarvākhyāteṣu vidyate ||
    1. sarvavākyeṣu cākhyātaṃ tenākāṅkṣānivartanāt |
    2. pravṛttisiddhir icchātaḥ, pratiṣedhāt tu varjanam ||
    1. vidhāvanāśrite sādhyaḥ puruṣārtho na labhyate |
    2. śrutasvargādibādhena dhātvarthaḥ sādhyatāṃ vrajet ||
    1. vidhau tu tam atikramya svargādeḥ sādhyateṣyate |
    2. tatsādhanasya dharmatvam evaṃ sati ca labhyate ||
    1. svapratyayāntarāpekṣā syād anāptanaroktiṣu |
    2. āptoktiṣu narāpekṣā nobhayaṃ codanāsu naḥ ||

{5.2}

    1. ādiśabdo makārāntaḥ, luki kleśena saṅgatiḥ |
    2. nañadhyāhriyate sūtre, saṅkarāt paricodanā ||
    1. pramāṇalakṣaṇājñānād vyabhicārāt parīkṣaṇam |
    2. naitat pratyakṣam ityevamaparīkṣopasaṃhṛtā ||
    1. tatrānyasyāyathārthatvaṃ pratyakṣe tu yathārthatā |
    2. yadābhāsaṃ hi vijñānaṃ tatsaṃyoge tad iṣyate ||
    1. sampūrṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hy etat, tatsator vyatyayaḥ kṛtaḥ |
    2. śobhanārthas tu sacchabdaḥ, yad vākhyāhārakalpanā ||
    1. arthāpattyetareṣāṃ ca pratyakṣābhāsalakṣaṇam |
    2. bādhakajñānalābho hi pūrvābādhe na sambhavet ||
    1. sa cāstīti, avabodhatve sati nānyonyasaṃśrayam |
    2. na cānāgatabādhe ca pūrveṇātmā hi labhyate ||
    1. nimittadoṣabodhena paścād yatrāpy abādhanam |
    2. bhavaty eva hi tatrāpi narāntaraviparyayaḥ ||
    1. sarveṣāṃ sarvadā yatra dhīḥ syāt tatra na bādhanam |
    2. na hi kāraṇaduṣṭatvabuddhis tatra balīyasī ||
    1. jātyādiṣu yadā jātā buddhiḥ paścād asambhavāt |
    2. nāśyate yuktibhis tatra vyaktam anyonyasaṃśrayam ||
    1. svataḥ prāmāṇyataś cātra nirṇayo 'stitvabodhanāt |
    2. tadrūpapratyayotpattes tadasadvādinām api ||

{5,3 nirālambanavāda NAV}

    1. pramāṇatvāpramāṇatve puṇyapāpādi tatphalam |
    2. vidhyarthavādamantrārthanāmadheyādikalpanā ||
    1. sarveṣu lakṣaṇeṣv evaṃ svapramāṇagaṇaiḥ sthitiḥ |
    2. vacanavyaktibhedena pūrvasiddhāntapakṣatā ||
    1. karmabhyaḥ phalasambandhaḥ pāralaukyaihalaukike |
    2. sarvam ityādy ayuktaṃ syād arthaśūnyāsu buddhiṣu ||
    1. tasmād dharmārthibhiḥ pūrvaṃ pramāṇair lokasammataiḥ |
    2. arthasya sadasadbhāve yatnaḥ kāryaḥ kriyāṃ prati ||
    1. yadā saṃvṛtisatyena sarvam etat prakalpyate |
    2. jñānamātre 'pi kasmād vo vṛthāgraho 'rthakalpane ||
    1. saṃvṛter na tu satyatvaṃ satyabhedaḥ kuto 'nvayam |
    2. satyā cet saṃvṛtiḥ keyaṃ mṛṣā cet satyatā katham ||
    1. satyatvaṃ na ca sāmānyaṃ mṛṣārthaparamārthayoḥ |
    2. virodhāt, na hi vṛkṣatvaṃ sāmānyaṃ vṛkṣasiṃhayoḥ ||
    1. tulyārthatve 'pi tenaiṣāṃ mithyāsaṃvṛtiśabdayoḥ |
    2. vañcanārtha upanyāso lālāvaktrāsavādivat ||
    1. nāstikyaparihārārthaṃ saṃvṛtiḥ, kalpaneti ca |
    2. kalpanāpi tv abhinnasya naiva nirvastuke bhavet ||
    1. tasmād yan nāsti nāsty eva, yat tv asti paramārthataḥ |
    2. tat satyam anyanmithyeti, na satyadvayakalpanā ||
    1. svapnādibhogavac cāpi yopabhogatvakalpanā |
    2. tannivṛttyartham eveha paramārthe kaś cit pravartate ||
    1. na hi svapnasukhādyarthaṃ dharme kaś cit pravartate |
    2. yādṛcchikatvāt svapnasya tūṣṇīmāsyeta paṇḍitaiḥ ||
    1. paramārthaphalāvāptim icchadbhis tena yatnataḥ |
    2. pratipattir vidhātavyā yuktibhir bāhyavastuṣu ||
    1. tatrārthaśūnyaṃ vijñānaṃ yogācārāḥ samāśritāḥ |
    2. tasyāpy abhāvam icchanti ye mādhyamikavādinaḥ ||
    1. tatra bāhyārthaśūnyatvaṃ tulyaṃ tāvad dvayor api |
    2. nivṛttyāsya tato jñāne tadvat saṃvṛtikalpanā ||
    1. tasmāt sādhāraṇatvena tanmūlatvena cāpy ayam |
    2. bāhyārthasadasadbhāve yatno bhāṣyakṛtā kṛtāḥ ||
    1. bāhyārthāpahnave 'dvaitam ekārthasya parīkṣaṇāt |
    2. pramāṇam āśritaś caikas tatrāstāṃ yaḥ prameyataḥ ||
    1. pramāṇasthas tu mūlatvād ihedānīṃ parīkṣyate |
    2. prastutaḥ sa dvidhā cātra prathamaṃ tv anumānataḥ ||
    1. pratyakṣabādhane cokte paścāt tacchaktyavekṣaṇāt |
    2. tatrānumānamāhedaṃ nanv iti, asya ca saṅgatiḥ ||
    1. tatsamprayogajaṃ nāma pratyakṣam iti bhāṣitam |
    2. tatrendriyārthasambandhabhedo na paramārthataḥ ||
    1. kalpitaḥ samprayogas tu svapnādāv api vidyate |
    2. tadatadyogajanyasya vibhāgas tena durlabhaḥ ||
    1. mithyātvaṃ yad dvidhaivoktaṃ nāyathety atra cocyate |
    2. sarvasyaiva ca mithyātve kiṃ viśiṣyābhidhīyate ||
