    1. stambhādipratyayo mithyā pratyayatvāt tathā hi yaḥ |
    2. pratyayaḥ sa mṛṣā dṛṣṭaḥ svapnādipratyayo yathā ||
    1. siddhasādhanabhāvo 'ṃśe dṛṣṭāntābhāva eva ca |
    2. mā bhūtām evaśabdaś ca vyartho 'śeṣaprasādhane ||
    1. sarva eveti tenātra jāgradbuddhiparigrahaḥ |
    2. svāṃśābhyupagamāc cāpi bāhyagrāhyanivāraṇam ||
    1. pratyayasyeti sādhyāṃśavyāptahetunidarśanam |
    2. hetuś copanyenātra jāgrato 'pīti darśataḥ ||
    1. vipakṣābhāvataś cātra vyatireko na kathyate |
    2. sāmānyasya ca hetutvāt kasmāt pakṣaikadeśatā ||
    1. jāgrajjñāne viśeṣo 'yaṃ yataḥ supariniścayaḥ |
    2. bāhyālambanasambandho na prasiddhaḥ paraṃ prati ||
    1. tasmād yad bhāṣyakāreṇa dattam uttam atra tu |
    2. vikalpasamatā vā syād vaidharmyasamatāpi vā ||
    1. dṛṣṭatvāt pūrvapakṣasya jātyukti kaiś cid āśritā |
    2. pratijñādoṣam evāhuḥ ke cit pratyakṣabādhanam ||
    1. śakṣyāmo yadi vispaṣṭaṃ svāṃśagrāhyanivāraṇam |
    2. tadā te śuddha eva syāt pakṣo grāhyanivāraṇaḥ ||
    1. pratyakṣādeś ca viṣayo bāhya evāvatiṣṭhate |
    2. tanniṣedhakṛtas tasya tair bhavet pakṣabādhanam ||
    1. suniścayena caiteṣāṃ bādhakapratyayād ṛte |
    2. pramāṇābhāsatā nāstīty etasmāt katyate balam ||
    1. duṣṭajñānagṛhītāpratiṣedho hi yujyate |
    2. gṛhītamātrabādhe tu svapakṣo 'pi na sidhyati ||
    1. agrāhyatvāc ca bhedena viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ |
    2. aprasiddhobhayatvaṃ vā vācyam anyatarasya vā ||
    1. vaktṛśrotroś ca yajjñānaṃ viśeṣaṇviśeṣyayoḥ |
    2. tannirālambanatvena svavāgbādho dvyor api ||
    1. sambhavo na ca bhedasya viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ |
    2. tasmān nirūpaṇaṃ nāsti pratijñārthasya śobhanam ||
    1. nirālambanatā nāma na kiñ cid vastu gamyate |
    2. tena yadvyatirekādau praśno naivopapadyate ||
    1. yady avastu kathaṃ tv asmāṃs tvaṃ bodhayitum icchasi |
    2. budhyase vā svabuddhyā tvam, kalpitā tv atha sādhyate ||
    1. asataḥ kalpanā kīdṛk, kḷptau vastu prasajyate |
    2. katham iṣṭam abhāve ced, vastu so 'pīti vakṣyate ||
    1. tathā pratyaya ity eṣa karma bhāvādi vā bhavet |
    2. bhāvādiṣu virodhaḥ syāt karma cet siddhasādhanam ||
    1. pratyāyyasya hi rūpāder nirālambanateṣyate |
    2. avijñānātmakatvena kiñ cin nālambate hy asau ||
    1. kartṛtve karaṇatve vā pakṣatvaṃ śabdayor api |
    2. tannirālambanatvena pakṣābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||
    1. pratyāyyena ca bhinnena vinā kartrādyasambhavaḥ |
    2. pratyaye tannimitte vā bādhaḥ svavacanena te ||
    1. athāpi rūḍhirūpeṇa pratyayaḥ syāt tathāpi tu |
    2. grāhakaṃ vastu siddhaṃ naḥ pratyayo 'nyasya vastunaḥ ||
    1. tam abhyupetya pakṣaś ced abhyupetaṃ virudhyate |
    2. viśeṣyasyāprasiddhaś ca tava, asmākam atādṛśe ||
    1. ātmadharmasvatantratvakalpane 'pi tathā bhavet |
    2. na ca pratyayamātratvaṃ kiñ cid asty anirūpaṇāt ||
    1. śabdārthamātrarūpeṇa yathānyeṣāṃ nirūpaṇam |
    2. tathā ca bhavato na syād vācyabhedamanicchataḥ ||
    1. nirālambanatā cāpi sarvathā yadi sādhyate |
    2. viśeṣaṇāprasiddhiś ca dṛṣṭāntaś ca na vidyate ||
    1. kena cic cet prakāreṇa nirālambanatocyate |
    2. rasajñānasya rūpādiśūnyatvāt siddhasādhanam ||
    1. atha buddhir yadākārā tadālambanavāraṇam |
    2. svākārasyābhyupetatvāt tadabhāvo virudhyate ||
    1. bāhyānālambanatve 'pi bāhya ity agraho yadi |
    2. stambhādau naiva tadbuddhir ityevaṃ siddhasādhanam ||
    1. atha stambhādirūpeṇa nirālambanatocyate |
    2. saṃvedanasya dṛṣṭatvāt tadvirodhaḥ prasajyate ||
    1. dvicandrādiṣu tulyaś cet, nendriyāprāptito hi naḥ |
    2. tatrānālambanoktiḥ syān nārthasaṃvittyabhāvataḥ ||
    1. sarvatrārthendriyāṇāṃ naḥ saṃyogasadasattayā |
    2. saṃvittau vidyamānāyāṃ sadasadgrāhikā sthitiḥ ||
    1. bhavatas tv indriyādīnām abhāvād grahaṇād ṛte |
    2. nālambanasya hetuḥ syān niṣedho 'to na yujyate ||
    1. bahirbhāvāprasiddhatvāt tenānālambanā matiḥ |
    2. kathañ cit sādhyate naiṣa pakṣo hi jñāyate tadā ||
    1. yathānyabodhanāśakter nāprasiddhe viśeṣaṇe |
    2. pakṣasiddhis tathaiva syād viśeṣaṇaviśeṣaṇe ||
    1. nāprasiddhe padārthe hi vākyārthaḥ sampratīyate |
    2. tatpūrvakatvāt pakṣaś ca vākyārthaḥ sthāpayiṣyate ||
    1. paryudāse niṣedhe vā vyatiriktasya vastunaḥ |
    2. prameyatvādyabhedena jagataḥ siddhasādhanam ||
    1. yadi cātyantabhedena nirālambanatocyate |
    2. kathañ cic ced virudhyeta prākpakṣaḥ kalpitena ||
    1. vastvādyākārataś cāpi dhīr nirālambaneṣyate |
    2. grāhakāc ced abhinnatvaṃ śaktibhedo virudhyate ||
    1. nirālambanabuddheś ca yady utpattiḥ prasādhyate |
    2. dṛṣṭatvāt seṣyate 'smābhir bāhyagrāhyavivarjitā ||
    1. samyaktvaṃ punar etasyās tvaṃ necchasi kathañ cana |
    2. ātmāṃśe 'vasitā hy eṣā mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhivat ||
    1. caitrādipratyayānāṃ ca nirālambanatā yadi |
    2. dharmabhūtā na gṛhyeta sādhanotthitayā dhiyā ||
    1. tato viṣayanānātvāt pratiyogyanirākṛtā |
    2. rūpāt sālambanaprāptiḥ satī kena nivāryate ||
    1. yadi pratyayaśabdo 'pi pratyayatvena gṛhyate |
    2. saṃvittyālambanatvaṃ ca vāryate, siddhasādhanam ||
    1. buddhyutpādanaśaktiś ced vāryā, sādhayaṃ na sidhyati |
    2. sādhanasya prayogo 'tra bodhakatvād vinā na te ||
    1. na cābhidhāstyasambandhād ṛte bhedāc ca nāsty asau |
    2. na cāsau tadgataṃ bhedaṃ bodhayantya dhiyā vinā ||
    1. prāśnikair agṛhīte ca vākyasyāvayave pṛthak |
    2. pakṣe hetau ca dṛṣṭānte vādini prativādini ||
    1. sādhanasyāprayogaḥ syād abhyupetyocyate yadi |
    2. pūrvābhyupagamenaiva pratijñā bādhyate tataḥ ||
    1. dharmādharmādibhede ca nāsiddhe paramārthataḥ |
    2. śiṣyātmanoś ca dharmāder upadeśo 'vakalpate ||
    1. tadanuṣṭhānato buddher iṣṭo bhedaḥ, sphuṭaṃ ca taiḥ |
    2. sūtrāntare 'bhyupetatvād bhaved āgamabādhanam ||
    1. sarvalokaprasiddhyā ca pakṣabādho 'tra te dhruvam |
    2. kṛtsnasādhanabuddhiś ca yadi mithyeṣyate tataḥ ||
    1. sarvābhāvo yatheṣṭaṃ vā nyūnatā vābhidhīyate |
    2. teṣāṃ sālambanatve vā tair anaikāntiko bhavet ||
    1. tadanyasya pratijñā cet, tadanyapratyayo mṛṣā |
    2. tanmithyātvaprasaṅge ca sarvaṃ pūrva na sidhyati ||
    1. stambhādisādhanajñānabhedo na hi tathā bhavet |
    2. yāvad yāvat pratijñeyaṃ tadaṅgasya pratīyate ||
    1. tāvat tāvat pareṣāṃ syān mithyātvād anyabādhanam |
    2. viruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ bādho vāpy anumānataḥ ||
    1. itthaṃ sarveṣu pakṣeṣu vaktavyaṃ pratisādhanam |
    2. bāhyārthālambanā buddhir iti samyak ca dhīr iyam ||
    1. bādhakāpetabuddhitvād yathā svapnādibādhadhīḥ |
    2. sāpi mithyeti ced brūyāt, svapnādīnām abādhanāt ||
    1. tasmāt sādharmyadṛṣṭānto bhavataḥ sādhane na hi |
    2. vijñānāstitvabhinnatvakṣaṇikatvādidhīs tathā ||
    1. samyak ced abhyupeyeta tadānaikāntiko bhavet |
    2. tanmithyābhyupapattau ca pakṣabādhaḥ prasajyate ||
    1. tathā ca baddham uktādivyavasthā na prakalpate |
    2. tataś ca mokṣayatnasya vaiphalyaṃ vaḥ prasajyate ||
    1. vikalpotpadyamānā ca jñānāstitvādidhīr yadi |
    2. mṛṣeṣṭā, na ca dṛṣṭātra pramāṇāntarato gatiḥ ||
    1. pramāṇābhāvatas tena jñānāstitvādi durlabham |
    2. sarvaṃ cāpy asmadādīnāṃ mithyā jñānaṃ vikalpanāt ||
    1. sānnidhyaviprakṛṣṭatve sattvāsattve ca durlabhe |
    2. mithyājñānāviśeṣe 'pi sāṃkhyādiparivarjanāt ||
    1. bauddhadarśana ekasmin pakṣapāto na yujyate |
    2. mṛṣātvaṃ yadi buddheḥ syād bādhaḥ kiṃ nopalabhyate ||
    1. bādhād vināpi tac cet syād vyavasthā na prakalpate |
    2. pratiyogini dṛṣṭe ca jāgrajjñāne mṛṣā bhavet ||
    1. svapnādibuddhir asmākaṃ tava bhedo 'pi kiṅkṛtaḥ |
    2. na cānyat pratiyogyasti jāgrajjñānasya śobhanam ||
    1. yaddarśanena mithyātvaṃ stambhādipratyayo vrajet |
    2. svapnādipratiyogitvaṃ sarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ ||
    1. tadīyadharmavaidharmyād bādhakapratyayo yathā |
    2. yogināṃ jāyate buddhir bādhikā pratiyoginī ||
    1. jāgratstambhādibuddhīnāṃ tataḥ svapnāditulyatā |
    2. prāptānāṃ tām avasthāṃ ca sarvaprāṇabhṛtām api ||
    1. bādho 'yaṃ bhavitā tena siddhā sapratiyogitā |
    2. iha janmani keṣāñ cin na tāvad upalabhyate ||
    1. yogyavasthāgatānāṃ tu na vidmaḥ kiṃ bhaviṣyati |
    2. yogināṃ cāsmādīyānāṃ tvaduktapratiyoginī ||
    1. tvaduktiviparītā vā bādhabuddhir bhaviṣyati |
    2. īdṛktve yogibuddhīnāṃ dṛṣṭānto na tavāsti ca ||
    1. dṛṣṭāntas tv asmādīnāṃ yo gṛhītaḥ sa vidyate |
    2. atha stambhādibuddhīnāṃ vadet sapratiyogitām ||
    1. bādhyatvaṃ cāpi buddhitvān mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhivat |
    2. iṣṭaṃ sapratiyogitvaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhibhiḥ ||
    1. tadātmanā ca bādhyatvaṃ grāhyāntaratayāpi ca |
    2. bādhakaiś cāpy anekāntaḥ, tadanyatve ca pūrvavat ||
    1. mithyādhīpratiyogitvaṃ svapnādāv iva te bhavet |
    2. rāgādikṣayayogitvanimittādhigatis tathā ||
    1. yāvān viśeṣa iṣṭaś cet sarvābhāvād viruddhatā |
    2. mahājanasya vā bādhādivānīmbādhabuddhivat ||
    1. vācyo 'numānabādho vā yadi vā pratisādhanam |
    2. pūrvasādhanadoṣāś ca sandheyāḥ, tasya cādhunā ||
    1. sādhyābhedād avācyatvād hetor nobhayasiddhatā |
    2. pratyayatvaṃ ca, sāmānyaṃ bhinnābhinnaṃ na vidyate ||
    1. bhavato 'tyantabhinnaṃ ca matpakṣe 'pi kathañ cana |
    2. sārūpyānyanivṛttī ca netyetat sādhayiṣyate ||
    1. tasmād dhetur na sāmānyam asti siddhaṃ dvayor api |
    2. viśeṣayoś ca hetutvaṃ pakṣatattulyasaṃsthayoḥ ||
    1. na syād anvayahīnatvād ataddharmatayāpi ca |
    2. na cārthahīnā tadbuddhir hetutvena bhaviṣyati ||
    1. āśrayāsiddhitā coktā viśeṣyasyāprasiddhitaḥ |
    2. tathā hetor viruddhatvaṃ dṛṣṭānte sādhyahīnatā ||
    1. viśeṣaṇāprasiddhatvavikalpenaiva bodhite |
    2. svapnādipratyaye bāhyaṃ sarvathā na hi neṣyate ||
    1. sarvatrālambanaṃ bāhyaṃ deśakālānyathātmakam |
    2. janmany ekatra bhinne vā tathā kālāntare 'pi vā ||
    1. taddeśo vānyadeśo vā svapnajñānasya gocaraḥ |
    2. alātacakre 'lātaṃ syāc chīghrabhramaṇasaṃskṛtam ||
    1. gandharvanagare 'bhrāṇi pūrvadṛṣṭaṃ gṛhādi ca |
    2. pūrvānubhūtatoyaṃ ca raśmitaptoṣaraṃ tathā ||
    1. mṛgatoyasya vijñāne kāraṇatvena kalpyate |
    2. dravyāntare viṣāṇaṃ ca śaśasyātmā ca kāraṇam ||
    1. śaśaśṛṅgadhiyaḥ, mauṇḍyaṃ niṣedhe śiraso 'sya ca |
    2. vastvantarair asaṃsṛṣṭaḥ padārthaḥ śūnyatādhiyaḥ ||
    1. kāraṇatvaṃ padārthānām asadvākyārthakalpane |
    2. atyantānanubhūto 'pi baddhyā yo 'rthaḥ prakalpyate ||
    1. tasyotpattau kathañ cit syuḥ pṛthivyādīni kāraṇam |
    2. eṣa pratyakṣadharmaś ca vartamānārthataiva yā ||
    1. sannikṛṣṭārthavṛttiś ca na tu jñānāntareṣv iyam |
    2. katham utpādayej jñānaṃ tatrāsaṃścet, kuto nviyam ||
    1. arthasyāvidyamānasya vijñānotpattyaśaktatā |
    2. bāhyālambanatāyāṃ nau vivādo 'rthasya saṃnidhiḥ ||
    1. yadi nāsti, kim evaṃ syād asmatpakṣanivartanam |
    2. tasmād yadanyathāsantam anyathā pratipadyate ||
    1. tannirālambanaṃ jñānam, abhāvālambanaṃ ca tat |
    2. bhāvāntaram abhāvo 'nyo na kaś cid anirūpaṇāt ||
    1. bhavatā dvayamatyetad durnirūpaṃ sahetukam |
    2. pratijñādoṣavac cāpi yojyā hetor viruddhatā ||
    1. samastavyastadharmādisvarūpādiviparyayāt |
    2. dṛṣṭāntadoṣāḥ sarve ca yojyāḥ, na hy ekavastuni ||
    1. tava sādhyāṃśahetvaṃśavyāptadharmādisambhavaḥ |
    2. ke cid vaidharmyadṛṣṭānto nāstīty apy anuyuñjate ||
    1. tadabhāvād avṛtteś ca nāsty atrāvasaras tava |
    2. vidhirūpapratijñāyām etad vaktuṃ hi śakyate ||
    1. tatrāvastuvipakṣe 'pi prayogasya hi sambhavaḥ |
    2. yasminn anityatā nāsti kāryatāpi na vidyate ||
    1. tasmin, yathā khapuṣpādāv iti śakyaṃ hi bhāṣitum |
    2. atra tv avastusādhyatvaṃ vastunaś ca vipakṣatā ||
    1. tena syād vyatireko 'sya vācyaḥ, yaś cāpi darśayet |
    2. pratiṣedhadvayāt tena vidhir eva pradarśitaḥ ||
    1. na ca śakyo vidhir vaktuṃ vastuny asati kena cit |
    2. evaṃ sthite ca sarvajñaniṣedhādāv iyaṃ gatiḥ ||
    1. pratyakṣāder asāmarthyaṃ tadīyasyāsmadādivat |
    2. vaidharmyāsambhave 'py etadanye tv āhur adūṣaṇam ||
    1. vinaiva tatprayogeṇa hetur aikāntiko yataḥ |
    2. sarvathā sadupāyānāṃ vādamārgaḥ pravartate ||
    1. adhikāro 'nupāyatvān na vāde śūnyavādinaḥ |
    2. nanu sarvaṃ bhavatsiddhaṃ mayedaṃ sādhanaṃ kṛtam ||
    1. kimarthaṃ tadasiddhyā tvaṃ vikalpyātrātthadūṣaṇam |
    2. vipralipsur ivāhaivaṃ kimarthaṃ nyāyavid bhavān ||
    1. nāśrauṣīḥ sādhanatvaṃ kiṃ prasiddhasya dvayor api |
    2. yo 'pi tāvat parāsiddhaḥ svayaṃ siddho 'bhidhīyate ||
    1. bhavet tatra pratīkāraḥ svato 'siddhe tu kā kriyā |
    2. taṃ sādhayan virundhyād dhi pūrvābhyupagataṃ naraḥ ||
    1. asādhite tu sādhyo 'rtho na tena pratipadyate |
    2. parāsiddho na paryāptaḥ pareṣāṃ pratipattaye ||
    1. tenāsādhanatā yuktā, svato 'siddhe tu kiṅkṛtā |
    2. dvayoḥ siddhasya hetutvaṃ nādṛṣṭāyopadiśyate ||
    1. pratyeṣyanti svasiddhena sādhanena svayaṃ yataḥ |
    2. vadet katham asiddhaṃ cet, ityanenāpi kiṃ tava ||
    1. gṛhītam agṛhītaṃ vā sādhyaṃ vā sādhanāpi vā |
    2. mayocyate cet tv asiddhaṃ kiṃ tvaṃ na pratipadyase ||
    1. yatra syāt puruṣādhīnā buddhis tatredam ucyate |
    2. kuto 'sya pūrvavijñānam ityatretanna yujyate ||
    1. yadi caivaṃ bhaved atra pratijñāmātra eva hi |
    2. maddoṣājñānamātreṇa pratipattir bhavet tava ||
    1. yatas tu sādhanāpekṣā tenāsyaiva pramāṇatā |
    2. tatsmṛtyutpattimātre tu vākyavyāpāra iṣyate ||
    1. tasmād yathaiva sādhyāṃśavyāptahetunidarśanāt |
    2. sādhyaṃ gṛhṇan na vaktāram apekṣeta tathā bhavān ||
    1. yac cāpi bhavato jñānaṃ pratyakādiḥ kim atra te |
    2. matprasiddhāsti yuktir vā sādhyaṃ vātra yathecchasi ||
    1. tasmān na viduṣām etaduttaṃ yujyate yataḥ |
    2. tava hetur asiddho 'yaṃ mama tena na sādhanam ||
    1. satyaṃ yadi mamaivātra pratipattiḥ phalaṃ bhavet |
    2. tadā tvadaprasiddhe 'pi hetau māṃ prati hetutā ||
    1. yadā tu jñānamātratvapratipattau bhavān mayā |
    2. pṛṣṭaḥ ko hetur atreti tadaivaṃ nopapadyate ||
    1. svayaṃ na hy agṛhītena matprasiddhena vā bhavān |
    2. hetunā sādhyam etat tu pratipannaḥ kathañ cana ||
    1. na ca vyāpriyate 'nyatra vacanaṃ prāśnikān prati |
    2. svaniścayāya yo hetus tasyaiva pratipādanāt ||
    1. matprasiddhatvam etasya kutaś cāvagataṃ tvayā |
    2. kathaṃ cetthaṃ vivakṣā te svayam artham ajānataḥ ||
    1. mayi jijñāsamāne 'pi buddhipūrvābhidhāyinaḥ |
    2. iti jñātvā ca vo vṛddhair bhāṣitobhayasiddhatā ||
    1. tena yadvanmamaitena tvamadhitsasi hetunā |
    2. sādhyajñānam, tathaivāham ajñānaṃ tava dūṣaṇaiḥ ||
    1. yathaiva ca bhavānīdṛk sādhyam uktvāsya sādhanam |
    2. sādhyānurūpam ajñātvā vihataḥ pratipādanāt ||
    1. tathaiva pratipādyo 'pi tādṛksādhyabubhutsayā |
    2. manvānaḥ sādhanaṃ duṣṭaṃ tataḥ sādhyaṃ na budhyate ||
    1. saṃvittyā sādhanaṃ matvā tatsadbhāve dṛḍhe sthite |
    2. sādhyasyāsambhavād eva tvaduktaṃ nāvabudhyate ||
    1. tenāśeyaṃ na kartavyā mohād api mayerite |
    2. sādhane sādhanaṃ jñātvā para evāvabhotsyate ||
    1. vispaṣṭaś cākṣapādokto virodho hetusādhyayoḥ |
    2. yamadṛṣṭvā parair uktam adūṣaṇam idaṃ kila ||
    1. nanu lokaprasiddhena pūrvam etena hetunā |
    2. sādhyasiddhir mamāpy āsīt paramārtho 'sya nāstitā ||
    1. yo 'dhunā paramārthena nāstītyevaṃ prakāśate |
    2. kathaṃ pūrvam asāv āsīd asaṃścet sādhanaṃ katham ||
    1. sādhanaṃ ced avaśyaṃ ca paramārthāstitā bhavet |
    2. siddhir nāparamārthena paramārthasya yujyate ||
    1. na dṛṣṭā śaśaśṛṅgādeḥ samyagjñānādihetutā |
    2. bāṣpādināpy adhūmena mithyā vahnyādibodhanam ||
    1. tasmād asatyahetor yā paramārthe matis tava |
    2. sāpy asatyā na satyaṃ hi satyābhāsena gamyate ||
    1. ye 'pi rekhādayo dṛṣṭā varṇānāṃ pratipādakāḥ |
    2. na te svenāpi rūpeṇa paramārthatvavarjitāḥ ||
    1. varṇātmanā na satyāś cet, sarvabhāveṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ |
    2. padārthāntararūpeṇa na satyaṃ kiñ cid iṣyate ||
    1. svarūpe vidyamāne tu yad apy evaṃ prakāśate |
    2. svarūpābhāvakḷptau tu na satyaṃ nāpy asatyatā ||
    1. hetvādīnāṃ tu bhavataḥ svarūpeṇāpy asatyatā |
    2. tena bāṣpādivat teṣām upāyatvam, na lekhyavat ||
    1. upāyānāṃ svarūpaṃ hi saṃvṛttyātmakam eva naḥ |
    2. tathā ca satyateṣṭaiva svarūpāsatyatā katham ||
    1. saṃvṛtyā yat svarūpaṃ hi tadvāṅmātranibandhanam |
    2. hetutvaṃ paramārthasya pratipattuṃ na śaknuyāt ||
    1. paramāthāc ca lokasya na bhede hetur asti te |
    2. laukikopāyagamyasya kena syāt paramārthatā ||
    1. nanv asty api bāhye 'rthe buddhyārūḍhe na sidhyati |
    2. vāsanāśabdabhedotthavikalpapravibhāgataḥ ||
    1. nyāyavidbhir idaṃ coktaṃ dharmādau buddhim āśrite |
    2. vyavahāro 'numānādeḥ kalpyate na bahiḥsthite ||
    1. astīdaṃ vacanaṃ teṣām idaṃ tatra parīkṣyatām |
    2. bhedo 'sataḥ kathaṃ hi syād buddhiśabdayoḥ ||
    1. nirvastuke kathañ cin nu prasavo buddhiśabdayoḥ |
    2. śabdabhedo 'pi bhavatas tadabhāvān na sidhyati ||
    1. yadi vā vidyamāno 'pi bhedo buddhiprakalpitaḥ |
    2. sādhyasādhanadharmāder vyavahārāya kalpyate ||
    1. tato bhavatprayukte 'smin sādhane yāvad ucyate |
    2. sarvatrotpadyate buddhir iti dūṣaṇatā bhavet ||
    1. yaś ca mantras tv ayokto 'yaṃ dharmyādau buddhim āśrite |
    2. na bāhyāpekṣayā sa syād asiddhyādau mayerite ||
    1. buddhiprakḷptisidhiś ca bhavatāṃ vyavahāriṇam |
    2. maduktaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ siddhaṃ tvaduktaṃ tu na sādhanam ||
    1. bāhyārthavyavahāritvāj jñānotpāde sthite 'pi naḥ |
    2. kathañ cin na hi kalpyeta vyavahāro 'rthavarjitaḥ ||
    1. nanu yadvanmayā hetur neṣyate dūṣaṇaṃ tathā |
    2. tena me dūṣaṇābhāvād aduṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ bhavet ||
    1. nedānīṃ dūṣaṇaiḥ kāryam, sādhanābhāvato yadi |
    2. tvayaivāsmadabhipretā svapakṣāsiddhir āśritā ||
    1. na cāsti vāsanābhedo nimittāsambhavāt tava |
    2. jñānabhedo nimittaṃ cet, tasya bhedaḥ kathaṃ punaḥ ||
    1. vāsanābhedataś cet syāt, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam |
    2. svacchasya jñānarūpasya na hi bhedaḥ svato 'sti te ||
    1. pramāṇaṃ vāsanāstitve bhede vāpi na vidyate |
    2. kuryād grāhakabhedaṃ sā grāhyabhedas tu kiṅkutaḥ ||
    1. saṃvittyā jāyamānā hi smṛtimātraṃ karoty asau |
    2. kṣaṇikeṣu ca cit teṣu vināśe ca niranvaye ||
    1. vāsyavāsakayoś caivam asāhityān na vāsanā |
    2. pūrvakṣaṇair anutpanno vāsyate nottaraḥ kṣaṇaḥ ||
    1. uttareṇa vinaṣṭatvān na ca pūrvasya vāsanā |
    2. sāhitye 'pi tayor naiva sambandho 'stīty avāsanā ||
    1. kṣaṇikatvād dvyasyāpi vyāpāro na parasparam |
    2. vinaśyac ca kathaṃ vastu vāsyate 'nyena naśyatā ||
    1. avasthitā hi vāsyante bhāvābhāvair avasthitaiḥ |
    2. avasthito hi pūrvasmād bhidyate nottaro yadi ||
    1. pūrvavad vāsanā tatra na syād evāviśeṣataḥ |
    2. bhaṅgure pūrvasādṛśyād bhinnatvāc cāsti vāsanā ||
    1. naitad asty anurūpaṃ tu kṣaṇikatve dhiyāṃ tava |
    2. pūrvajñānaṃ tv anutpannaṃ kāryaṃ nārabhate kvacit ||
    1. na vinaṣṭaṃ, na tasyāsti niṣpannasya kṣaṇaṃ sthitiḥ |
    2. tenotpannavinaṣṭatvān nāsty ārambhakṣaṇo 'pi hi ||
    1. niranvayavinaṣṭatvād ānurūpyaṃ kutaḥ punaḥ |
    2. na tadīyosti kaś cic ca dharma uttarabuddhiṣu ||
    1. samānadharmatāṃ muktvā nānurūpyaṃ ca vidyate |
    2. yadi syād ānurūpyāc ca vāsanā godhiyo yadā ||
    1. hastibuddhir bhavet tatra vailakṣaṇyān na vāsanā |
    2. tataḥ paraṃ ca gojñānaṃ nirmūlatvān na sambhavet ||
    1. sarvaṃ vilakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ na syād eva vilakṣaṇāt |
    2. bāhyārthānugrahābhāvāt pārārthyenāvaśīkṛtāḥ ||
    1. niranvayavināśinyaḥ kuryuḥ kāryaṃ kathaṃ kramāt |
    2. vināśe kāraṇasyeṣṭaḥ kāryārambhaś ca nānyathā ||
    1. tataiva jñānanāśena vinaṣṭāḥ sarvavāsanāḥ |
    2. tena sarvābhya etābhyaḥ sarvākāraṃ yadutthitam ||
    1. jñānam ekakṣaṇenaiva vināśaṃ gantum arhati |
    2. yady āśrayavināśe 'pi śaktyanāśo 'bhyupeyate ||
    1. kṣaṇikatvaṃ ca hīyeta na cārambho 'nyathā bhavet |
    2. vāsanānāṃ pravāho 'pi yadi jñānapravāhavat ||
    1. vāsanātas tato jñānaṃ na syāt tasmāc ca vāsanā |
    2. kuryātāṃ tulyam evaite nānyonyaṃ tu kadā cana ||
    1. nānyo vilakṣaṇo hetur yenānyādṛk phalaṃ bhavet |
    2. tasmāt saṃvṛtisatyaiṣā kalpitā nāsti tattvataḥ ||
    1. na cedṛśena bhavena kāryam utpadyate kva cit |
    2. yasya tv avasthito jñātā jñānābhyāsena yujyate ||
    1. sa tasya vāsanādhāro vāsanāpi sa eva vā |
    2. kusume bījapūrāder yallākṣādyupasicyate |
    3. tadrūpasyaiva saṃkrāntiḥ phale tasya, ity avāsanā ||
    1. yuktyānupetām asatīṃ prakalpya yadvāsanām arthanirākriyeyam ||
    2. āsthānivṛttyarthamavādi bauddhair grāhaṃ gatās tatra kathañ cid anye ||

{5,4 śunyavāda SNV}

    1. evam ukte 'numānasya jñānam āśritya dūṣaṇe |
    2. jñānapravṛttyaśaktyā tu paraḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate ||
    1. yat tāvanmanyamānena pratyakṣaṃ bhavatocyate |
    2. dūṣaṇaṃ tadvirodhādi tadidānīṃ parīkṣyatām ||
    1. pravartituṃ hi kiṃ śaktaṃ stambhādyarthe bahiḥ sthite |
    2. atha vātmāṃśa evaitat grāhye kṣīṇaṃ na vastuni ||
    1. tad yady etena bāhyo 'rtho gṛhyate dūṣaṇaṃ tataḥ |
    2. tvaduktaṃ sarvam ātmāṃśe grāhye tannopapadyate ||
    1. tatra tāvad idaṃ siddhaṃ sarvaprāṇabhṛtām api |
    2. grāhyataṃ nīlapītādidīrghādyākāravastunaḥ ||
    1. na cāpy ākārabhedena jñānajñeyāvadhāraṇā |
    2. na cānyataradharmatvaṃ vispaṣṭaṃ tatra gṛhyate ||
    1. gṛhyamāṇasya cāstitvaṃ nāgrāhyasyāpramāṇakam |
    2. tasmād ākāravad vastu grāhyatvād vidyate dhruvam ||
    1. ataḥ parīkṣamāṇānāṃ jñānam ākāravad yadi |
    2. tanmātre ca pramā kṣīṇā tato nāsty arthakalpanā ||
    1. yadi vākāravattā syād bāhyasyaiveha vastunaḥ |
    2. tad asti gṛhyamāṇatvāt tatsiddhaivāsti dhīr api ||
    1. kiṃ tāvad atra yuktaṃ syāj jñānam ākāravat, kutaḥ |
    2. ekam ākāravad vastu grāhyam ity adhyagīṣmahi ||
    1. tad yady ākāravānartho bāhyaḥ kalpyate tasya ca |
    2. grāhyatvam anyathā na syād iti grāhakakalpanā ||
    1. tenākāravataḥ kḷptād grāhyād ākāravarjitam |
    2. vastvantaraṃ prakalpyaṃ syād grāhakaṃ niṣpramāṇakam ||
    1. tasyākalpanam icchaṃś ced arthe grāhakatāṃ vadeḥ |
    2. saṃjñāmātre visaṃvadaḥ sidddhā tv ekārthakalpanā ||
    1. grāhyagrāhakayor aikyaṃ sarvathā pratipādyate |
    2. bāhyābhyantararūpaś ca parikalpyo mṛṣeṣyate ||
    1. matpakṣe yady api svaccho jñānātmā paramārthataḥ |
    2. tathāpy anādau saṃsāre pūrvajñānaprasūtibhiḥ ||
    1. citrābhiś citrahetutvād vāsanābhir upaplavāt |
    2. svānurūpyeṇa nīlādi grāhyagrāhakarūṣitam ||
    1. pravibhaktam ivotpannaṃ nānyam artham apekṣate |
    2. anyonyahetutā caiva jñānaśaktyor anādikā ||
    1. anekakalpanāyāś ca jyāyasī hy ekakalpanā |
    2. śaktimātrasya bhedaś ca vastubhedād viśiṣyate ||
    1. tasmād ubhayasiddhatvāj jñānasyākārakalpanā |
    2. jyāyasī, bhavatas tv arthaṃ kalpayitvā bhaved iyam ||
    1. tadasiddhāvaśaktatvāt, tenaivaṃ viprakṛṣṭatā |
    2. pratyāsannaṃ ca, sambaddhaṃ grāhyaṃ mama bhaviṣyati ||
    1. itaś cākāravajjñānam, yasmāt tadvat prakāśakam |
    2. svayamprakāśahīnasya bāhyasyopāsanaṃ matam ||
    1. na cāgrhīte jñānākhye prakāśyo 'rtho 'vadhāryate |
    2. tadadhīnaprakāśatvād dīpābhāse yathā ghaṭaḥ ||
    1. utpanneṣv api cārtheṣu prakāśābhāvataḥ kva cit |
    2. pratibandhakayogād vā saṃvittir nopajāyate ||
    1. jñānasyotpadyamānasya pratibandho na kaś cana |
    2. na cāprakāśarūpatvaṃ yenāsyāgrahaṇaṃ bhavet ||
    1. prāk cārthagrahaṇādiṣṭā tasyotpattis tadaiva ca |
    2. saṃvedanaṃ bhaved asya, na cet kālāntare 'pi na ||
    1. kiṃ hi tasya bhaved ūrdhvaṃ prāk ca nāsīn na yena tat |
    2. pūrvaṃ gṛhītaṃ paścāt ca gṛhītam iti bhāṣyate ||
    1. jñānāntarasya cotpattiṃ prakāśo na pratīkṣate |
    2. tasya tasyāpi cānyena saṃvittāvasthitir bhavet ||
    1. jñānapṛṣṭena yo 'py ūrdhvam arthābhāve 'pi |
    2. parāmarśo 'rthorūpasya sa kathaṃ vopapadyate ||
    1. tadrūpamārthamālikhya yadi dhīrnopajāyate |
    2. bhūtakāle ca yadyarthas tatpūrvaṃ nopalakṣitaḥ ||
    1. vaktāraś cāpi dṛśyante varttamānārthabuddhiṣu |
    2. nīlo 'rtho 'yaṃ yato me 'tra tadrūpā jāyate matiḥ ||
    1. tasmāt pūrvagṛhītāsu buddhiṣv arthopalmbhanam |
    2. na copalabdhir astīhi nirākārāsu buddhiṣu ||
    1. vivekabuddhyabhāvāc ca, sākārasya ca darśanāt |
    2. ākāravattayā bodho jñānasyaiva prasajyate ||
    1. na hy evaṃ kalpanā śakyā nirākārād ito matiḥ |
    2. gṛhyate 'rthas tataḥ paścāt sākāraḥ sampratīyate ||
    1. ākāravattvabhedo hi jñātvā śakyeta bhāṣitum |
    2. prāgbuddhigrahaṇād arthe saṃvittir neti sādhitam ||
    1. na cārthākāra evāyaṃ jñānārūḍhaḥ pratīyate |
    2. na hi so 'ntaḥpraveśāya paryāpto nārthahānaye ||
    1. itthambhāve pramāṇaṃ ca tasya vaktuṃ na śakyate |
    2. tadīyapratibimbatvam etasmād eva neṣyate ||
    1. niścandre bimbarūpaṃ hi dṛṣṭaṃ yena divā jalam |
    2. sa rātrau khe ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā jānāti pratibimbatām ||
    1. vijñāne na kadā cit tu prāṅ nirākāradarśanam |
    2. bāhye vākāravattādhīr yenaivaṃ kalpanā bhavet ||
    1. śabdagandharasānāṃ ca kīdṛśī pratibimbatā |
    2. jñāne ca gṛhyamāṇasya kathaṃ syād arthadharmatā ||
    1. bāhyābhyantaradeśatvān na cārthajñānayor mithaḥ |
    2. samparko 'sti yato mohādavivekamatir bhavet ||
    1. asammūḍhasya cādṛṣṭe na sammohaprakalpanā |
    2. kalpyamāne 'tha vāpy evaṃ tad dvayor avatiṣṭhate ||
    1. saṃsargadhama ākāras tasmād eva na yujyate |
    2. deśabhedād asaṃsargaḥ, mūrāmūrtatayā tathā ||
    1. tailokyena prasaṅgāc ca saṃsargo naikakālatā |
    2. na cāpy ārjavataḥ sthānaṃ jñāne nārthasya vidyate ||
    1. sarvathā kalpanāyāṃ ca cakṣuṣāpi rasādayaḥ |
    2. gṛhyeran sarvabhāvānāmaṇvākārāś ca tadgatāḥ ||
    1. na cāpi viṣayatvena sthāne saṃsargakalpanā |
    2. viṣayatvaṃ hi kīdṛk syāt prāgākāropalambhanāt ||
    1. na hy asañcetito bhāvo viṣayatvena kalpyate |
    2. viṣayatvāt tadākāra ākārād viṣayaś ca saḥ ||
    1. dvayor ākāranirmuktaṃ sattvaṃ saṃsṛṣṭatā tathā |
    2. svarūpataḥ paricchidya vaktum ityādi yujyate ||
    1. na cāpy asyeha sadbhāvaḥ prāg gṛhīto na copari |
    2. na hy ākāravinirmuktaṃ grāhyam astīti bhāṣitam ||
    1. tasmād arthena saṃsargo niṣpramāṇaka eva te |
    2. jñānavaicitryasiddhyarthaṃ na cāstyarthasya kalpanā ||
    1. tadadhīnaṃ hi vaicitryaṃ kva dṛṣṭaṃ yena kalpyate |
    2. nirākāreṇa cotpattir vaicitryākārayoḥ katham ||
    1. nirākārāc ca viṣayād buddhyākāro 'tivismayaḥ |
    2. smṛtisvapnādibodhe ca syād anākāratā tava ||
    1. na hi tatrārthasaṃsargaḥ kevalā vāsanaiva tu |
    2. hetutvenopapanneti saiva jāgraddhiyām api ||
    1. anvayavyatirekābhyām evaṃ jñānasya gamyate |
    2. na hi bāhyasya jñānāpeto nidarśyate ||
    1. bāhyāpeto mayā yadvat, tasmāt saṃsargavāgiyam |
    2. nirākāre 'pi vijñāne vāsanāsv eva yujyate ||
    1. dvayor apy eka ākāra ityetasyāpramāṇatā |
    2. deśabhedād asaṃsargaḥ, dvayoś cānavadhāraṇāt ||
    1. evam evārthabuddhyoḥ syāt sādṛśyān nāvibhaktatā |
    2. bhede jñāte hi sādṛśyaṃ nājñāte syāt khapuṣpavat ||
    1. tathā dvicandramāyādāv anyathārthe vyavasthite |
    2. yā syād ākārasaṃvittir nāsāv arthanibandhanā ||
    1. nakṣatraṃ tārakā tiṣyo dārā ityevamādiṣu |
    2. naikatrārthe viruddhatvāl liṅgānekatvasambhavaḥ ||
    1. parivrāṭkāmukaśunāṃ kuṇapādimatis tathā |
    2. dīrghahrasvatvabuddhiś ca hy ekasminn apy apekṣayā ||
    1. ghaṭatvāt pārthavadravyaprameyādimatis tathā |
    2. yugapadgrāhakāṇāṃ ca na syād aikātmyavattayā ||
    1. nārthe hy ekatra yugapad viruddhākārasambhavaḥ |
    2. pratyayānāṃ tu bhinnatvād bhavec chaktyanusārataḥ ||
    1. nirapekṣaṃ svarūpeṇa tasmāj jñānaṃ yadākṛti |
    2. tathārtho na yathārthaṃ tu jñānam utpadyate kva cit ||
    1. itthaṃ vijñānatantratve ko nv arthaṃ kalpayiṣyati |
    2. dhīranāropitākārā svātmany evopayokṣyate ||
    1. naitad asti, tvayaikaṃ hi grāhyaṃ grāhakam iṣyate |
    2. na caikasyaivam ātmatve dṛṣṭāntaḥ kaścid asti te ||
    1. agnyādayo ghaṭādīnāṃ prasiddhā ye prakāśakāḥ |
    2. na te prakāśyarūpā hi prakāśasya, anapekṣaṇāt ||
    1. grāhyatvaṃ tu yadā teṣāṃ tadākṣaṃ grāhakaṃ matam |
    2. akṣagrahaṇakāle tu grāhikā dhīr bhaviṣyati ||
    1. tasyāṃ tu gṛhyamāṇāyām anyā dhīr grāhikeṣyate |
    2. nanv ātmā grāhako grāhyo bhavatābhyupagamyate ||
    1. kathañcid dharmarūpeṇa bhinnatvāt pratyayasya tat |
    2. grāhakatvaṃ bhavet tatra grāhyaṃ dravyādi cātmanaḥ ||
    1. yas tu nātyantabhedo 'tra kva vāsāv iṣyate mayā |
    2. pratyāsattinimittā tu pratyagātmapravarttitā ||
    1. asmatprayogasambhinnā jñānasyaiva tu kartari |
    2. bhavantī tatra saṃvittir yujyetāpy ātmakartṛkā ||
    1. na cātra karaṇajñānagrāhakākāravedanam |
    2. grāhyatvaṃ yena buddheḥ syād abhinnatve 'pi pūrvavat ||
    1. anyarūpāpi saṃvittir yady anyaviṣayeṣyate |
    2. jñānākārāpi saṃvittiḥ kasmān nārthasya kalpyate ||
    1. abhinnatvaṃ yadā ceṣṭaṃ grāhyagrāhakavastunoḥ |
    2. tadānyatarasaṃvittau dvyākāraṃ grahaṇaṃ bhavet ||
    1. yadā tu grāhyam ākāraṃ nīlādi pratipadyate |
    2. na tadā grāhakākārā saṃvittir dṛśyate kva cit ||
    1. tasmād abhinnatā cet syāt tasyāpy anubhavo bhavet |
    2. grāhyo vā nānubhūyeta grāhakānanubhūtivat ||
    1. grāhakagrahaṇe 'py evaṃ grāhyasaṃvedanaṃ bhavet |
    2. śuddham eva nirākāraṃ grāhakaṃ saṃvidasti hi ||
    1. grāhyād abhinnatāyā ca sā saṃvittir na yujyate |
    2. grāhako vā na gṛhyeta tadgrāhyānanubhūtivat ||
    1. yathāvad grāhyasaṃvittau grāhakagrahaṇe 'pi vā |
    2. grāhyagrāhakasaṃvittir nāsty eva syād dvayor api ||
    1. sa bahirdeśasambaddhaḥ ity anena nirūpyate |
    2. grāhyākārasya saṃvittir grāhakānubhavād ṛte ||
    1. paraṃ prati hi sādhyatvad arthasyākārasiddhaye |
    2. bahirdeśena sambandho na hetutvāya kalpate ||
    1. tasmād bahir itīhedaṃ niṣkṛṣṭaṃ grāhakāṃśataḥ |
    2. saṃvedyaṃ nīlapītādi pratyakṣāder udāhṛtam ||
    1. na pūrvaṃ jñāyate buddhir ityatraitad vadiṣyate |
    2. grāhakasyaiva saṃvittir lakṣyate grahaṇe kva cit ||
    1. na smarāmi mayā ko 'pi gṛhīto 'rthas tadeti hi |
    2. smaranti grāhakotpādagrāhyarūpavivarjitam ||
    1. tasmād abhinnatāyāṃ ca grāhye 'pi smaraṇaṃ bhavet |
    2. grāhakasmṛtinirbhāsāt tatrāpy eṣaiva gṛhyate ||
    1. tadatyantāvinābhāvān naikākāraṃ hi jāyate |
    2. anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ siddhaivaṃ bhinnatā tayoḥ ||
    1. grāhyāṃśo grāhakāṃśena gṛhyate, grāhakaḥ punaḥ |
    2. gṛhyeteti na vaktavyam, grāhakāntaravarjanāt ||
    1. grāhyāṃśenāpy aśaktatvān na tasya grahaṇaṃ bhavet |
    2. grāhakatvena caitasya hīyetaiva dvirūpatā ||
    1. grāhake gṛhyamāṇe ca grāhyamātraprasañjanam |
    2. na syād ākāra ekaś ced itarasyāpi nāstitā ||
    1. udbhavābhibhavābhyāṃ ca grāhyāgrāhyatvadarśanam |
    2. yathā dīpaprabhādīnāṃ rūpamātropalambhanam ||
    1. divā cāgneḥ samīpasthaiḥ sparśa evopalabhyate |
    2. gandhavad dravyavṛttau ca gandhasyaivopalambhanam ||
    1. na guṇāntarasaṃvittir yathātrābhibhavāt, tathā |
    2. nākārāntarasaṃvittir grāhyagrāhakabuddhiṣu ||
    1. grāhyād ananyabhūto 'pi kaś cin naivopalabhyate |
    2. nityānityādayo dharmāḥ śabdādigrahaṇe yathā ||
    1. abhedaṃ vābhyupetyāyaṃ prasaṅgo yadi gīyate |
    2. ekasmin gṛhyamāṇe 'śe na gṛhyetāparaḥ katham ||
    1. tasmād yat syād yadā yogyaṃ tasyaiva grahaṇaṃ tadā |
    2. dvayaṃ ca tvadupanyastaṃ śaktyabhāvān na gṛhyate ||
    1. kuto 'yam ekavastutve yogyāyogyatvasambhavaḥ |
    2. udbhavābhibhavātmatvaṃ kathaṃ caikasya kalpitam ||
    1. ekāṃśābhibhave ca syād itarābhibhavo 'pi te |
    2. tathā tasyābhibhūtatvād grāhyatvaṃ na ca yujyate ||
    1. ayogyatā vikalpyaivam, dṛṣṭāntā ye 'tra kīrtitāḥ |
    2. rūpādibhedāt tatra syād udbhavābhibhavādyapi ||
    1. yadāpy ekāntato bhedo rūpāder na parasparam |
    2. tadāpi dravyarūpasya pariṇāmas tathā tathā ||
    1. abhinnatve 'pi na grāhyam iti yac cābravīd bhavān |
    2. kṛtakatvādidharmāṇāṃ dhībhede 'nanyatā katham ||
    1. na hy anyatpratyayād asti bhinnād grāhyasya bhedakam |
    2. na ceyattaiva bhedasya deśato mūrtito 'pi vā ||
    1. kāraṇānāṃ hi sambandhaḥ kāryaiḥ kṛtakocyate |
    2. vibhāgo 'vayavānāṃ ca bhavet kva cid anityatā ||
    1. buddhyāder ātmarūpādisthānaṃ nāśitvam ucyate |
    2. nityatvaṃ sarvadā sattā, vastutvaṃ saiva kīrtyate ||
    1. pramāṇajñānasambandhaḥ prameyajñeyatocyate |
    2. sarvatra cātra bhinnatvam asti kena cid ātmanā ||
    1. tasmād yathaiva rūpāder deśabhedādibhir vinā |
    2. buddhibhedena bhedo 'sti tathaivātra pratīyatām ||
    1. atyantabhinnatāsmābhir naiva kasya cid iṣyate |
    2. sarvaṃ hi vasturūpeṇa bhidyate na parasparam ||
    1. sarvaṃ ca kṛtakatvādi kriyāhetvādyapekṣayā |
    2. gṛhyate tadasaṃvittāvabhede 'pi na gṛhyate ||
    1. jñāne naivaṃvidho bhedo nāpekṣānyatra vidyate |
    2. paraspareṇa cāpekṣā syāc cet, sannihitaś ca saḥ ||
    1. nanu grāhakam ityevaṃ grāhyam ity api vā matiḥ |
    2. nīlādigrahaṇe nāstīty apekṣā katham ucyate ||
    1. mā bhūd evaṃ tathāpy atra dvyākāre grahaṇaṃ bhavet |
    2. evaṃ cāgṛhyamāṇe vā jñāne dvyākāratā katham ||
    1. uttarottaravijñānaviśeṣād yā prakalpyate |
    2. grāhakākārasaṃvittiḥ smaraṇāc cānumānikī ||
    1. ekākāraṃ kila jñānaṃ prathamaṃ yadi kalpyate |
    2. tatas tadviṣayāpy anyā tadrūpaiva matir bhavet ||
    1. ghaṭavijñānatajjñānaviśeṣo 'to na sidhyati |
    2. grāhakākārasaṃvittau tv ākārapracayo bhavet ||
    1. jāyate pūrvavijñānaṃ dvyākāraṃ yatra tat punaḥ |
    2. tasyātmīyaś ca pūrvau ca viṣayasthāvupaplutau ||
    1. preṣv ākāravṛddhyaivaṃ pūrvebhyo bhinnatā, tathā |
    2. grāhyavat smaraṇāt paścāt saṃvittau grāhakaḥ purā ||
    1. na tāvad evamākārān paśyāmaḥ pracayānvitān |
    2. viṣayavyapadeśāc ca narte jñānanirūpaṇam ||
    1. tasmāj jñānātmanaikatve grāhyabhedanibandhaḥ |
    2. saṃvittibhedaḥ siddho 'tra kimākārāntareṇa naḥ ||
    1. nirākāratasāmye 'pi yathākāravatāṃ dhruvam |
    2. bhedaḥ svābhāvikas tadvajjñānānāṃ kiṃ na sidhyati ||
    1. smṛter uttarakālaṃ cetyetanmithyaiva gīyate |
    2. tadaiva hy asya saṃvittir arthāpattyopajāyate ||
    1. gṛhītam eva yac coktaṃ tadabhedāt, na tad, yataḥ |
    2. nāsmabhir vākyavṛttes tvaṃ nimittam anuyujyase ||
    1. grāhyagrāhakataivāsya kena cin nopalabhyate |
    2. pratyakṣajñānapakṣe ca naiṣā syād ānumānikī ||
    1. ekākāre ca vijñāne yady anyo 'py atra kalpyate |
    2. sahasrākārataikasya kasmān na parikalpyate ||
    1. grāhyagrāhakayor bhedo nanv asty eva parasparam |
    2. siddho naḥ pakṣa evaṃ syāt, na, jñānatvād abhedataḥ ||
    1. bhinnābhinnatvam ekasya kuto 'tra parikalpitam |
    2. tvayā sāṃkhyamatenaivam uktvā buddhasya śāsanam ||
    1. ekaṃ ced grāhakaṃ grāhyaṃ kuto bhinnatvavāgiyam |
    2. bhinnaṃ cet katham ucyeta tasyaikatvaṃ punas tvayā ||
    1. ekajñānād ananyatvād grāhyagrāhakayor mithaḥ |
    2. ekatvena bhavej jñānaṃ grāhyaṃ grākam eva vā ||
    1. tatra cānyatarāpāye dvitīyāpāyataḥ punaḥ |
    2. jñānasyāṃśadvayāsattvān naiḥsvābhāvyād abhāvatā ||
    1. bhinnābhyāṃ vāpy abhinnatvād bhedo jñānātmano bhavet |
    2. tatsvātmanaḥ, tataś caivaṃ siddhaṃ vastudvayaṃ hi naḥ ||
    1. tayoś ca yadi saṃjñeyaṃ jñānam ity astv arthāpi vā |
    2. jñānaṃ jñāyata ityartho dhīrbhāve karaṇe 'pi vā ||
    1. sarvathā vastubhedo naḥ siddhaḥ śabdo yathāruci |
    2. pravartatāṃ na nas tatra kācid vipratipannatā ||
    1. atha saty api bhinnatve grāhyaṃ jñānāntaraṃ bhavet |
    2. jñānatve tasya kā yuktiḥ, pūrvoktā yadi seṣyate ||
    1. jñānaṃ jñānam itīdaṃ tu na dvayor anuvartate |
    2. vyatiriktaṃ ca sāmānyaṃ tvayā nābhyupagamyate ||
    1. vyatireke tayor jñānān na jñānātmakatā bhavet |
    2. tadrūparahitatve ca jñānābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||
    1. tābhyāṃ ca tasya sambandhe pratyekaṃ vyatiṣajya ca |
    2. bhedasāvayavatvādi doṣo vaiśeṣikādivat ||
    1. yathā hi teṣāṃ jātyādau doṣā hy uktāḥ parair amī |
    2. tathaivaiṣāṃ prasajyante bhinnābhinnārthasaṅgatau ||
    1. tābhyām avyatireke vā bhedaḥ pūrvokta eva te |
    2. sādṛśyāpohasāmānyakalpanā vārayiṣyate ||
    1. vastvantarasya cābhāvāt tvayāpoho 'pi duṣkaraḥ |
    2. nājñānaṃ nāma kiñ cit syād apohyaṃ jñānavādinaḥ ||
    1. apoho na hy abhāvasya kathañ cid upapadyate |
    2. vastvantaram abhāvaḥ syād, apohyatvāc ca vastutā ||
    1. tenājñānanivṛttau hi jñāne 'nyārtha prasajyate |
    2. kalpitaṃ syād apohyaṃ cet, nātyantāsatyakalpanā ||
    1. buddhir ajñānanirbhāsā tavājñānaṃ prakalitam |
    2. tataś ca jñānam evaikam apohyatvena sammatam ||
    1. na cātmāpoha evāsti kva cit sāmānyakalpane |
    2. vṛkṣasya na hy apohyatvaṃ vṛkṣeṇaiva kadā cana ||
    1. apohye caiva vijñāne jñānatvaṃ na bhavet tava |
    2. vṛkṣatvaṃ na hy apohyeṣu kalaśādiṣu yujyate ||
    1. tataś cājñānam evārtha ity abhinnārthatā bhavet |
    2. ajñānapratyayaś cāyaṃ kimālambana iṣyate ||
    1. na tāvaj jñānanirmuktam ajñānaṃ grāhyam asti te |
    2. na ca vastu niṣiddhaṃ tadabhāvaḥ kiṃ na gṛhyate ||
    1. bhāvo na gṛhyate yena tasyābhāveṣu kā kathā |
    2. svāṃśaparyavasānaṃ ca tulyam atrāpi kāraṇam ||
    1. tena jñānāntaraṃ vā syād grāhyam ātmāṃśa eva vā |
    2. svarūpaviparītaṃ ca kathaṃ grāhyaṃ pratīyate ||
    1. yathoṣṇe 'nuṣṇadhīr nāsti, jñāne 'py ajñānadhīs tathā |
    2. tena na jñānamātratve syād apohyaṃ kathañ cana ||
    1. grāhyagrāhakayoś cāto na jñānātmasamānatā |
    2. tasmād anyataratredaṃ jñānatvaṃ sampratīyate ||
    1. tatrāpy ubhayasiddhatvād grāhakasyeti gamyate |
    2. vastubhede prasiddhe ca vyapadeśo yathāruci ||
    1. jñānam astūbhayaṃ vārtho grāhako vārtha ucyatām |
    2. buddhyor ayugapadbhāvān na dvayor mayamānatā ||
    1. kṣaṇikā hītyanenoktam, artho hy ekaḥ prasajyate |
    2. anyonyanirapekṣatvād yugapac cāpi janmani ||
    1. mānameyatvāstitvam, kriyākārakavarjanāt |
    2. arthavijñānayor atra yā mitiṃ prati saṅgatiḥ ||
    1. kāryakāraṇabhāvo 'yam, nānyatraivaṃ ca dṛśyate |
    2. niyamaś ca na labhyeta savyadakṣiṇaśṛṅgavat ||
    1. idaṃ kāryam ayaṃ hetuḥ, dvayaṃ na, anyonyasaṃśrayāt |
    2. tadbhāvabhāvitāmātraṃ hetuḥ kair naiva varṇyate ||
    1. paurvāparyavinirmuktaṃ kāryakāraṇalakṣaṇam |
    2. gavāśvasya yathā nāsti paurvāparye 'pi tat tathā ||
    1. yugapajjāyamāne 'pi santatyantaraje kṣaṇe |
    2. rūpādiṣu ghaṭe yadvat, tasmāt pūrvam avasthite ||
    1. yo yasmāj jāyate paścāt sa tatkāryam itīṣyate |
    2. hetuhetumatāṃ siddhaṃ yaugapadyanidarśanam ||
    1. yat pradīpaprabhādyuktaṃ sūkṣamaḥ kālo 'sti tatra naḥ |
    2. durlakṣas tu yathā vedhaḥ padmapattraśate tathā ||
    1. bhāgayor yaugapadyena tathaiva syān nirākriyā |
    2. na ca śaktyarpaṇadvāraṃ krameṇālambanaṃ bhavet ||
    1. grāhyaṃ tadā hy atītaṃ syāt, tadrūpyaṃ cāpramāṇakam |
    2. atītvānuviddho hi smṛtyā grāhyo 'nubhūyate ||
    1. tadvad eva bhaved atra, svapne na syāt, viparyayāt |
    2. tatra hy avartamāno 'pi gṛhyate vartamānavat ||
    1. bādhajñānād idaṃ bhrāntam, na tv atraivaṃ viparyayaḥ |
    2. tasmāt pratyakṣabuddhīnāṃ nātito viṣayo bhavet ||
    1. atītatvād yathaivāsāṃ vṛtto janmāntareṣu yaḥ |
    2. tadrūpatvena vā jñānaṃ hetur bhāvivad ucyate ||
    1. atītatve 'pi nārtho 'yaṃ dhr eṣety atra kā pramā |
    2. atītaṃ yac ca vijñānaṃ grāhyatvena prakalpitam ||
    1. tasmād grāhakarūpaṃ vā grāhyaṃ vobhayathāpi vā |
    2. grāhyākāratvamātre syād arthaḥ śabdāntareṇa te ||
    1. svakāle cāpy asaṃvitter na syāc chaktyarpaṇaṃ tataḥ |
    2. yathaivānāgatāj jñānāt santatyantarajād api ||
    1. dṛḍhatvenāpy avijñātāt tathotpannād vinaśyataḥ |
    2. kevalagrāhakatve tu viṣayatvaṃ na yujyate ||
    1. kimapekṣya ca tasyedaṃ grāhakatvaṃ prakalpyate |
    2. dvyākāratā nirastaiva, saṃvedyeta tadaiva ca ||
    1. tataś cottaravijñānaṃ na pratīkṣeta bodhakam |
    2. dvyākārakalpanāyāṃ ca parasyātmāṃśa eva te ||
    1. pramāparyavasānena nātīto viṣayo bhavet |
    2. pūrvagrāhyasarūpatve grāhakatvaṃ prahīyate ||
    1. grāhakākāramātre syād viṣayo nāsarūpataḥ |
    2. na ca śaktyarpaṇasyātra vyāpāra upalabhyate ||
    1. śaktyarpaṇasya cābhāvo yuṣmatpakṣe prasādhitaḥ |
    2. santānāntaravac caiṣāṃ niṣedhyā hetusādhyatā ||
    1. vāsyavāsakabhāvaś ca jñānatvād ekasantatau |
    2. tasmād yadbhāsakaṃ rūpaṃ tadgrāhyāt tasya bhinnatā ||
    1. tatsaṃvittāv asaṃvitte rasādigrāhakaṃ yathā |
    2. grāhyaṃ tadgrāhakāc caiva tatparāmṛśatā yataḥ ||
    1. na parāmṛśyate 'vaśyaṃ rasādigrāhakaṃ yathā |
    2. dvayaṃ paraspareṇaivaṃ bhinnaṃ sādhyaṃ rasādivat ||
    1. aikarūpyeṇa cājñānāt santānāntarabuddhivat |
    2. jñānaṃ svāṃśaṃ na gṛhṇāti jñānotpatteḥ svaśaktivat ||
    1. grāhyatvapratiṣedhaś ca dvayahīnā hi vāsate |
    2. caitrajñānaṃ tadudbhūtajñānāṃśagrāhyabodhakam ||
    1. jñānatvān na bhaved yadvat tasya dehāntarodbhavam |
    2. etayaiva diśā vācyā śaktidvayanirākriyā ||
    1. pramāṇāntarasiddhatvād anyatrānekaśaktitā |
    2. na tv atra kāraṇaṃ tādṛk śaktibhedakṛdasti te ||
    1. tasmād ubhayasiddhatvāl lāghavād yaḥ parigrahaḥ |
    2. upāyatvāc ca yat tasya pūrvagrahaṇakalpanam ||
    1. cakṣuradīndriyair atra tadanaikāntikaṃ bhavet |
    2. yad apy apratibaddhatvād utpattau gṛhyatām iti ||
    1. tatrātmanā na śaktyaṃ tannānyotpattis tadasti vā |
    2. tenaitat kāraṇābhāvāt tadānīṃ nānubhūyate ||
    1. nānyathā hy arthasadbhāvo dṛṣṭaḥ sannupapadyate |
    2. jñānaṃ cen netyataḥ paścāt pramāṇam upajāyate ||
    1. na cāpy apratibandhena kevalena graho bhavet |
    2. viśiṣṭakāraṇābhāve 'py artho naivānubhūyate ||
    1. vyāpṛtaṃ cārthasaṃvittau jñānaṃ nātmānamṛcchati |
    2. tena prakāśakatve 'pi bodhāyānyat pratīkṣyate ||
    1. īdṛśaṃ vā prakāśatvaṃ tasyārthānubhavātmakam |
    2. na cātmānubhavo 'sty asyetyātmano na prakāśakam ||
    1. sati prakāśakatve ca vyavasthā dṛśyate yathā |
    2. rūpādau cakṣurādīnāṃ tathātrāpi bhaviṣyati ||
    1. prakāśakatvaṃ bāhye 'rthe śaktyabhāvāt tu nātmani |
    2. anyena vānubhāve 'sāv anavasthā prasajyate ||
    1. tatra tatra smṛtiṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvānubhavakalpanā |
    2. ekena tv anubhūtatve sarvaṃ tatraiva sambhavet ||
    1. tatrāpi smṛtir ity etan na lokānumataṃ vacaḥ |
    2. na hi vijñānasantānaṃ kaś cit smarati laukikaḥ ||
    1. ghaṭādāv agṛhīte 'rthe yadi tāvad anantaram |
    2. arthāpattyāv abudhyante vijñānāni punaḥ punaḥ ||
    1. yāvacchramaṃ tataḥ paścāt tāvatyeva smariṣyati |
    2. tadā tv akalpite 'py evaṃ smṛtivarndhyāsutādivat ||
    1. smṛtibhrāntaś ca yāpy atra paścāj jñāneṣu jāyate |
    2. tadaivārthasmṛter eṣāṃ tajñānādipramāṇatā ||
    1. yāvacchramaṃ ca tadbuddhis tatprabandhe mahaty api |
    2. śramād rucyānyasamparkād vicchedo viṣayeṣv iva ||
    1. tatrāpi smṛtir ity eṣāṃ prathame pratyaye yadi |
    2. tanmātragrahaṇād evaṃ nānavasthā prasajyate ||
    1. smaraṇaṃ tv atha sarveṣu tatsiddhyai grahaṇaṃ tathā |
    2. pramāṇavattvād āyātaḥ pravāhaḥ kena vāryate ||
    1. atha tānyādyavijñānaviṣayāṇīti kalpyate |
    2. nottarottarabuddhīnāṃ viśeṣa upapadyate ||
    1. vijñānaviṣayatvaṃ ca yasya sarvāsu buddhiṣu |
    2. ghaṭavijñāna tajñānaviśeṣas tena durlabhaḥ ||
    1. smaran yathaiva vijñānaṃ nirākāraṃ smaratyayam |
    2. tathā smaran gṛhītārthaṃ nirākāratayā smaret ||
    1. jñānapṛṣṭena yo 'py ūrdhvaṃ parāmarśo bhavaty asau |
    2. tasyārtheṣv abhyupāyatvān na tu grāhyatvakāritaḥ ||
    1. pratyāsannatvasambandhau grāhyatvāsambhavāc cyutau |
    2. viṣayatvena vāpy etau staḥ kiṃ deśāvibhāgataḥ ||
    1. arthākārasya yo 'py ukto mithyājñāneṣv asambhavaḥ |
    2. dośakālānyathāmātrasambhavaḥ keṣu cit kṛtaḥ ||
    1. pratyakṣād anyavijñānam atītānāgatair api |
    2. janyate 'rthe bhavantīṣu vāsanāsvasatīṣu vā ||
    1. yaḥ punar nānubhūto 'rtho na vāpy anubhaviṣyate |
    2. vāsanābhāvatas tatra tavāpy anubhavaḥ katham ||
    1. vināpi vāsanātaś ced buddhir utpadyate tataḥ |
    2. vāsanāyā nimittatvam abhyupetaṃ virudhyate ||
    1. vāsanā ced bhavet tatra sā ca saṃvittipūrvikā |
    2. tathā sati ca pūrvatra gṛhītaḥ kvāpy asau dhruvam ||
    1. evaṃ ca naiva vaktavyam atyantābhavanaṃ kva cit |
    2. anyathānupapatyā hi siddhā janmāntare 'stitā ||
    1. duṣṭatvena ca vijñānam anyathāpi vyavasthitam |
    2. pṛthivyādiṣu gṛhṇīyād ākāraṃ tannibandhanam ||
    1. tānyapāsya tu naivārthe kva cid ākārakalpanā |
    2. na jñānaṃ hy anavaṣṭambham ātmānaṃ labdhum arhati ||
    1. vijñānasyaiva vā kāryaṃ yady eṣo 'nye ca kalpitāḥ |
    2. viśeṣaḥ ko 'tra yenāyam atyantāsannitīṣyate ||
    1. tasmād bhrāntir api tv eṣāṃ kalpayantyartham eva naḥ |
    2. kalpayatyanyathā santaṃ na tv ātmānaṃ vyavasyati ||
    1. tataś ca bādhakajñānād vācoyuktir iyaṃ bhavet |
    2. arthe 'nyathāpi saty eṣa dhiyākāraḥ pratīyate ||
    1. dvicandrādimatiṣv evam, tārakādimatau tathā |
    2. strītvādyanyatra dṛṣṭaṃ syāt, kathañ cid veha sambhavet ||
    1. śabdamātrapratīyā vā, dṛṣṭair vā kaiś cid iṅganāt |
    2. saṃstyānaprasavasthānair yathā pātañjale mate ||
    1. tena liṅgatrayasyātra sadbhāvaḥ syāt pramāṇavān |
    2. apekṣābhedataś cātra virodho 'pi na vidyate ||
    1. kuṇapādimatau caivaṃ sārvarūpye vyavasthite |
    2. vāsanāḥ sahakāriṇyo vyavasthākāradarśane ||
    1. svapratyayānukāro hi bahvākāreṣu vastuṣu |
    2. nirdhāraṇe bhaved dhetur nāpūrvākārakalpane ||
    1. tathā dīrghaghaṭatvādau bhinnāpekṣānibandhanā |
    2. ākārabhedasampattir aviruddhā bhaviṣyati ||
    1. nānekākārasaṃvitter nirākāratvakalpanā |
    2. yuktā, pratītibhedāt tu bahvākāratvasambhavaḥ ||
    1. saṃvitteś ca viruddhānām ekasminn api sambhavaḥ |
    2. ekākāraṃ bhaved ekam iti neśvarabhāṣitam ||
    1. tathaiva tadupetavyaṃ yad yathaivopalabhyate |
    2. na cāpy aikāntikaṃ tasya syād ekatvaṃ ca vastunaḥ ||
    1. tasmād deśādisadbhāvanimittaiḥ pratyayaiḥ pṛthak |
    2. vastvākārāḥ pratīyerann udbhavābhibhavātmakāḥ ||
    1. yugapadgrāhāṇāṃ ca yo yadākāravācinam |
    2. śabdaṃ smarati tenāsāv ākāraḥ sampratīyate ||
    1. nityaṃ satsu tathā loke rūpādiṣu ghaṭe pṛthak |
    2. cakṣurādyanurodhena saṃvittir vyavatiṣṭhate ||
    1. evam eva ghaṭatvādau sarvān prati bhavaty api |
    2. vācakasmṛtibhedena saṃvittir vyavatiṣṭhate ||
    1. tasmād bahiḥ sthito 'py ātmā narāṇāṃ cakṣurādibhiḥ |
    2. prāpya vāprāpya vā buddher viṣayatvena kalpyate ||
    1. vadanti laukikā yac ca yādṛg jñānaṃ tathā bahiḥ |
    2. te punar jñānasaṃvittyā tathārthaṃ prati jānate ||
    1. grāhakatvena vijñānaṃ yathārthaṃ naḥ samarpayet |
    2. tādṛgarthaḥ sa ityevaṃ teṣāṃ vā tadupāyataḥ ||
    1. laiṅgikāsattvam aprāptair etair bāhyārthavādibhiḥ |
    2. jñānānubhavam utkramya bāhya eva pratīyate ||
    1. yathā loke ca tadbuddhir vācyam evaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ |
    2. na yādṛgantarākāras tādṛg bāhyo 'vakalpate ||
    1. utpadyamānā gṛhyeta dhīrarthagrahaṇe yadi |
    2. pūrvapakṣasya kiṃ siddham, kathaṃ cārthāntaraṃ vadet ||
    1. bāhyārthavādinaṃ brūte bhavān kiṃ naivam icchati |
    2. pratibandho na tasyāsti gṛhṇātyarthāntaraṃ yadā ||
    1. uttaraṃ grahakābhāvāl liṅgābhāvāc ca nāsti naḥ |
    2. tadā grahaṇam ity etat, anyatarkeṣu cocyate ||
    1. teṣu tarkeṣu vijñānam arthakāle 'vagamyate |
    2. tathā satyarthanāśaḥ syād ity etadupadiśyate ||
    1. nanv ity etadasambaddhaṃ pareṣṭasyaiva codanāt |
    2. paurvāpryavibhāgo 'pi prāguktena virudhyate ||
    1. kṣaṇikatvena yuktaṃ syāj jñātatvam atha cet tadā |
    2. bhūtakālāśrayād brūyād, pṛthoktasya punarvacaḥ ||
    1. atrāpi na svasiddhāntamūce vyājāt parasya tu |
    2. bhrāntatvād anyathā pakṣaṃ gṛhītveti sma pṛcchati ||
    1. sahotpattyupalabdhā hi jñānasyaikāntataḥ sthitiḥ |
    2. prāgūrdhvaṃ vārthasaṃvitter yugapad veti cintyate ||
    1. evaṃ cārthasya saṃvitteḥ paścāj jñānāvabodhanam |
    2. bravītu nūnam etasya paścād utpadyate 'pi tat ||
    1. na caitac chaktyate tasmād utpatter apakarṣaṇam |
    2. karomi tāvat tatkālā saṃvittir api setsyati ||
    1. prāk ca tadgrahaṇe siddhe bāhyābhyantarayor dhruvam |
    2. vivekādarśanam, tasmād idam, pūrvaṃ ca coditam ||
    1. yugapad gṛhyamāṇe 'pi nākāro 'rthasya lakṣyate |
    2. tasmād arthasya saṃvittiḥ pūrvaṃ yatnena sādhyate ||
    1. yas tv etasyottaro granthaḥ prāg evāsau nirūpitaḥ |
    2. na tv etat sādhanaṃ sākṣāt pūrvaṃ buddher abodhane ||
    1. na parāmṛśyate 'rthātmā jñāto 'py ajñātavad yataḥ |
    2. tasān na grahaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ buddheḥ kiṃ kena saṅgatam ||
    1. ataḥ pūrvopalabdhyā yo buddhyākāro 'tra vāñchitaḥ |
    2. tannirākaraṇenaiva phalatvād granthavarṇanā ||
    1. kāmaṃ buddher iti tv etadarthādhīnatvam ucyate |
    2. na cārtharūpād bhedena dhiyām asti nirūpaṇam ||
    1. pararūpanirūpyaṃ ca na meyaṃ mṛgatoyavat |
    2. asadgrāhyānusāreṇa jñānasaṃvedyatā tava ||
    1. svacchatvāt tu svarūpasya kalpitā grāhyatā dhiyām |
    2. vāsanopaplavāt tena na meyaṃ pāramārthikam ||
    1. nimittaniyatatvaṃ tu samānam ubhayor api |
    2. nijaśaktyanusāritvāj jñānabāhyārthavādinoḥ ||
    1. tantvarthair api kasmād vaḥ kriyate kevalaḥ paṭaḥ |
    2. nārabhyate ghaṭaḥ kiṃ tair mṛtpiṇḍārthena vā paṭaḥ ||
    1. tantumṛtpiṇḍavijñāne hy anuyojye mate yadi |
    2. arthaparyanuyogo 'pi tadvad eva prasajyate ||
    1. arthārambhavyavasthā cet sāmarthyaniyamāśrayā |
    2. jñānārambhavyavasthāyāṃ sāmarthyaṃ kena vāryate ||
    1. tasmād yatrobhayor doṣaḥ parihāro 'pi vā samaḥ |
    2. naikaḥ paryanuyoktavyas tādṛgarthavicāraṇe ||
    1. deśakālanimittāni vyañjakānyarthavādinaḥ |
    2. śaktīnāṃ kāraṇasthānāṃ svakāryaniyamaṃ prati ||
    1. śaktayo 'pi ca bhāvānāṃ kāryārthāpattikalpitāḥ |
    2. prasiddhāḥ pāramārthikyaḥ pratikāryaṃ vyavasthitāḥ ||
    1. bhavatas tu na vijñānād bhinnābhinnā nirūpyate |
    2. śaktiḥ saṃvṛtisadbhāvam utsṛjya paramārthataḥ ||
    1. vāsanaiva ca yuṣmābhiḥ śaktiśabdena gīyate |
    2. nimittaniyatatvaṃ ca vāsanāyā yad ucyate ||
    1. tasyāś cāsambhavenaitad apārārthyāc ca durlabham |
    2. deśakālanimittādi na ca te 'sti niyāmakam ||
    1. matvaitad api cety āha bhāṣyakāraḥ paraṃ prati |
    2. tasmād aparihāro 'yaṃ tantubhyas te yathā paṭaḥ ||
    1. tathā me tantubuddhibhyaḥ paṭabuddhir itīdṛśaḥ |
    2. evamādyapramāṇābhyāṃ na tāvad bāhyaśūnyatā ||
    1. āgamasya tu naiveha vyāpāraḥ, ato 'nyathāpi vā |
    2. nopamā sadṛśābhāvāt, nārthāpattir viparyayāt ||
    1. tasmād abhāvagamyatvaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ sthitaṃ hi naḥ |
    2. evaṃ pramāṇato 'siddhā yaiḥ prameyāśrayocyate ||
    1. bāhyasyāṇusamūhāder grāhyasyāsambhavekṣaṇāt ||
    1. tairāntarāsambhavato yathoktād jñeyatvam anyasya balād upeyam |
    2. grāhyā na ceṣṭāḥ paramāṇavo 'taḥ satyaḥ samūhaḥ pratipādanīyaḥ ||
    1. iti bahirviṣayapratipādanād tadabhāvakṛtā matisaṃvṛtiḥ |
    2. ubhayatattvavidāṃ paramārthataḥ, kṣamam idaṃ dhuri dharmavicāraṇe ||

{5,5 anumānapariccheda AMP}

    1. pratyakṣāvyabhicāritvād evaṃlakṣaṇakaṃ ca yat |
    2. prasiddham anumānādi na parīkṣyaṃ tad apy ataḥ ||
    1. pramātā jñātasambandhaḥ, ekadeśyatha vocyate |
    2. karmadhārayapakṣo vā sambandhinyekadeśatā ||
    1. dvayaṃ vā jñātasambandham upalabdhaṃ parasparam |
    2. tasyaikadeśaśabdābhyām ucyete samudāyinau ||
    1. sambandho vyāptir iṣṭātra liṅgādharmasya liṅginā |
    2. vyāpyasya gamakatvaṃ ca vyāpakaṃ gamyam iṣyate ||
    1. yo yasya deśakālābhyāṃ samo nyūno 'pi vā bhavet |
    2. sa vyāpyo vyāpakas tasya samo vābhyadhiko 'pi vā ||
    1. tena vyāpye gṛhīte 'rthe vyāpakas tasya gṛhyate |
    2. na hy anyathā bhavaty eṣā vyāpyavyāpakatā tayoḥ ||
    1. vyāpakatvagṛhītas tu vyāpyo yady api vastutaḥ |
    2. ādhikye 'py aviruddhatvād vyāpyaṃ na pratipādayet ||
    1. vispaṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭam etac ca goviṣāṇitvayor mitau |
    2. vyāpyatvād gamikā gāvo vyāpikā na viṣāṇitā ||
    1. tena yatrāpy ubhau dhrmau vyāpyavyāpakasammatau |
    2. tatrāpi vyāpyataiva syād aṅgaṃ na vyāpitā miteḥ ||
    1. tena dharmyantareṣv eṣā yasya yenaiva yādṛśī |
    2. deśe yāvati kāle vā vyāpyatā prāṅ nirūpitā ||
    1. tasya tāvati tādṛk sa dṛṣṭo dharmyantare punaḥ |
    2. vyāpyāṃśo vyāpakāṃśasya tathaiva pratipādakaḥ ||
    1. bhūyodarśanagamyā ca vyāptiḥ, sāmānyadharmayoḥ |
    2. jñāyate bhedahānena, kva cic cāpi viśeṣayoḥ ||
    1. kṛttikodayamālakṣya rohiṇyāsattikḷptivat |
    2. vyāpteś ca dṛśyamānāyāḥ kaś cid dharmaḥ prayojakaḥ ||
    1. asmin saty amunā bhāvyam iti śaktyā nirūpyate |
    2. anye paraprayuktānāṃ vyāptīnām upajīvakāḥ ||
    1. tair dṛṣṭair api naiveṣṭā vyāpakāṃśāvadhāraṇā |
    2. ye tu tān api visrabdhaṃ sādhyasiddhyau prayuñjate ||
    1. sulabhaiḥ pratihetvādidoṣair bhrāmyanti te ciram |
    2. teṣv āgamaviruddhatvaṃ svayaṃ ceṣṭavighātitā ||
    1. alaukikavivādāś ca varṇyas te haitukais tataḥ |
    2. niṣiddhitvena hiṃsānām adharmatvaṃ prayujyate ||
    1. tadabhāve na tatsiddhir hiṃsātvād aprayojakāt |
    2. hetudvayaprayukte ca mithyātve sarvabuddhiṣu ||
    1. jñānatvotpattimattvādisādhako naprayojakaḥ |
    2. traivarṇikaprayuktā ca yāgādeḥ svargahetutā ||
    1. na manuṣyatvamātreṇa śūdrasthena prayujyate |
    2. kṛtasāvayavatvādiprayuktā ca vināśitā ||
    1. prayatnānantarajñānasadṛśair na prayujyate |
    2. jātimattvendriyatvādi vastusanmātrabandhanam ||
    1. śadānityatvasiddhyarthaṃ ko vaded yo na tārkikaḥ |
    2. tasmād ya eva yasyārtho dṛṣṭaḥ sādhanaśaktitaḥ ||
    1. sa eva gamakas tasya na prasaṅgānvito 'pi yaḥ |
    2. upāttaś caikadeśābhyāṃ dharmy apy atraikadeśatā ||
    1. apārārthye hi dhūmādeḥ svarūpair naikadeśatā |
    2. sa eva cobhayātamāyaṃ gamyo gamaka eva vā ||
    1. asiddhenaikadeśena gamyaḥ siddhena bodhakaḥ |
    2. ataḥ pṛthagabhinno vāprayoktāṇāṃ vivakṣaya ||
    1. anityaḥ kṛtako yasmād dhūmavān agnimān iti |
    2. dharmyabhinnam upādānam, bhedo 'trāgnir itīdṛśe ||
    1. ekadeśaviśiṣṭaś ca dharmyevātrānumīyate |
    2. na hi tannirapekṣatve sambhavaty anumeyatā ||
    1. na dharmamātraṃ siddhatvāt, tathā dharmī, tathobhayam |
    2. vyastaṃ vāpi samastaṃ vā svātantryeṇānumīyate ||
    1. ekadeśasya liṅgatvaṃ sādhyenānugamo 'sya ca |
    2. dvayaṃ ca na syād iṣṭaṃ sat pakṣeṣv eṣu yathākramam ||
    1. anityatvādayo dharmāḥ kṛtakatvādayo na hi |
    2. dhvaninānugamo naiṣāṃ nobhayasyobhayena vā ||
    1. sambandho 'py anupādānān nāmnā ṣaṣṭhyāpi vā mitau |
    2. na cāpy anugamas tena liṅgasyeha nidarśyate ||
    1. na cākāradvayaṃ tasya sādhyasādhanabhāg bhavet |
    2. tasmad arthagṛhītatvānmatubarthasya gamyatā ||
    1. na svāntantryeṇa mantavyā, yathā daṇḍyādiśabdataḥ |
    2. viśīṣṭārthapratītau syāt sambandho nāntarīyakaḥ ||
    1. viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvam āpannau dvāv imāv ataḥ |
    2. gamyau, aṅgāṅgibhāvas tu kaiś cid iṣṭo vikalpataḥ ||
    1. sarvathā dharmiṇo dharmo dharmeṇa tv avagamyate |
    2. viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatve na viśeṣo 'vadhāryate ||
    1. tatrotaraṃ vadanty anye yadi dharmī viśeṣaṇam |
    2. hetudharmeṇa samandhas tasyāprādhānyataḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
    1. pradhānatvād dhi dharmeṇa sambandho vākyato bhavet |
    2. tatrāsambhavataḥ paścāt kalpyo 'sau dharminā saha ||
    1. dhvaner ity atha vā vācyam, anvayasya tu darśane |
    2. bhedopāttasya dharmasya guṇābhāvo na duṣyati ||
    1. agner deśaviśiṣṭatve na caitat pakṣalakṣaṇam |
    2. viśiṣṭatāsya deśena bhaved evamprakārikā ||
    1. yo 'gniḥ so 'sti kva cid deśe yo dṛṣṭo yatra tatra vā |
    2. agniḥ pūrvānubhūto vā deśamātreṇa saṅgataḥ ||
    1. yo 'gniḥ so 'nena yukto vā, yo dṛṣṭo 'nena so 'tha vā |
    2. yo 'yaṃ sa deśamātreṇa yuktaḥ, pūrveṇa vāpy ayam ||
    1. etaddeśaviśiṣṭo vā yo 'yam agnir iti, iha tu |
    2. pūrvayoḥ siddhasādhyatvaṃ pareṣu syād viruddhatā ||
    1. vyāptir etena deśena sarvāgnīnāṃ na yujyate |
    2. nāpi pūrvasya, nāpy eṣa vahniḥ sarvair viśiṣyate ||
    1. deśaiḥ, pūrveṇa vāpy asya na deśena viśeṣyatā |
    2. etaddeśaviśiṣṭo 'yam ity etat kathyate katham ||
    1. yadā deśānapekṣo 'gnir nāyam ity avadhāryate |
    2. agneḥ pūrvataraṃ cātra deśa evāvadhāryate ||
    1. tajjñānakālabuddhaś ca na deśaḥ syād viśeṣaṇam |
    2. deśasya parvatādes tu svarūpe pāvakād ṛte ||
    1. gṛhīte 'gniviśiṣṭasya punarjñānaṃ na duṣyati |
    2. tasmād dharmaviśiṣṭasya dharmiṇaḥ syāt prameyatā ||
    1. sā deśasyāgniyuktasya, dhūmasyānyaiś ca kalpitā |
    2. nanu śabdavad eva syāl liṅgamyaṃ viśiṣaṇam ||
    1. naivam, na hy atra liṅgasya śaktyanekatvakalpanā |
    2. na ca tasyānumeyatvam, viśeṣyaś cāvadhāritaḥ ||
    1. viśiṣṭatvena cājñānāt tanmātrasyānumeyatā |
    2. nanu dhūmaviśeṣyatve hetoḥ pakṣaikadeśatā ||
    1. naitad asti, viśeṣe hi sādhye sāmānyahetutā |
    2. dhūmatajjānasambandhasmṛtiprāmāṇyakalpane ||
    1. phalena viṣayaikatvaṃ tadvyāpārāt puroditam |
    2. prameyadhīpramāṇatvaṃ bhāṣyakāras tu manyate ||
    1. pratyakṣāniyamoktaś ca sarvatraivānuṣajyate |
    2. anumānagṛhītasya tenaiva pratipādanam ||
    1. parebhyo vāñchatā vācyaḥ pūrvapakṣo yathoditaḥ |
    2. tatra dharmiṇam uddiśya sādhyadharmo vidhīyate ||
    1. niyamas tadvipakṣāc ca kalpyate nāvirodhinaḥ |
    2. asannikṛṣṭavācā ca dvayam atra jihāsitam ||
    1. tādrūpyeṇa paricchittis tadviparyayato 'pi ca |
    2. pramitasya pramāṇe hi nāpekṣā jāyate punaḥ ||
    1. tādrūpyeṇa paricchinne pramāṇaṃ niṣphalaṃ param |
    2. vaiparītyaparicchinne nāvakāśaḥ parasya tu ||
    1. mūle tasya hy anutpanne pūrveṇa viṣayo hṛtaḥ |
    2. pratyakṣādeś ca ṣaṭkasya yenaivārtho 'vadhāritaḥ ||
    1. tenaivottarabādhaḥ syād, vikalpāder asambhavāt |
    2. agrāhyatā tu śabdādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virudhyate ||
    1. teṣām aśrāvaṇatvādi viruddham anumānataḥ |
    2. na hi śrāvaṇatā nāma pratyakṣeṇāvagamyate ||
    1. sānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ gamyate badhirādiṣu |
    2. tridhā śabdavirodhaḥ syāt pratijñādivibhāgataḥ ||
    1. pratijñāpūrvasañjalpasarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ |
    2. yāvajjīvam ahaṃ maunīty uktimātreṇa bādhyate ||
    1. sarvavākyamṛṣātve tu dharmoktyaivātmabādhanam |
    2. dharmyuktyāhaṃ yato jātaḥ sā vandhyā jananī mama ||
    1. bauddhasya śabdanityatvaṃ pūrvopetena bādhyate |
    2. candraśabdābhidheyatvaṃ śaśino yo niṣedhati ||
    1. sa sarvalokasiddhena candrajñānena bādhyate |
    2. jñātagogavayākāraṃ prati yaḥ sādhayed idam ||
    1. na gor gavayasādṛśyaṃ tasya bādhopamānataḥ |
    2. gehāvagatanāstitvo jīvaṃś caitro yadā bahiḥ ||
    1. nāstīti sādhyate bādhas tatrārthāpattito bhavet |
    2. agnāvadāhake sādhye śabde cānabhidhāyake ||
    1. śrotrādināstitāyāṃ ca śabdānityatvasādhane |
    2. śrutārthāpattibādho 'tra yadāptoktinivārite ||
    1. divābhujau niṣidhyeta hetunā rātribhojanam |
    2. śaśaśṛṅgādisadbhāvavirodho 'nupalabdhitaḥ ||
    1. evaṃ ca dharmasambandhabādhas tāvad udāhṛtaḥ |
    2. dharmadharmyubhayeṣāṃ ca svarūpasvaviśeṣayoḥ ||
    1. śrutyarthākṣiptayor vākye vācyaḥ sarvapramāṇakaḥ |
    2. tṛṇādivikriyāhetor agnimaddhimasādhane ||
    1. pratyakṣāvagatāc chaityāt tadviśeṣotthabādhanam |
    2. adharmo vihito duḥkhaṃ karotyalpam itīha tu ||
    1. vihitatvād adharmasya svarūpasyaiva bādhanam |
    2. tathā duḥkhanimittatvaṃ viśeṣas tasya bādhyate ||
    1. ayathārthā dhiyaḥ sarvāḥ ity ukte dvayabādhanam |
    2. svarūpasvaviśeṣābhyām, taddhīmithyātvasādhanāt ||
    1. kṣaṇikātyantamithyātve viśeṣau ca dvayor iha |
    2. darśanād ekadeśasyety anenaitad vyudasyate ||
    1. yatraikasyobhayor vāpi saṃśayādhīviparyayāḥ |
    2. śaityān na dāhako bahniś cākṣuṣatvād anityatā ||
    1. śabdasyetyevamādau tu dvayoḥ siddho viparyayaḥ |
    2. kṛtakatvaguṇatvādau parokte yājñikaṃ prati ||
    1. svokte caivamprakāre syād asiddho 'nyatarasya tu |
    2. bāṣpādibhāvasandigdho dvayor anyatarasya vā ||
    1. dhūmas tridhāpy asiddhaḥ syāt, evaṃ tāvat svarūpataḥ |
    2. eta eva prakārāḥ syur āśrayāsiddhikalpane ||
    1. jñāte 'pi hi svarūpeṇa nātaddharme 'sti hetutā |
    2. sarvatra dṛṣṭakāryatvād ātmā sarvagatas tv iti ||
    1. bauddhaṃ pratyāśrayāsiddhaḥ, laukikādes tu saṃśayaḥ |
    2. bāṅmātrāsiddhimātreṇa vyavahārāprakalpanāt ||
    1. dvābhyāṃ yo 'sattvato jñātas tadvaco dūṣaṇaṃ matam |
    2. itarat sādhanaṃ tu syād vādinā yadi sādhyate ||
    1. nirākaraṇasiddhau vā dūṣaṇaṃ prativādinaḥ |
    2. sandehaviparītatvahetū cātra nirākṛtau ||
    1. jñātasambandhavacanāt, trayaḥ saṃśayahetavaḥ |
    2. san sādhye tadabhāve vā dvābhyāṃ vyāvṛtta eva ca ||
    1. dvau viruddhārthasambaddhau yāv ekatraikadeśini |
    2. prameyānityatāmūrtidharmāḥ sādhāraṇā dvayoḥ ||
    1. nityāyatnotthayatnotthānityeṣu dviranityataḥ |
    2. nityā bhūrgandhavattvena syād asādhāraṇas tvayam ||
    1. niścayaikāṅgavaikalyād eṣa saṃśayakāraṇam |
    2. sādhāraṇo yathā dṛṣṭo buddhidvayanimittakaḥ ||
    1. viruddhaikānavāpteś ca saṃśaye kāraṇaṃ matam |
    2. atrāsādhāraṇo nāsti tadabhāvamukhena tu ||
    1. dvayāsattvavirodhāc ca mataḥ saṃśayakāraṇam |
    2. sandigdhahetutā caiṣāṃ viṣayāpekṣayocyate ||
    1. nirṇayasyāpi hetutvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sādhyāntare yataḥ |
    2. vyavacchedānvayau labdhvā, niṣkriyādāv amūrtivat ||
    1. kṣityekadeśasiddhatve gandhavattvasya hetutā |
    2. yatrāpratyakṣatā vāyor arūpatvena sādhyate ||
    1. sparśāt pratyakṣatā vāsau viruddhāvyabhicāritā |
    2. ke cij jātyantaraṃ caināṃ varṇayantyapare punaḥ ||
    1. sādhāraṇatvam aṃśena samastaṃ vāpy ananvayam |
    2. pratijñā yatra bādhyeta pūrvoktair yasya sādhanaiḥ ||
    1. tat parājayataḥ kāryo nirṇayo bādhavarjanāt |
    2. kva cit saṃśayahetū yau pratyekatvena lakṣitau ||
    1. saṅghāte nirṇayas tābhyāmūrdhvatākākavattvavat |
    2. pratyekaṃ saṃhatau vāpi gamakāvavirodhinau ||
    1. tasmād bhinnau viruddhārthau hetū cātra nidarśitau |
    2. ṣoḍhā viruddhatām āhuś caturddhā vaikadhāpi vā ||
    1. śrutyarthoktasya bādhāyāṃ pratijñārthasya hetunā |
    2. nityatve kṛtakatvasya dharmabādhād viruddhatā ||
    1. bādho dharmaviśeṣasya yadā tv evaṃ prayujyate |
    2. arthavacchabdarūpaṃ syāt prāksambandhāvadhāraṇāt ||
    1. vibhaktimattvāt paścādvat svarūpeṇeti cāśrite |
    2. asvarūpārthayogas tu paścāc chabdasya dṛśyate ||
    1. tena prāg api sambandhād asvarūpārthatā bhavet |
    2. ihapratyayahetutvād dravyāder vyatiricyate ||
    1. samavāyo yathehāyaṃ ghaṭa ityādisaṅgatiḥ |
    2. atrāpy asamavāyatvaṃ saṃyogasyeva sidhyati ||
    1. tena dharmisvarūpasya vaiparītyād viruddhatā |
    2. yac ca sattāvad ekatvaṃ samavāyasya kalpitam ||
    1. tatra saṃyogavadbhedāt syād viśeṣaviruddhatā |
    2. nityam ātmāstitā kaiś cid yadā sautrāntikaṃ prati ||
    1. sādhyate 'vayavābhāvād vyomavad dvayabādhanam |
    2. tadobhayaviśeṣasya bādho 'yaṃ sādhyate yadā ||
    1. pārārthyaṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ saṅghātāc chayanādivat |
    2. śayane saṅghapārārthyaṃ bhautikavyāptahetuke ||
    1. ātmānaṃ prati pārārthyam asiddham iti bādhanam |
    2. asaṃhataparārthatve dṛṣṭe saṃhatatāpi ca ||
    1. anahaṅkārikatvaṃ ca cakṣurādeḥ prasajyate |
    2. gamakasyaikadeśasya vyāptir gamyeti bhāṣitum ||
    1. sādhyasādharmyavaidharmyadṛṣṭāntaḥ pratipādyate |
    2. tatra hetvartham uddiśya sādhyopādānam iṣyate ||
    1. uddeśyo vyāpyate dharmo vyāpakaś cetaro mataḥ |
    2. yadvṛttayoḥ prāthamyam ity ādyuddeśalakṣaṇam ||
    1. tadvṛttam eva kāraś ca syād upādeyalakṣaṇam |
    2. vadatyarthaṃ svaśaktyā ca śabdo vaktranapekṣayā ||
    1. sādhyahetutvam arthānāṃ vyāptiśaktyanurodhataḥ |
    2. tatrājñānād yadā vakta sahacāravivakṣayā ||
    1. viparyayeṇa vā hetau na vyāptatvaṃ vivakṣati |
    2. vivakṣann api vā śabdaṃ tadyogyaṃ na vaded yadi ||
    1. ghaṭe kṛtakanāśitve nāśivyāptaṃ kṛtena vā |
    2. na tadeṣṭasya hetutvam, syād aniṣṭasya caiva tat ||
    1. tasmād vyāpyatvarūpeṇa vācyo hetutvasammataḥ |
    2. yadā samyak prayukte 'pi vākye 'rtho na tathā bhavet ||
    1. sādhyahetūbhayavyāptiśūnyatvāt paramārthataḥ |
    2. nityo dhvaniramūrttatvāt karmavat paramāṇuvat ||
    1. ghaṭavad vyomavaccāpi, tadasadvādinaṃ prati |
    2. dharmyasiddhāv api hy evaṃ dṛṣṭāntābhāsatā bhavet ||
    1. tat sadbhāve 'pi ca vyomni dvayayukte 'pi kīrtite |
    2. karmādyālocanād vyāptir hetor nāstīti varjanam ||
    1. vyāptyā sādharmya ukte ca na vaidharmyam apekṣyate |
    2. sahabhāvitvadṛṣṭyā tu yadā vyāptiṃ na lakṣayet ||
    1. paraḥ sādharmyadṛṣṭāntāt tac ca nāpekṣate yadā |
    2. vaktā vā sahabhāvitvaṃ śuddhaṃ tena vaded yadā ||
    1. viparītānvayaṃ vāpi tat samādhitsayā tadā |
    2. pūrvajñānopamardena vaidharmyeṇeṣṭasādhanam ||
    1. sāhityamātraṃ pūrvoktaṃ hetos tatropayujyate |
    2. vyāpyavyāpakabhāvo hi bhāvayor yādṛg iṣyate ||
    1. tayor abhāvayos tasmād viparītaḥ pratīyate |
    2. dhūmabhāve 'gnibhāvena vyāpte 'nagnis tataś cyutaḥ ||
    1. adhūma eva vidyetetyevaṃ vyāpyatvamaśnute |
    2. tathānagnāvadhūmena vyāpte dhūmas tatacyutaḥ ||
    1. anyatrānavakāśatvād vyāpyate dhruvam agninā |
    2. vyāpakau tu yadocyete bhāvābhāvau tadā tataḥ ||
    1. naiva vyāpyād vipakṣasya pracyutiḥ kathitā bhavet |
    2. tasmād dhūmena sādhyatvam agneḥ prārthayate yadā ||
    1. tadānagnir adhūmena vyāpto vācyaḥ, na cānyathā |
    2. anagnyadhūmasāhitye vyāpter vāpi viparyaye ||
    1. na prastutopakāraḥ syād anyad vāpi prasādhyate |
    2. yatrāpy arthasya śūnyatvaṃ dvābhyām ekena vā bhavet ||
    1. yad anityaṃ tu tan mūrtam aṇuvad buddhivat khavat |
    2. sādhyena vyāptisiddhyaiva vyatireko 'tra kathyate ||
    1. yasyāyaṃ nāsty asau hetus tena sādhyena nāpyate |
    2. tena dṛṣṭe 'pi sāhitye na sarvo gamya iṣyate ||
    1. sahadṛṣṭir na sambandho vyāptir naiva ca tāvatā |
    2. mūrtānityatvayukte 'pi tasmād aṅgīkṛte ghaṭe ||
    1. karmādau vyāptyabhāvena na dṛṣṭāntatvam iṣyate |
    2. aśeṣāpekṣitatvāc ca saukaryāc cāpy adarśanāt ||
    1. sādhane yadyapīṣṭo 'tra vyatireko 'numāṃ prati |
    2. tāvatā na hy anaṅgatvaṃ yuktiḥ śābde hi vakṣyate ||
    1. bodhaprasaṅgo bhedānāṃ na cāvyāpter bhaviṣyati |
    2. astisāmānyavastveṣu vyāpitā tatra gamyatām ||
    1. ke cit sādharmyadṛṣṭānte vyāptyāpi kathite punaḥ |
    2. vaidharmyoktim apīcchanti, vyāvṛttiniyamecchayā ||
    1. hetau sādharmyadṛṣṭāntāt sādhyenaivāvadhārite |
    2. vyāvṛttiḥ sarvataḥ prāptā sādhyābhāve niyamyate ||
    1. tat tu mandaphalaṃ yasmāt pakṣe 'py evaṃ nirūpitam |
    2. vyāpakābhāvamātraṃ hi vyāpyān nityaṃ nivartate ||
    1. tasmād yathaiva śuklatve paṭasyokte virodhinām |
    2. nivṛttir na tu dairdhyādes tathātrāpi bhaviṣyati ||
    1. dvaividhyaṃ nopapannaṃ tu yathaiva hy agnidhūmayoḥ |
    2. pratyakṣadṛṣṭaḥ sambandho gatiprāptyos tathaiva hi ||
    1. āditye 'nupalabdhiś cen na deśe 'py adhunātane |
    2. kva cit tatropalabdhiś ced devadatte 'pi dṛśyatām ||
    1. yadi dharmyantarāpekṣā tatra sāmānyadṛṣṭatā |
    2. syād agnidhūmayoḥ saiva, tasmād evaṃ pracakṣate ||
    1. pratyakṣadṛṣṭasambandhaṃ yayor eva viśeṣayoḥ |
    2. gomayendhanatajjanyaviśeṣādimatiḥ kṛtā ||
    1. taddeśasthena tenaiva gatvā kālāntare 'pi tam |
    2. yadāgnir budhyate, tasya pūrvabodhāt punaḥ punaḥ ||
    1. sandihyamānasadbhāvavastubodhāt pramāṇatā |
    2. viśeṣadṛṣṭam etac ca likhitaṃ vindhyavāsinā ||
    1. ākṛtyor eva caiṣeṣṭā vyavacchedena kena cit |
    2. hetusādhyavyavastheti viśeṣo nopadarśitaḥ ||
    1. agnidhūmāntaratve ca vācye sāmānyato mitau |
    2. sāmānyadṛṣṭam ekāntād atretyāditya ucyate ||
    1. pratyakṣaviṣayatvaṃ ca sāmānyasya prasādhitam |
    2. vastutvaṃ ca, atra hetur vā dvayasyāpy abhidhīyate ||
    1. dhūmād agnyanumānasya vastvālambanatā bhavet |
    2. abhāvānyapramāṇatvāt svārthe śrotrādibuddhivat ||
    1. sāmānyasya ca vastutvaṃ pratyakṣagrāhyatāpi ca |
    2. abhāvānyaprameyatvād asādhāraṇavastuvat ||
    1. sāmānyaṃ nānumānena vinā yasya pratīyate |
    2. na ca liṅgavinirmuktam anumānaṃ pravartate ||
    1. asāmānyasya liṅgatvaṃ na ca kena cid iṣyate |
    2. na cānavagataṃ liṅgaṃ kiñ cid asti prakāśakam ||
    1. tasya vāpy anumānena syād anyena gatiḥ punaḥ |
    2. tadutpattiś ca liṅgāt syāt sāmānyajñānasaṃhitāt ||
    1. tasya cāpy anumānatvāt bhavel liṅgena codbhavaḥ |
    2. anumānāntarād eva jñānenaivaṃ ca kalpane ||
    1. liṅgaliṅgyanumānānām ānantyād ekaliṅgini |
    2. gatir yugasahasreṣu bahuṣv api na vidyate ||
    1. atha sāmānyabhūte 'pi liṅge 'nyasmād gatir bhavet |
    2. pramāṇād apramāṇād vā, tathā liṅgigatir bhavet ||
    1. evam apy anumānasya nityocchedaḥ prasajyate |
    2. pramāṇāntaram eva syāt sāmānyasyāvabodhakam ||
    1. apramāṇāvabuddhād vā liṅgāl liṅgini yā matiḥ |
    2. sāpi mithyā bhaven nityaṃ bāṣpajātāgnibuddhivat ||
    1. nanv apramāṇabhūtāpi sambandhasmṛtir iṣyate |
    2. yathā liṅgigatau hetus tathā liṅgagatir bhavet ||
    1. tatra yat pūrvavijñānaṃ tasya prāmāṇyam iṣyate |
    2. tadupasthānamātreṇa smṛteḥ syāc caritārthatā ||
    1. na tu liṅgagatau kiñ cit pramāṇam upapadyate |
    2. tadabhāvāsmṛtiś cātra na kathañ cit pravartate ||
    1. smārtam etadabhedena vijñānam iti yo vadet |
    2. tasya vandhyāsute 'py asti nūnaṃ smaraṇaśaktatā ||
    1. na cāsādhāraṇo 'rthātmā sāmānyajñānakāraṇam |
    2. yasmān nāsyāvinābhāvas tena dṛṣṭaḥ kathañ cana ||
    1. syād vā sambandhadṛṣṭyāsau sāmānyaṃ kṛtakatvavat |
    2. na hy asādhāraṇaṃ vastu pūrvatreha ca vidyate ||
    1. na cāpy avyapadeśasya vikalparahitasya ca |
    2. vinā pūrvānusandhānāl liṅgatvam upapadyate ||
    1. kalpyante ca viśeṣā ye te 'py aliṅgam ananvayāt |
    2. etasmād eva hetoḥ syāt tajñānasyāpy aliṅgatā ||
    1. sāmānyarūpatāyāṃ vā tathaivānavadhāraṇam |
    2. kva cid vā dṛṣṭasambandhe sarvaḥ pratyāyako bhavet ||
    1. sambandhānubhavo 'vaśyam eṣitavyaś ca liṅganaḥ |
    2. anumānapravṛttes tu prāg jñānaṃ tatra nāsti te ||
    1. na cāpi vāsanāmātrāl liṅgajñānasya sambhavaḥ |
    2. liṅgijñānaṃ ca tadvat syāt trirūpāl liṅgato na tat ||
    1. tatrābhāvasya liṅgatvaṃ na cāsāv ānumānikaḥ |
    2. pramāṇāntaragamyatvāt tatra doṣo na jāyate ||
    1. pratyakṣāvagatāl liṅgād yasya liṅgigatir bhavet |
    2. tasya nāto 'dhikaṃ kiñ cit prārthanīyaṃ prasajyate ||
    1. yatrāpy anumitāl liṅgāl liṅgini grahaṇaṃ bhavet |
    2. tatrāpi maulikaṃ liṅgaṃ pratyakṣād eva gamyate ||
    1. liṅgatvaṃ kṛtakatvādau kriyāyāḥ kārakasya vā |
    2. pratyakṣatvaṃ ca tasyeṣṭam iti dūraṃ na gamyate ||
    1. evaṃ śabdopamānādau sāmānyāśrayatā yataḥ |
    2. taddaussthityena daussthityaṃ sarvatrātaḥ prasajyate ||
    1. tasmāt pratyakṣapūrvatvaṃ pramāṇāntara iṣyate |
    2. pratyakṣatvaṃ ca sāmānye nānyathā hi gatir bhavet ||
    1. pratyakṣālambanatvaṃ ca viśeṣasya kathaṃ bhavet |
    2. yadā vastvantarāpekṣaḥ sāmānyāṃśaḥ sa kīrtyate ||
    1. rūpādayo hi sāmānyaṃ sarve nīlādyapekṣayā |
    2. svaviśeṣānapekṣyātha nīlādīnāṃ samānatā ||
    1. te cāpi tāvat sāmānyaṃ yāvat syuḥ paramāṇavaḥ |
    2. dvyaṇukasyāpi yadrūpaṃ tad dhi sādhāraṇaṃ dvayoḥ ||
    1. na cāntyena viśeṣeṇa vyavahāro 'sti kasya cit |
    2. na ca pratyakṣatā tasya saṅghāte kevalasya vā ||
    1. bhedenāgṛhyamāṇasya nābhedo grāhyatāṃ vrajet |
    2. na ca bhinneṣv abhinnatvabuddher grāhyatvasambhavaḥ ||
    1. samudāyo na vāpy asti bhavatāṃ na ca sarvadā |
    2. sarveṣām asatārthena pratyayotpattisambhavaḥ ||
    1. na caikajātiyogena vināsti samudāyatā |
    2. samudāye 'pi cāṇutvaṃ naiteṣām apagacchati ||
    1. sāmānyam ity adṛśye 'pi tena sāmānya eva naḥ |
    2. vyāsaṅginī bhavaty eṣā dhīrvināpy ekakalpanāt ||
    1. vyāsajya vartamānasya sāmānyasya yathendriyaiḥ |
    2. grahaṇaṃ tadvad eva syāt prativyaktiniveśinaḥ ||
    1. mīmāṃsakaiś ca nāvaśyam iṣyante paramāṇavaḥ |
    2. yadbalenopalabdhasya mithyātvaṃ kalpayed bhavān ||
    1. samūharūpaṃ pratyakṣam adṛśyaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ |
    2. yo 'pahnute śaśasyāpi so 'bhāvaṃ śṛṅgato vadet ||
    1. samūhaparamārthatve sthite tatsiddhihetukā |
    2. yadi nāmāvagamyeta paramāṇvastitā punaḥ ||
    1. tasmād yad gṛhyate vastu yena rūpeṇa sarvadā |
    2. tat tathaivābhyupetavyaṃ sāmānyam atha vetarat ||
    1. sattādisāmānyam apekṣya sarvaṃ gotvādi sādhāraṇatām upaiti |
    2. tasmād asādhāraṇam akṣagamyaṃ vadan na sāmānyam apahnuvīta ||
    1. sāmānyarupeṇa na gṛhyate cet, kiṃ vāstyasādhāraṇabuddhir atra |
    2. yadvastu lokaḥ pratipadyate 'smin dvidhāpi tacchaktyata eva vaktum ||

{5,6 śabdapariccheda SBP}

    1. pratyakṣādiṣu vaktavyaṃ śabdamātrasya lakṣaṇam |
    2. adatitvariteneha kiṃ śāstrād abhidhīyate ||
    1. sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ tyaktvā viśeṣasyaiva lakṣaṇam |
    2. na śakyaṃ kevalaṃ vaktum ito 'py asya na vācyatā ||
    1. yac coktaṃ śabdavijñānād arthe jñānam itīdṛśamū |
    2. aviśiṣṭaṃ viśiṣṭasya na tacchāstrasya lakṣaṇam ||
    1. pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā nityena kṛtakena vā |
    2. puṃsāṃ yenopadiśyeta tacchāstram abhidhīyate ||
    1. svarūpakathanaṃ yat tu kasya cit tatra dṛśyate |
    2. tadaṅgatvena tasyāpi śāstratvam avagamyate ||
    1. bhāvanāyāṃ samastāyāṃ vākyād evopajāyate |
    2. pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā tacchāstraṃ na padād yataḥ ||
    1. aparīkṣāmiṣeṇāpi lakṣaṇāni vadannayam |
    2. na svatantropayogitvanirapekṣāṇi jalpati ||
    1. tatra yallokavākyasthaṃ kathayecchabdalakṣaṇam |
    2. vedaṃ vyākhyātukāmasya tannātīvopayujyate ||
    1. pratyakṣādyupayogaṃ tu varṇamātrāditaḥ puraḥ |
    2. śāstrārthajñānavelāyāṃ matvā tallakṣaṇaṃ kṛtam ||
    1. yat tu gāmānayetyādivākyasthaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam |
    2. tasya nehopayogo 'sti tasmāc chāstragataṃ kṛtam ||
    1. veśeṣaś ca na sāmānyam antareṇāsti kaś cana |
    2. tasmāt tam apy udāhṛtya sāmānyaṃ lakṣayet sukham ||
    1. sāmānyarūpam apy etadadhikārād viśiṣyate |
    2. codanā copadeśaś ca śāstram evety udāhṛtam ||
    1. yathā ca codanāśabdo vaidikyām eva vartate |
    2. śabdajñānārthavijñānaśabdau śāstre tathā sthitau ||
    1. pratyakṣādyaparīkṣyatve tadantarbhāvahetukam |
    2. śāstrasyāpy aparīkṣyatvamanayaiva dhiyoditam ||
    1. tatrānumānam evedaṃ bauddhair vaiśeṣikaiḥ śritam |
    2. bhedaḥ sāṃkhyādibhis tv iṣṭo na tūktaṃ bhedakāraṇam ||
    1. pūrvasaṃskārayuktāntyavarṇavākyādikalpanā |
    2. vivakṣādi ca dhūmādau nāstīty etena bhinnatā ||
    1. yair uktā tatra vaidharmyavikalpasamajātitā |
    2. dhūmānityaviṣāṇyādiviśeṣān na hi bhinnatā ||
    1. tailakṣaṇyaparityāgo yāvan na pratipādyate |
    2. tāvad viśeṣamātreṇa vadato jātitā bhavet ||
    1. yatheṣṭaviniyogena pratītir yāpi śabdataḥ |
    2. na dhūmāder itīhāpi vyabhicāro 'ṅgavṛttibhiḥ ||
    1. hastasaṃjñādayo ye 'pi yadarthapratipādane |
    2. bhaveyuḥ kṛtasaṅketāste na liṅgam iti sthitiḥ ||
    1. puruṣākṣiptatayāṃ ca tathaiva vyabhicāritā |
    2. padavaidikavākyānāṃ na satyavyāpitā bhavet ||
    1. sambandhātubhavaś cāyaṃ so 'nyatrāpi vilakṣaṇaḥ |
    2. etasmin puruṣāpekṣā deśāpekṣāgnidhūmayoḥ ||
    1. kālādyapekṣayā cānyaḥ, uktā cānyair abhinnatā |
    2. āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyād anumānataḥ ||
    1. na cāpūrvādiśabdānāṃ bhedāt sarvatra bhinnatā |
    2. na cehāśvādiśabdebhyo bhedas teṣāṃ pratīyate ||
    1. na cāpy ajñātasambandhaṃ padaṃ kiñ cit prakāśakam |
    2. sambandhān anubhūtyāto na syād ananumānatā ||
    1. tulyākāratayāpy atra śabdajñānārthataddhiyām |
    2. agnidhūmeṣv adṛṣṭatvān na bhedas tannivāraṇāt ||
    1. pratibimbeṣv anaikānto bimbaṃ yādṛgghi darpaṇe |
    2. tādṛṅ mukhādi budhyante, na cātrānanumānatā ||
    1. pratyakṣatā tadāpy atra tadānyair vyabhicāritā |
    2. yatra pādādi bambena gatānām anumīyate ||
    1. ekavākyāt sakṛc coktān nāpy anekasya tatkṣaṇam |
    2. syād viruddhāviruddhasya bodhād etasya bhinnātā ||
    1. liṅgasyāpi hi tādrūpyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hetuviruddhayoḥ |
    2. virodhān nānumānaṃ cet, syād anāgamatāpi te ||
    1. yatra caikārthatā vākye tatra syād anumānatā |
    2. sakṛduccarite cāsmin vivakṣaikaiva dṛśyate ||
    1. yas tv anirdhānaṃ ca dhūmādau vyabhicāritam |
    2. sa liṅge 'py asphuṭe dṛṣṭas tasmān naitena bhidyate ||
    1. dṛṣṭāntānabhidhānaṃ ca dhūmādau vyabhicāritam |
    2. prasiddhatvād dhi tatrāpi na dṛṣṭānto 'bhidhīyate ||
    1. anabhyas te tv apekṣante śabde sambandhinaḥ smṛtim |
    2. atra pratyukta ity evaṃ budhyante hi cirāt kva cit ||
    1. paroktā hetavaś cātra nābhedasya nivāritāḥ |
    2. śabdānumānayor aikyaṃ dhūmād agnyanumānavat ||
    1. anvayavyatirekābhyām ekapratyakṣadarśanāt |
    2. sambandhapūrvakatvāc ca pratipattir ito yataḥ ||
    1. pratyakṣānyapramāṇatvāt tadadṛṣṭārthabodhanāt |
    2. sāmānyaviṣayatvāc ca traikālyaviṣayāśrayāt ||
    1. kaiś cin mīmāṃsakair ukto bhedo 'tra viṣayāntarāt |
    2. pūrvābhyāṃ hy aparicchinne śāstram arthe pravartate ||
    1. tatrāpi nāgamatvaṃ syāt puruṣokte, tathās tu cet |
    2. pratyayaḥ kin nimitto 'rthe, vaktṛbuddheḥ, kuto nv asau ||
    1. na śabdārthasya sāliṅgaṃ na śabdo 'syāḥ kathañ cana |
    2. viśeṣo gamyate tābhyāṃ na caitasyānumeyatā ||
    1. tena vaktur abhiprāye pratyakṣādyanirūpite |
    2. puruṣoktir api śroturāgamatvaṃ prapadyate ||
    1. na cāpy ananumeyatvam āgamārthasya śakyate |
    2. liṅgaṃ hi śabda evāsya dhūmo 'gner iva kalpyate ||
    1. na cāpy ananumeyavāt pramāṇāntaragamyatā |
    2. rūpasyāśrāvaṇatvena na hy apratyakṣateṣyate ||
    1. evaṃ sati svayūthyā na ke cin nātiprapañcinaḥ |
    2. anumānaviśeṣo 'yam īdṛg dharmasya bodhakaḥ ||
    1. bhaviṣyatyartharūpaṃ tu liṅgaṃ dharme nirākṛtam |
    2. saṃjñānumānatecchā tu na duṣyedāgame 'pi naḥ ||
    1. lakṣaṇena tv abhinnatvaṃ yadi śabdānumānayoḥ |
    2. vedajñānāpramāṇatvaṃ syād atallakṣaṇatvataḥ ||
    1. āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyān nṛvacassu hi |
    2. lakṣaṇenānumānatvāt prāmāṇyaṃ siddhimṛcchati ||
    1. vede tv āptanarābhāvāt sambandhānubhavād ṛte |
    2. lakṣaṇaṃ nānumānasyety aprāmāṇyaṃ prasajyate ||
    1. nanv ekadeśasatyatve tasya syād anumānatā |
    2. vedatvād agnihotrādau vāyukṣepiṣṭhavākyavat ||
    1. nādityayūpe 'naikāntāt, tadvad vā gauṇatā bhavet |
    2. nātaḥ pratyanumānānām evaṃ pūrvoktayā viśā ||
    1. tasmāl lakṣaṇabhedena yadi śabdapramāṇatā |
    2. samā loke ca vede ca siddhā vedapramāṇatā ||
    1. tena cāptopadeśatvaṃ na syād āgamalakṣaṇam |
    2. nāptasya sambhavo vede, loke nāsmāt pramāṇatā ||
    1. purastād varṇitaṃ hy etat, tsmāc chabdena yā matiḥ |
    2. tasyāḥ svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ na cet syād doṣadarśanam ||
    1. anumānena caitasya prāmāṇyaṃ kevalaṃ samam |
    2. pade tāvat kṛto yatnaḥ parair ity atra varṇyate ||
    1. viṣayo 'nyādṛśas tāvad dṛśyate liṅgaśabdayoḥ |
    2. sāmānyaviṣayatvaṃ ca padasya sthāpayiṣyati ||
    1. dharmādharmaviśiṣṭaś ca liṅgīty etac ca sādhitam |
    2. na tāvad anumānaṃ hi yāvat tadviṣayaṃ na tat ||
    1. sāmānyād atiriktaṃ tu śābde vākyasya gocaraḥ |
    2. sāmarthyād anumeyatvād aśrute 'pi padāntare ||
    1. saṃkhyādimān padārthaś cet, na tāvat so 'vyayādiṣu |
    2. yatrāpi te pratīyante tatra vyakter viśeṣaṇam ||
    1. padāntarābhidheyasya tādarthyāc ca kriyātmanaḥ |
    2. vākyārthe 'pi padaṃ yatra gomadādi prayujyate ||
    1. saty apy atra viśeṣṭatve siddhatvān naiva pakṣatā |
    2. tāvān eva hi tatrārtho yaḥ pūrvam avadhāritaḥ ||
    1. bhedabuddheś ca vaiṣamyaṃ prakṛtipratyayārthayoḥ |
    2. viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyārthasvātantryagrahaṇaṃ na ca ||
    1. viśeṣyapūrvikā tatra buddhiś cātra viparyayaḥ |
    2. atha śabdo 'rthavattvena pakṣaḥ kasmān na kalpyate ||
    1. pratijñārthaikadeśo hi hetus tatra prasajyate |
    2. pakṣe dhūmaviśeṣe ca sāmānyaṃ hetur iṣyate ||
    1. śabdatvaṃ gamakaṃ nātra gośabdatvaṃ niṣetsyate |
    2. vyaktir eva viśiṣyāto hetuś caikā prasajyate ||
    1. bhaved vyañjakabhedāc cet, na tv evaṃ pratyayo 'sti naḥ |
    2. kathaṃ cāsya viśiṣṭatvaṃ na tāvad deśakālataḥ ||
    1. tatpratītiviśiṣṭaś cet, paraṃ kim anumīyate |
    2. na pratyāyanaśaktiś ca viśeṣasyānumīyate ||
    1. viśeṣāṇāṃ na śaktir hi saikadeśe 'gnijātivat |
    2. sāmānyasyaiva śaktatvaṃ pakṣo hetus tad eva ca ||
    1. tasmād arthaviśiṣṭasya na śabdasyānumeyatā |
    2. kathaṃ ca pakṣadharmatvaṃ śabdasyeha nirūpyate ||
    1. na kriyākartṛsambandhād ṛte sambandhanaṃ kva cit |
    2. rājā bharttā manuṣyasya tena rājñaḥ sa ucyate ||
    1. vṛkṣas tiṣṭhati śākhāsu tā vā tatreti tasya tāḥ |
    2. deśe 'gnimati dhūmasya kartṛtvaṃ bhavanaṃ prati ||
    1. kāryakāraṇabhāvādau kriyā sarvatra vidyate |
    2. na cānavagatākāraḥ sambandho 'stīti gamyate ||
    1. na cāsty asati sambandhe ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣo 'pi vā |
    2. tasmān na pakṣadharmo 'yam iti śakyā nirūpaṇā ||
    1. nivṛtte 'nyatra sambandhe ye 'pi tadviṣayātmanā |
    2. vadeyuḥ pakṣadharmatvaṃ śabdasyānupalabdhivat ||
    1. tair apy etannirūpyaṃ tu śabdas tadviṣayaḥ katham |
    2. na taddeśādisadbhāvo nābhimukhyādi tasya vā ||
    1. tasmād utpādayaty eṣa yato 'rthaviṣayā matim |
    2. tena tadviṣayaḥ śabda iti dharmatvakalpanā ||
    1. tatra vācakatāyāṃ ca siddhāyāṃ pakṣadharmatā |
    2. na pratītyaṅgatāṃ gacchen na caivam anumānatā ||
    1. gamakatāc ca dharmatvaṃ dharmatvād gamako yadi |
    2. syād anyonyāśrayatvaṃ hi tasmān naiṣāpi kalpanā ||
    1. na cāgṛhītasambandhāḥ svarūpavyatirekataḥ |
    2. śabdaṃ jānanti yenātra pakṣadharmamatir bhavet ||
    1. na ca svarūpamātreṇa dhūmādeḥ pakṣadharmatā |
    2. na cāpi pūrvasambandham apekṣyaiṣā prasajyate ||
    1. dhūmavān ayam ity evam apūrvasyāpi jāyate |
    2. pakṣadharmamatiḥ, tena bhidyetottaralakṣaṇāt ||
    1. na tv atra pūrvasambandhād adhikā pakṣadharmatā |
    2. na cārthapratyayāt pūrvam ity anaṅgam iyaṃ bhavet ||
    1. na ca dharmī gṛhīto 'tra yena taddharmatā bhavet |
    2. parvatādir yathā deśaḥ prāgdharmatvāvadhāraṇāt ||
    1. yaś cātra kathyate dharmī prameyo 'sya sa eva naḥ |
    2. na cānavadhṛte tasmiṃs taddharmatvāvadhāraṇam ||
    1. prāk sa cet pakṣadharmatvād gṛhītaḥ kiṃ tataḥ param |
    2. paṣadharmādibhir jñātair yena syād anumānitā ||
    1. anvayo na ca śabdasya prameyeṇa nirūpyate |
    2. vyāpāreṇa hi sarveṣām anvitatvaṃ pratīyate ||
    1. yatra dhūmo 'sti tatrāgner astitvenānvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ |
    2. na tv evaṃ yatra śabdo 'sti tatrārtho 'stīti niścayaḥ ||
    1. na tāvat tatra deśe 'sau tatkāle vāvagamyate |
    2. bhaven nityavibhutvāc cet, sarvārtheṣu ca tat samam ||
    1. tena sarvatra dṛṣṭatvād vyatirekasya cāgateḥ |
    2. sarvaśabdair aśeṣārthapratipattiḥ prasajyate ||
