    1. athaivaṃ deśakālābhyām asatyatvaprakalpane |
    2. vācakapratyayaṃ kaś cid brūyād arthadhiyānvitam ||
    1. naivam apy asti dṛṣṭo hi vināpy arthadhiyā kva cit |
    2. vācakapratyayo 'smābhir avyutpannanarān prati ||
    1. dvitīyādiprayoge ca bhaved anvayakalpanā |
    2. śatakṛtvaḥ prayukte 'pi na ca dṛṣṭārthadhīḥ kva cit ||
    1. nanu ye jñātasambandhās teṣāṃ dṛṣṭo 'nvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ |
    2. yady evam anvayāt pūrvaṃ sambandhaḥ ko 'pi kalpitaḥ ||
    1. nāṅgam arthadhiyām eṣā bhaved anvayakalpanā |
    2. anvayādhīnajanmatvam anumānasya ca sthitam ||
    1. jñāte pratītisāmarthye tadvaśād eva jāyate |
    2. paścād anvaya ity eṣa kāraṇaṃ katham ucyate ||
    1. tasmāt tannirapekṣaiva śabdaśaktiḥ pratīyate |
    2. na ca dhūmānvayāt pūrvaṃ śaktatvam avagamyate ||
    1. vyatireko 'py avijñātād arthāc chabdadhiyau yadi |
    2. so 'pi paścāt sthitatvena nārthapratyayasādhanam ||
    1. sambandhaṃ yaṃ tu vakṣyāmastasya nirṇayakāraṇam |
    2. syād anvayo 'tirekaś ca na tv arthādhigamasya tau ||
    1. tasmād ananumānatvaṃ cābde pratyakṣavad bhavet |
    2. trairūpyarahitatvena tādṛgviṣayavarjanāt ||
    1. sati cāsya pramāṇatve bhedābhedanirūpanā |
    2. yuktā na tu padajñānāt padārtho 'tra pramīyate ||
    1. padaṃ prayujyamānaṃ hi caturddhārthe prayujyate |
    2. pratyakṣe ca parokṣe ca jñāte 'jñāte 'pi vā purā ||
    1. tatra yat pūrvavijñāte pratyakṣe ca prayujyate |
    2. pramite ca prayuktatvād anuvādo 'dhikād vinā ||
    1. adṛṣṭapūrve tv ajñānaṃ sambandhapratyayo 'pi vā |
    2. sambandho na ca tasyārthaḥ, yo 'rthaḥ sa tv anyagocaraḥ ||
    1. parokṣe 'nanubhūte ca nābhidheye matir bhavet |
    2. parokṣaś cānubhūtaś ca yas tatra smṛtir iṣyate ||
    1. pramite ca pravṛttatvāt smṛter nāsti pramāṇatā |
    2. paricchedaphalatvād dhi prāmāṇyam upajāyate ||
    1. tādātvikaparicchedaphalatvena pramāṇatā |
    2. pratyabhijñānavat kasmāt smṛter api na kalpyate ||
    1. yāvān pūrvaparicchinnas tāvān evāvadhāryate |
    2. smṛtyā tadanusāreṇa tadāsattve 'sya naiva dhīḥ ||
    1. padam abhyadhikābhāvāt smārakān na viśiṣyate |
    2. padādhikyaṃ bhavet kiñ cit tatpadasya na gocaraḥ ||
    1. prāṇam anumānaṃ vā yady api syāt padānmitiḥ |
    2. vākyārthasyāgamārthatvād doṣo nāgamavādinām ||
    1. vākyārthe tu padārthebhyaḥ sambandhānubhavād ṛte |
    2. buddhir utpadyate tena bhinnā 'sāvakṣabuddhivat ||
    1. vākyādhikaraṇe cāsya hetoḥ siddhir bhaviṣyati |
    2. sarveṣāṃ ca paroktānāṃ vākyabuddhāvasiddhatā ||
    1. vākyeṣv adṛṣṭeṣv api sārthakeṣu padārthavinmātratayā pratītim |
    2. dṛṣṭvānumānavyatirekabhītāḥ kliṣṭāḥ padābhedavicāraṇāyām ||

{5,7 upamānapariccheda UMP}

    1. kīdṛggavaya ityevaṃ pṛṣṭo nāgarikair yadi |
    2. bravītyāraṇyako vākyaṃ yathā gaur gavayas tathā ||
    1. etasminn upamānatvaṃ prasiddhaṃ śabare punaḥ |
    2. tasyāgamābahirbhāvād anyathaivopavarṇitam ||
    1. puruṣapratyayenaiva tatrārthaḥ sampratīyate |
    2. tadīyavacanatvena tasmād āgama eva saḥ ||
    1. sadṛśād upajāyeta yā matiḥ sadṛśāntare |
    2. dhyānādismṛtitulyatvāt sā pramāṇaṃ kathaṃ bhavet ||
    1. deśakālādibhedena yathānyatra viśiṣyate |
    2. prameyaṃ naivam asty atra nagarasthānusārataḥ ||
    1. śrutātideśavākyānām āraṇye gavaye matiḥ |
    2. yā sopamānaṃ keṣāñ cid gosādṛśyānurañjitā ||
    1. pratyakṣo gavayas tāvat sādṛśyasmṛtir atra tu |
    2. nanu sādṛśyayukte 'rthe na smṛtir nendriyād gatiḥ ||
    1. pūrvavākyārthavijñānān nādhikyaṃ gavaye yadi |
    2. smaraṇād aviśiṣṭatvāt saṅgater na pramāṇatā ||
    1. atha tv adhikatā kā cit pratyakṣādivaśād bhavet |
    2. yāvaddhīndriyasambandhas tat pratyakṣam iti sthitam ||
    1. syaryamāṇasya cāṃśasya vivedenāpramāṇatā |
    2. śrutātideśavākyatvaṃ na cātīvopayujyate ||
    1. ye 'pi hy aśrutatadvākyās teṣām api bhavaty ayam |
    2. pratyakṣadṛṣṭagotvānāṃ vane gavayadarśinām ||
    1. atha saṃjñānusandhānaṃ teṣāṃ nāstīti varṇyate |
    2. na nāma vastu tat tāvat sarvathā taiḥ pratīyate ||
    1. na ca śabdārthasambandhaḥ prameyo 'tra tadeṣyate |
    2. sādṛśyāvadhṛte vākye vākyād avagato hy asau ||
    1. na cāsya pratyabhijñānaṃ punarutpadyate vane |
    2. śaktyor atīndriyatvena smṛtir eva hi seṣyate ||
    1. śabdānuviddhabodhe 'pi pratyakṣam upapāditam |
    2. tasmāt sādṛśyayuktārthaḥ prameyo 'pūrva ucyatām ||
    1. vyavasāyātmakatvaṃ tu pratyakṣasya yadeṣyate |
    2. jātyādivat tadā tena sādṛśyaṃ kiṃ na mīyate ||
    1. pratyakṣābhāsam etat tu nirvikalpakavādinām |
    2. prameyavastvabhāvāc ca nābhipretā pramāṇatā ||
    1. sādṛśyasyāpi vastutvaṃ na śakyam apabādhitum |
    2. bhūyo 'vayavasāmānyayogo jātyantarasya tat ||
    1. sadṛśāvayavatvaṃ tu yatra padmadalākṣivat |
    2. tat svāvayavasāmānyabhūmnā teṣā bhaviṣyati ||
    1. evaṃ jātiguṇadravyakriyāśaktisvadharmataḥ |
    2. ekaikadvitrisāmastyabhedād etasya citratā ||
    1. na dharmā eva sādṛśyaṃ bhūyastā vā tadāśrayā |
    2. bhūyastvavaddhi jātyādi sadṛśatvena dṛśyate ||
    1. yamayoḥ katham etac ced, dṛṣṭatvāt kim ihocyate |
    2. kva cid dhi bhūyasām etat kva cid alpīyasām api ||
    1. naitāvatā viśeṣeṇa vastutvaṃ tasya hīyate |
    2. sāmānyāny api caitāni nāśīnyāśrayanāśataḥ ||
    1. anantāśrayayogāc ca na nāśo 'nyatra vidyate |
    2. tena sarvaṃ na sāmānyaṃ nityatvena prakalpyate ||
    1. sāmānyānāṃ na vā nāśaḥ kva cid abhyupagamyate |
    2. sarvasya hy āśrayaḥ kaś cid asti deśāntarādiṣu ||
    1. teṣāṃ bhūyas tayā cedaṃ sādṛśyam atiricyate |
    2. tāni vyastāni santy evaṃ pratyakṣe 'pi kva cit kva cit ||
    1. sadṛśāvayavatvaṃ tu yatra nāma pratīyate |
    2. tad apy avayavānāṃ syāt samānavayavāntaraiḥ ||
    1. evaṃ tāvad yato nāsti parābhedaprakalpanā |
    2. tataḥ paraṃ tu sāmānyaṃ bhavet sādṛśyavarjitam ||
    1. pradhānānāṃ tu sāmānyaṃ yatraikaṃ sampratīyate |
    2. sa eveti bhavet tatra tadbhede sadṛśatvadhīḥ ||
    1. citrādau yatra sādṛśyaṃ sāmānyaṃ tatra kiṃ bhavet |
    2. tatrāpi pṛthivīvarṇaviśeṣādisamānatā ||
    1. rūpagandharasānāṃ ca kasya cit tulyatā kva cit |
    2. nāvaśyaṃ sarvasāmānyāt sādṛśyam upajāyate ||
    1. pṛthivyādiṣu caiteṣāṃ satām eva svabhāvataḥ |
    2. pariṇāmādibhir vyaktir yathādṛṣṭyavadhāryate ||
    1. na hi śaktyātmanā kiñ cid asajjama prapadyate |
    2. dharmāṇāṃ na ca nānātvam, asti cāvāntararasthitiḥ ||
    1. vastutve sati cāsyaivaṃ sambandhasya ca cakṣuṣā |
    2. dvayor ekatra vā dṛṣṭeḥ pratyakṣatvaṃ na vāryate ||
    1. sāmānyavac ca sādṛśyam ekaikatra samāpte |
    2. pratiyoginyadṛṣṭe 'pi tasmāt tadupapadyate ||
    1. tatra yady api gāṃ smṛtvā tadbhānam upajāyate |
    2. sannidhergavayasthatvād bhaved indriyagocaraḥ ||
    1. tasmād yat smaryate tat syāt sādṛśyena viśeṣitam |
    2. prameyam upamānasya sādṛśyaṃ vā tadanvatam ||
    1. pratyakṣeṇāvabuddhe 'pi sādṛśye gavi ca smṛteḥ |
    2. viśiṣṭasyānyato 'siddher upamānanapramāṇatā ||
    1. pratyakṣe 'pi yathā deśe smaryamāṇe ca pāvake |
    2. viśiṣṭaviṣayatvena nānumānāpramāṇatā ||
    1. yatra tv asadṛśād eva kalpayitvopajāyate |
    2. sādṛśyapratyayas tatra tadābhāsatvakalpanā ||
    1. bādhakapratyayāc caiṣā sādṛśyābhāsatā matā |
    2. yathā palālakūṭasya sādṛśyaṃ kuñjarādinā ||
    1. samīpastho 'pi jānāti sādṛśyaṃ neti tatra hi |
    2. na bādhyate samīpādau yat tu sādṛśyam eva tat ||
    1. na caitasyānumānatvaṃ pakṣadharmādyasambhavāt |
    2. prāk prameyasya sādṛśyaṃ na dharmatvena gṛhyate ||
    1. gavaye gṛhyamāṇaṃ ca na gavām anumāpakam |
    2. pratijñārthaikadeśatvād gogatasya na liṅgatā ||
    1. gavayaś cāpy asambandhān na gor liṅgatvamṛcchati |
    2. sādṛśyaṃ na ca sarveṇa pūrvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tadanvayi ||
    1. ekasminn api dṛṣṭe 'rthe dvitīyaṃ paśyato vane |
    2. sādṛśyena sahaivāsmiṃs tadaivotpadyate matiḥ ||
    1. śṛṅgitvāder athocyeta sambandhāl liṅgatā gavi |
    2. na, teṣāṃ gavayajñānavyāpāraṃ pratyupakṣayāt ||
    1. yadi tebhyaḥ pratītiḥ syān niḥsādṛśyaiva sā bhavet |
    2. na gauḥ śṛṅgādisadṛśī sadṛśī gavayena tu ||
    1. sadṛśapratyayaṃ dṛṣṭvā śṛṅgādipratyayāt param |
    2. gavayapratyayād eva gojñānam upajāyate ||
    1. sadṛśāvayavatve tu teṣām evopamā bhavet |
    2. na ca śṛṅgādayo yatra tatra gaur anumīyate ||
    1. itthaṃ cānumimānasya bhrāntajñānaṃ prasajyate |
    2. nagarasthe tu gojñānaṃ smaraṇān nātivartate ||
    1. bhinnānumānād upameyam uktam, sauryādivākyair asahāyi dṛṣṭam |
    2. sādṛśyato 'gnyādiyutaṃ kathaṃ nu, pratyāyayed ity upayujyate naḥ ||
    1. pratinidhir api caivaṃ vrīhisādṛśyayogād bhavati tadapacāre yatra nīvārajātau |
    2. tad api phalam abhīṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇasyopamāyāḥ pratikṛtir api gauṇair bodhyate yatra cānyaiḥ ||
    1. matir api ca tathaiva drāgivotpadyate 'sminn |
    2. itaraviṣayabodhe 'saty apītthaṃ ca bādhaḥ ||

{5,8 arthāpattipariccheda AAP}

    1. pramāṇaṣaṭkavijñāto yatrārtho nānyathā bhavet |
    2. adṛṣṭaṃ kalpayed anyaṃ sārthāpattir udāhṛtā ||
    1. dṛṣṭaḥ pañcabhir apy asmād bhedenoktā śrutodbhavā |
    2. pramāṇagrāhiṇītvena yasmāt pūrvavilakṣaṇā ||
    1. tatra pratyakṣato jñānād dāhād dahanaśaktatā |
    2. vahner anumitāt sūrye yānāt tacchaktiyogyatā ||
    1. śrutārthāpattir atraiva parastād abhidhāsyate |
    2. gavayopamitā yā gaus tajjñānagrāhyatā matā ||
    1. abhidhānaprasiddhyartham arthāpattyāvabodhitāt |
    2. śabde bodhakasāmarthyāt tannityatvaprakalpanam ||
    1. abhidhā nānyathā sidhyed iti vācakaśaktatām |
    2. arthāpattyāvagamyaivaṃ tadananyagateḥ punaḥ ||
    1. arthāpattyantareṇaiva śabdanityatvaniścayaḥ |
    2. darśanasya parārthatvād ity asminn abhidhāsyate ||
    1. pramāṇābhāvanirṇītacaitrābhāvaviśeṣitāt |
    2. gehāc caitrabahirbhāvasiddhir yā tv iha darśitā ||
    1. tām abhāvotthitām anyām arthāpattim udāharet |
    2. pakṣadoṣeṣu cānyāsāmudāharaṇavistaraḥ ||
    1. abhāvāvagatāc caitrād bahirbhāvasya sūcanam |
    2. pakṣadharmādyanaṅgatvād bhinnaivāpy anumānataḥ ||
    1. bahirdeśaviśiṣṭe 'rthe deśe vā tadviśeṣite |
    2. prameye yo gṛhābhāvaḥ pakṣadharmas tv asau katham ||
    1. tadabhāvaviśiṣṭaṃ tu gṛhaṃ dharmo na kasyacit |
    2. gṛhābhāvaviśiṣṭas tu tadāsau na pratīyate ||
    1. gamyate tu gṛhaṃ tatra na ca caitraḥ pratīyate |
    2. na cātrādarśanaṃ hetur yathābhāve 'bhidhāsyate ||
    1. tena veśmanyadṛṣṭatvād iti hetur na kalpyate |
    2. adarśanād abhāve ca prameyasyāvadhārite ||
    1. bahirbhāvamatir nāsau tenādarśanahetukā |
    2. caitrābhāvasya hetutvaṃ gehe 'bhāvaś ca saṃsthitaḥ ||
    1. pūrvaṃ na cāgṛhītasya dharmiṇaḥ syāt prameyatā |
    2. na cātra bāhyadeśo vā caitro vā gṛhyate purā ||
    1. nadīpūreṇa yā vṛṣṭir upariṣṭāt pratīyate |
    2. deśe katham adṛṣṭe tu pakṣadharmatvasambhavaḥ ||
    1. vṛṣṭimatparadeśatvaṃ nadīpuravato 'tra tu |
    2. deśasya pratipadyante yadvārthāpattir eva sā ||
    1. jīvataś ca gṛhābhāvaḥ pakṣadharmo 'tra kalpyate |
    2. tatsaṃvittir bahirbhāvaṃ na cābuddhvopajāyate ||
    1. agnimattānapekṣā tu dhūmavattā pratīyate |
    2. na tadgrahaṇavelāyām agnyadhīnaṃ hi kiñcana ||
    1. gehābhāvas tu yaḥ śuddho vidyamānatvavarjitaḥ |
    2. sa mṛteṣv api dṛṣṭatvād bahirvṛtter na sādhakaḥ ||
    1. vidyamānatvasaṃsṛṣṭagṛhābhāvadhiyānayā |
    2. gehād utkālitaś caitro vidyate bahir eva hi ||
    1. gehābhāvatvamātraṃ tu yat svatantraṃ pratīyate |
    2. na tāvatā bahirbhāvaś caitrasyaivāvadhāryate ||
    1. siddhe sadbhāvavijñāne gehābhāvadhiyātra tu |
    2. gehād utkālitā sattā bahir evāvatiṣṭhate ||
    1. tenāsya nirapekṣasya vyabhicāro mṛtādinā |
    2. yasya tv avyabhicāritvaṃ na tato 'nyat pratīyate ||
    1. tasmāt pratyakṣato gehe caitrābhāve hy abhāvataḥ |
    2. jñāte yat sattvavijñānaṃ tad evedaṃ bahiḥ sthitam ||
    1. pakṣadharmātmalābhāya bahirbhāvaḥ praveśitaḥ |
    2. tadviśiṣṭo 'numeyaḥ syāt pakṣadharmānvayādibhiḥ ||
    1. pakṣadharmādivijñānaṃ bahiḥ sambodhato yadi |
    2. taiś ca tadbodhato 'vaśyam anyonyāśrayatā bhavet ||
    1. anyathānupapattau tu prameyānupraveśitā |
    2. tādrūpyeṇaiva vijñānān na doṣaḥ pratibhāti naḥ ||
    1. avinābhāvitā cātra tadaiva parikalpyate |
    2. na prāg avadhṛtety evaṃ saty apy eṣā na kāraṇam ||
    1. gṛhābhāvabahirbhāvau na ca dṛṣṭau niyogataḥ |
    2. sāhitye 'pi pramāṇaṃ ca tayor anyan na vidyate ||
    1. anyathānupapattyaiva hy ekenānyat pratīyate |
    2. tathā na kalpyate tac cet sāhityaṃ na pratīyate ||
    1. tena sambandhavelāyāṃ sambandhyanyataro dhruvam |
    2. arthāpattyāvagantavyaḥ paścād asty anumānatā ||
    1. gṛhadvāri sthito yas tu bahirbhāvaṃ prakalpayet |
    2. yadaikasminn ayaṃ deśe na tadānyatra vidyate ||
    1. tadāpy avidyamānatvaṃ na sarvatra pratīyate |
    2. na caikadeśe nāstitvād vyāptir hetor bhaviṣyati ||
    1. nanv atrāvidyamānatvaṃ gamyate 'nupalabdhitaḥ |
    2. sā cāprayatnasādhyatvād ekasthasyaiva sidhyati ||
    1. naitayānupalabdhyātra vastvabhāvaḥ pratīyate |
    2. taddeśāgamanāt sā hi dūrastheṣv asti satsv api ||
    1. gatvā gatvā tu tān deśān yady artho nopalabhyate |
    2. tato 'nyakāraṇābhāvād asann ity avagamyate ||
    1. nanu cāgnyādyabhāve 'pi dhūmādivyatirekiṇām |
    2. taddeśāgamanāt spaṣṭo vyatireko na sidhyati ||
    1. yasya vastvantarābhāvaḥ prameyas tasya duṣyati |
    2. mama tv adṛṣṭamātreṇa gamakaḥ sahacāriṇaḥ ||
    1. nanv evam itaratrāpi sambandho 'nupalabdhitaḥ |
    2. caitrābhāvasya bhāvena dṛṣṭatvād upapadyate ||
    1. sāhitye mitadeśatvāt prasiddhe cāgnidhūmayoḥ |
    2. vyatirekasya cādṛṣṭer gamakatvaṃ prakalpyate ||
    1. iha sāhityam evedam ekasya sahabhāvinaḥ |
    2. anantadeśavarttitvān na tāvad upapadyate ||
    1. nanu deśāntaraṃ śūnyaṃ caitreṇaivaṃ pratīyate |
    2. taddeśavyatiriktatvāt samīpasthitadeśavat ||
    1. viruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ tadvad eva hi gamyate |
    2. samīpadeśabhinnatvāt caitrādhiṣṭhitadeśavat ||
    1. puruṣasya tu kārtsnyena yad ekatropalambhanam |
    2. tasyānyathā na siddhiḥ syād ity anyeṣv asya nāstitā ||
    1. tenārthāpattipūrvatvam atra yatra ca kāraṇe |
    2. kāryādarśanataḥ śakter astitvaṃ sampratīyate ||
    1. kāryasya nanu liṅgatvaṃ na sambandhānapekṣaṇāt |
    2. dṛṣṭvā sambandhitāṃ caiṣā śaktir gamyeta nānyathā ||
    1. taddarśane tadānīṃ ca pratyakṣāder asambhavāt |
    2. arthāpatteḥ pramāṇatvaṃ trailakṣaṇyād vinā bhavet ||
    1. anumānād abhinnatvān noktau jayaparājayau |
    2. vadhyaghātakabhāvena yau sarpanakulādiṣu ||
    1. pīno divā na bhuṅkte cety evamādivacaḥ śrutau |
    2. rātribhojanavijñānaṃ śrutārthāpattir ucyate ||
    1. tām arthagocarāṃ kecid apare śabdagocarām |
    2. kalpayanty āgamāc cainām abhinnāṃ pratijānate ||
    1. prāyaśaś cānayā vede vyavahāro vyavasthitaḥ |
    2. so 'vaidikaḥ prasajyeta yady eṣā bhidyate tataḥ ||
    1. vacanasya śrutasyaiva so 'py arthaḥ kaiścid āśritaḥ |
    2. tadarthopaplutasyānyair iṣṭo vākyāntarasya tu ||
    1. na tāvac chrūyamāṇasya vacaso 'rtho 'yam iṣyate |
    2. na hy anekārthatā yuktā vākye vācakatā tathā ||
    1. padārthānvayarūpeṇa vākyārtho hi pratīyate |
    2. na rātryādipadārthaś ca divāvākyena gamyate ||
    1. na divādipadārthānāṃ saṃsargo rātribhojanam |
    2. na bhedo yena tadvākyaṃ tasya syāt pratipādakam ||
    1. anyārthavyāpṛtatvāc ca na dvitīyārthakalpanā |
    2. tasmād vākyāntareṇāyaṃ buddhisthena pratīyate ||
    1. tasya cāgamikatve 'pi yat tad vākyaṃ pratīyate |
    2. pramāṇaṃ tasya vaktavyaṃ pratyakṣādiṣu yad bhavet ||
    1. na hy anuccārite vākye pratyakṣaṃ tāvad iṣyate |
    2. nānumānaṃ na cedaṃ hi dṛṣṭaṃ tena saha kvacit ||
    1. yadi tv anupalabdhe 'pi sambandhe liṅgateṣyate |
    2. taduccāraṇamātreṇa sarvavākyamatir bhavet ||
    1. na cārthāpattigamyāni sarvaiḥ sarvavacāṃsi hi |
    2. sambaddhāny upalabdhāni yena teṣv anumā bhavet ||
    1. na ca sattānumānena viśeṣo vānumīyate |
    2. iha vākyaviśeṣasya sattaiva tv avagamyate ||
    1. pūrvasiddhaḥ svatantro 'rthaḥ svatantreṇa viśeṣitaḥ |
    2. dharmādharmaviśiṣṭo 'tra nānumeyaḥ pratīyate ||
    1. atha śrutasya vākyasya mīyate tadviśiṣṭatā |
    2. tataḥ pakṣo 'bhyupetaḥ syād aprasiddhaviśeṣaṇaḥ ||
    1. kiñ ca liṅgāntarābhāvād etasya yadi liṅgatā |
    2. pratijñārthaikadeśatvaṃ padavat te prasajyate ||
    1. tadvad eva nirākāryā vacaso dharmadharmitā |
    2. nāgṛhīte hi taddharmo gṛhīte nānumeyatā ||
    1. kriyākārakasambandhād ṛte nāsti tu dharmatā |
    2. avācakatayā caitan na dharmo viṣayātmanā ||
    1. pratīter vācakatvaṃ cet prasaktānekaśaktitā |
    2. anumāviṣayotthaṃ tu dharmatvaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet ||
    1. padārthair api tadvākyaṃ nāsambandhāt pratīyate |
    2. sāmānyānyanyathāsiddher viśeṣaṃ gamayanti hi ||
    1. na tu vākyāntareṇaiṣāṃ vinā kiñcin na sidhyati |
    2. na cāpy anyaḥ prakāro 'sti tena vākyena saṅgatau ||
    1. athaitad vāci kalpyeta vākyam anyat tathaiva ca |
    2. prasaṅgāt tatra dūre 'pi nāsambandhāt pramucyate ||
    1. tataś ca prathamād eva varaṃ jñātum asaṅgatāt |
    2. anvayavyatirekau ca pratiṣedhyau pade yathā ||
    1. śrutavākyena sādṛśyaṃ nāśrutasyāsti kiñcana |
    2. tasmād anupamānatvam arthasyāpy anayā diśā ||
    1. upamānatvaliṅgatve vākyaṃ prati nivārite |
    2. arthe 'pi caivam eva syāt, tasmāt pūrveṣv asambhavaḥ ||
    1. ataḥ śrutasya vākyasya yad arthapratipādanam |
    2. tadātmalābha eva syād vinā nety etad iṣyate ||
    1. etadarthād vinā nāyam ity arthaḥ kiṃ na kalpyate |
    2. vākyārthavac ca kiṃ nāyam āgamārthaḥ pratīyate ||
    1. savikalpakavijñānaiḥ śabdaḥ pūrvaṃ pratīyate |
    2. labdhaprayojane vākye paraṃ nāgamikaṃ ca naḥ ||
    1. nanu cāsati sambandhe sati vānavadhārite |
    2. gamyajñānam idaṃ vākyaṃ prasajyetāpramāṇakam ||
    1. sambandhasya pramāṇatvaṃ sthitaṃ kiñceśvarājñayā |
    2. pratyakṣasya pramāṇatvaṃ kathaṃ vā saṅgater vinā ||
    1. astīndriyārthasambandhas tatra cen nānapekṣaṇāt |
    2. na hi pratyakṣavelāyāṃ sarveṇāsau nirūpyate ||
    1. yenāpi tu nirūpyeta paścād anubhavād asau |
    2. na syād eva pramāṇāṅgam asatā tulya eva saḥ ||
    1. aprāpyakāriṇī yeṣāṃ cakṣuḥśrotre ca te yathā |
    2. tajjñānasya pramāṇatvam icchanty evaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
    1. tasmād asattve sattve vā sambandhasya yad eva naḥ |
    2. jāyetābhaṅguraṃ jñānaṃ tasyaiva syāt pramāṇatā ||
    1. na cāpy asyāḥ pramāṇatve kaścid vipratipadyate |
    2. bhedābhede visaṃvādaḥ kṛtas tatra ca nirṇayaḥ ||
    1. kṛte yatra ca sambandhād buddhir eva na jāyate |
    2. tatra ki kriyatāṃ so 'pi prāmāṇye naiva kāraṇam ||
    1. smṛtyā śrutir yā parikalpyate 'smin liṅgādibhir yā viniyojikā ca |
    2. phalādibhir yat paripūraṇaṃ ca sambandhadṛk tatra na kācid asti ||
    1. tat sarvam ityādy asamañjasaṃ syān na cediyaṃ syād anumānato 'nyā |
    2. evaṃsvabhāvāpy anumānaśabdaṃ labheta ced asti yathepsitaṃ naḥ ||

{5,9 abhāvapariccheda ABH}

    1. pramāṇapañcakaṃ yatra vasturūpe na jāyate |
    2. vastusattāvabodhārthaṃ tatrābhāvapramāṇatā ||
    1. vastvasaṅkarasiddhiś ca tatprāmāṇyasamāśrayā |
    2. kṣīre dadhyādi yan nāsti prāgabhāvaḥ sa ucyate ||
    1. nāstitā payaso dadhni pradhvaṃsābhāva iṣyate |
    2. gavi yo 'śvādyabhāvas tu so 'nyonyābhāva ucyate ||
    1. śiraso 'vayavā nimnā vṛddhikāṭhinyavarjitāḥ |
    2. śaśaśṛṅgādirūpeṇa so 'tyantābhāva ucyate ||
    1. kṣīre dadhi bhaved evaṃ dadhni kṣīraṃ ghaṭe paṭaḥ |
    2. śaśe śṛṅgaṃ pṛthivyādau caitanyaṃ mūrtir ātmani ||
    1. apsu gandho rasaś cāgnau vāyau rūpeṇa tau saha |
    2. vyomni saṃsparśitā te ca na ced asya pramāṇatā ||
    1. na ca syād vyavahāro 'yaṃ kāraṇādivibhāgataḥ |
    2. prāgabhāvādibhedena nābhāvo bhidyate yadi ||
    1. na cāvastuna ete syur bhedās tenāsya vastutā |
    2. kāryādīnām abhāvaḥ ko yo 'bhāvaḥ kāraṇāditaḥ ||
    1. yadvānuvṛttivyāvṛttibuddhigrāhyo yatas tv ayam |
    2. tasmād gavādivad vastu, prameyatvāc ca gamyate ||
    1. na caupacārikatvaṃ vā bhrāntir vāpi yadṛcchayā |
    2. bhavaty ato na sāmānyaviśeṣātmakatā mṛṣā ||
    1. pratyakṣāder anutpattiḥ pramāṇābhāva ucyate |
    2. sātmanaḥ pariṇāmo vā vijñānaṃ vākyavastuni ||
    1. svarūpapararūpābhyāṃ nityaṃ sadasadātmake |
    2. vastuni jñāyate kaiś cid rūpaṃ kiñ cit kadā cana ||
    1. yasya yatra yadodbhūtir jighṛkṣā vopajāyate |
    2. cetyate 'nubhavas tasy tena ca vyapadiśyate ||
    1. tasyopakārakatvena varttate 'śastadetaraḥ |
    2. ubhayor api saṃvittāv ubhayānugamo 'sti hi ||
    1. ayam eveti yo hy eṣa bhāve bhavati nirṇayaḥ |
    2. naiṣa vastvantarābhāvasaṃvittyanugamād ṛte ||
    1. nāstīty api ca saṃvittir na vastvanugamād ṛte |
    2. jñānaṃ na jāyate kiñ cid upaṣṭambhanavarjitam ||
    1. pratyakṣādyavatāras tu bhāvāṃśo gṛhyate yadā |
    2. vyāpāras tadanutpatter abhāvāṃśe jighṛkṣite ||
    1. na tāvad indriyair eṣā nāstīty utpadyate matiḥ |
    2. bhāvāṃśenaiva saṃyogo yogyatvādindriyasya hi ||
    1. nanu bhāvād abhinnatvāt samprayogo 'sti tena ca |
    2. na hy atyantam abhedo 'sti rūpādivad ihāpi naḥ ||
    1. dharmayor bheda iṣṭo hi dharmyabhede 'pi naḥ sthite |
    2. udbhavābhibhavātmatvād grahaṇaṃ cāvatiṣṭhate ||
    1. idam eva nimittaṃ ca vivekasya pratīyate |
    2. bhāvābhāvadhiyor akṣaiḥ sambandho 'kṣānapekṣaṇam ||
    1. rūpāder api bhedaṃ ca ke cid grāhakabhedataḥ |
    2. varṇayanti yathaikasya puṃsaḥ putrādirūpatām ||
    1. buddhimātrakṛto bhedo rūpādau nityam eva hi |
    2. na ca deśādyabhinnānāṃ samudāyāvakalanā ||
    1. sadguṇadravyarūpeṇa rūpāder ekateṣyate |
    2. svarūpāpekṣayā caiṣāṃ parasparavibhinnatā ||
    1. yadi tadvadapekṣātra na syād bhedo 'tra naiva hi |
    2. sadasadrūpatā buddher bhaved anyataratra naḥ ||
    1. tatsambandhe sad ityevaṃ tadrūpatvaṃ pratīyate |
    2. nāsty atredam itīdaṃ tu tadasaṃyogahetukam ||
    1. gṛhītvā vastusadbhāvaṃ smṛtvā ca pratiyoginam |
    2. mānasaṃ nāstitājñānaṃ jāyate 'kṣānapekṣaṇāt ||
    1. svarūpamātraṃ dṛṣṭvāpi paścāt kiñ cit smarann api |
    2. tatrānyanāstitāṃ pṛṣṭas tadaiva pratipadyate ||
    1. na cāpy atrānumānatvaṃ liṅgābhāvāt pratīyate |
    2. bhāvāṃśo nanu liṅgaṃ syāt, tadānīṃ nājighṛkṣaṇāt ||
    1. abhāvāvagater janma bhāvāṃśe hy ajighṛkṣite |
    2. tasmin pratīyamāne tu nābhāve jāyate matiḥ ||
    1. na caiṣa prakṣadharmatvaṃ padavat pratipadyate |
    2. saha sarvair abhāvaiś ca bhāvo naikāntato gataḥ ||
    1. kva cid bhāve 'pi sadbhāvo jñāto yasya kadā cana |
    2. tasyābhāvo 'pi tatraiva kadā cid avagamyate ||
    1. yatrāpy adṛṣṭapūrvatvaṃ yadabhāvasya tatra ca |
    2. tadabhāvamatir dṛṣṭā sambandhe 'kṣānapekṣayā ||
    1. kasya cid yadi bhāvasya syād abhāvena kena cit |
    2. sambandhadarśanam, tatra sarvamānaṃ prasajyate ||
    1. gṛhīte 'pi ca bhāvāṃśe naivābhāve 'nyavastunaḥ |
    2. sarvatra matir ityevaṃ vyabhicārād aliṅgatā ||
    1. sambandhe gṛhyamāṇe ca sambandhigrahaṇaṃ dhruvam |
    2. tatrābhāvamatiḥ kena pramāṇopajāyate ||
    1. tadānīṃ na hi liṅgena sambandhigrahaṇaṃ bhavet |
    2. tatrāvaśyam abhāvasya pramāṇāntarato gatiḥ ||
    1. pratyakṣāder anutpattir na tu liṅgaṃ bhaviṣyati |
    2. na viśeṣaṇasambandhas tasyāḥ sāmānyato bhavet ||
    1. na cāpy abhāvasāmānye pramāṇam upajāyate |
    2. vyabhicārād viśeṣās tu pratīyeran kathaṃ tayā ||
    1. na cānavagataṃ liṅgaṃ gṛhyate ced asāv api |
    2. abhāvatvād abhāvena gṛhyetānyena hetunā ||
    1. sa cānyena grahītavyo nāgṛhīte hi liṅgatā |
    2. tadgṛhītir hi liṅgena syād anyenety anantatā ||
    1. liṅgābhāve tathaiva syād anavastheyam ity ataḥ |
    2. kvāpy asya syāt pramāṇatvaṃ liṅgatvena vinā dhruvam ||
    1. nāstīti dhīḥ phalaṃ caiṣā pratyakṣāder ajanmanaḥ |
    2. tasyaiva ca pramāṇatvam ānantaryāt pratīyate ||
    1. trilakṣaṇena yā buddhir janyate sānumeṣyate |
    2. na cānutpattirūpasya kāraṇāpekṣitā kva cit ||
    1. mānaṃ katham abhāvaś cet, prameyaṃ cāsya kīdṛśam |
    2. meyo yadvadabhavo hi mānam apy evam iṣyatām ||
    1. bhāvātmake tathā meye nābhāvasya pramāṇatā |
    2. tathābhāvaprameye 'pi na bhāvasya pramāṇatā ||
    1. bhāvātmakasya mānatvaṃ na ca rājājñayā sthitam |
    2. paricchedaphalatvād dhi prāmāṇyaṃ syād dvayor api ||
    1. yadi cāsya pramāṇatvam abhāvatvena neṣyate |
    2. vastunaḥ kāraṇatvaṃ hi dṛṣṭam ity abhimānitā ||
    1. na liṅgatvaprameyatve bhavetāṃ tadvad eva hi |
    2. tathā sati ca pūrvokto vyavahāro na sidhyati ||
    1. pramāṇānām anutpatter nābhāvasyāpi dharmatā |
    2. yatrābhāvo 'sti tenāsyāḥ sambandho naiva vidyate ||
    1. yo na sannihitas tatra tasya dharmo bhaved iyam |
    2. na ca tasya prameyatvaṃ dharmadharmitvavarjanāt ||
    1. abhāvena tu sambandho bhavet tadviṣayatvataḥ |
    2. tajjānād viṣayatvaṃ ca jñāne meyaṃ na vidyate ||
    1. saṃyogasamavāyādisambandho naiva vidyate |
    2. nāgṛhīte hi dharmatvaṃ gṛhīte siddhasādhanam ||
    1. abhāvaśabdavācyatvāt pratyakṣādeś ca bhidyate |
    2. pramāṇānām abhāvo hi prameyāṇām abhāvavat ||
    1. abhāvo vā pramāṇena svānurūpeṇa mīyate |
    2. prameyatvād yathā bhāvas tasmād bhāvātmakāt pṛthak ||
    1. karmāṇi sarvāṇi phalaiḥ samastaiḥ sarvair yathāvac ca yadaṅgakāṇḍaiḥ |
    2. na saṅgatānīha parasparaṃ ca nāṅgaṃ tadetat prabhavaṃ kratūnām ||
    1. yuktyāgamābhyām iti tarkito 'yaṃ pramāṇaṣaṭkaṃ pravibhajya bhāṣye |
    2. tato 'dhikaṃ yad dvayam iṣṭam anyair bhedo na tasyety api siddham etat ||
    1. iha bhavati śatādau sambhavādyāsahasrānmatir aviyutabhāvāt sānumānād abhinnā |
    2. jagati bahu na tathyaṃ nityam aitihyam uktaṃ bhavati tu yadi satyaṃ nāgamād bhidyate tat ||

{5,10 citrākṣepavāda CAV}

    1. paralokaphalāḥ pūrvam ākṣiptāś codanāḥ paraiḥ |
    2. idānīm aihikākṣepaḥ, sūtrakāreṇa codyate ||
    1. citrāpaśuphalatvādiviṣayāś codaṇā mṛṣā |
    2. pratyakṣādyadhikāre 'pi tair arthāsaṅgatir yataḥ ||
    1. yadīdṛk tanmṛṣā dṛṣṭaṃ vipralipsor yathā vacaḥ |
    2. nadītīre phalānīti tatrādṛśyāni tāni cet ||
    1. na vā paśuphalā citrā svakāle tadadānaḥ |
    2. snānabhujyādivat te 'pi tatsādhyā na bhavanti vā ||
    1. tadutpattāvasadbhāvāt svarge tṛptisukhādivat |
    2. vaidharmyeṇobhayatrāpi bhavetāṃ sukham ardane ||
    1. ānantaryam ayuktaṃ cet, na sāmarthyāvabodhanāt |
    2. śabdaikadeśabhūtena tena tat pratipāditam ||
    1. kālāntarānupādānāt karmasvābhāvyato 'pi ca |
    2. codyamānasya citrāder ānantaryaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||
    1. atra tāvadasaṃvādo virodhaś cottarasya tu |
    2. svargayānaviruddho hi bhasmībhāvo 'tra dṛśyate ||
    1. yajñāyudhivaco mithyā pratyakṣeṇa virodhataḥ |
    2. sādharmyeṇa śilāvākyaṃ vaidharmyeṇāptabhāṣitam ||
    1. śarīrād yadi cānyaḥ syān nāsau yajñāyudhī bhavet |
    2. na cāsya yajamānatvaṃ sadbhāvo 'pi ca durlabhaḥ ||
    1. yadi syād vidhiśabdo 'tra naivādarśanato bhavet |
    2. viśeṣo 'syeti bhedena nopāttaṃ syād idaṃ tataḥ ||
    1. vidhiśabde bhaviṣyattvaṃ phalasya parikalpya hi |
    2. virodhaparihāraḥ syād vartamāne 'pi nāsty asau ||
    1. phalaṃ ca na bhaved evaṃ bhasmībhāvād vidhāv api |
    2. tatsāmarthyena yā cānyā kalpanā tāṃ niṣedhati ||
    1. prāyaś caivamprakāratvam arthavādeṣu dṛśyate |
    2. mantreṣu ceti te sarve pakṣīkāryāḥ prayatnaḥ ||
    1. evaṃ saty agnihotrādivākyeṣv api mṛṣārthatā |
    2. vedavākyaikadeśatvāc citrādivacaneṣv api ||

{5,11 sambandhākṣepavāda SAV}

    1. svapakṣasādhanaṃ tāvat na mṛṣā vaidikaṃ vacaḥ |
    2. svārthe vaktranapekṣatvāt padārthapadabuddhivat ||
    1. tatkṛtaḥ pratyayaḥ samyaṅ nityavākyodbhavatvataḥ |
    2. vākyabuddhivad eva atra pūrvoktāś cāpi hetavaḥ ||
    1. nityān śabdārthasambandhānāśrityoktena hetunā |
    2. svataḥ prāmāṇyasiddhyartham aprāmāṇye nir kṛte ||
    1. asambandhodbhavatvena paro mithyātvam abravīt |
    2. sambandho 'sti ca nityaś cety uktam autpattikādinā ||
    1. mithyā tv asya nirāsārthaṃ tatparair neṣyate dvayam |
    2. naiva cāsty atra sambandhaḥ kṛtako veti vakṣyate ||
    1. asambhavena śeṣāṇāṃ saṃśleṣaḥ pariśiṣyate |
    2. asminn eva ca sambandhe pratītir laukiko dhruvā ||
    1. tanniṣedhamataḥ prāha na śabdo 'rthena saṅgataḥ |
    2. taddeśānantarādṛṣṭer vindhyo himavatā yathā ||
    1. evam artho dvayaṃ vāpi sādhanīyam asaṅgatam |
    2. kṣuretyādi ca siddhyarthahetor uktam athāparaḥ ||
    1. śaktirūpaṃ gṛhītvāha saṃśleṣo yadi vāryate |
    2. sambandhasiddhasādhyatvam atha sambandhamātrakam ||
    1. pitāputrādisambandhair anekāntaḥ prasajyate |
    2. ekabhūmyādisambandhād dṛṣṭānte sādhyahīnatā ||
    1. vācyavācakasambandhaniṣedhe lokabādhanam |
    2. virodhaś ca svavākyena na hi sambandhavarjitaiḥ ||
    1. pratijñārthaṃ padaiḥ śākyaḥ pratīpādayituṃ paraḥ |
    2. abhidhānakriyāyāṃ hi karmatvaṃ vācyasaṃśritam ||
    1. śabdānāṃ karaṇatvaṃ vā kartṛtvaṃ vā nirūpitam |
    2. pratipattāv upādānāt sāhitye ca vivakṣite ||
    1. niyamyate yadekasyāṃ sambandhaḥ so 'rthaśabdayoḥ |
    2. tatra yady apy asambandhaḥ kārakāṇāṃ parasparam ||
    1. tathāpi yatkriyā tasyām upakāryopakāritā |
    2. sa kriyāsaṅgateḥ paścāt sambandhaḥ kīrtyate tayoḥ ||
    1. na cātrāpy avinābhāva upayogīti sādhitam |
    2. saṃjñeti gamakatvaṃ cen na tadaṅgam iyaṃ bhavet ||
    1. gamayantīṃ śrutiṃ dṛṣṭvā kalpyate vyavahārataḥ |
    2. na caiṣā gamayatyarthaṃ sambandhe 'navadhārite ||
    1. tasmād gamakatā paścād dhūmāder iva jāyate |
    2. sānaṅgaṃ tadvad eva syād neyaṃ dhūmādibhiḥ samā ||
    1. nirūpite 'vinābhāve tatra tatkāritā hy asau |
    2. gamakatvena pūrvaṃ ca tatra notpadyate matiḥ ||
    1. iha vācakatāyāḥ prāṅ nāvinābhāvitāmatiḥ |
    2. yad eva ceha sambandhaṃ vṛddhebhyaḥ pratipadyate ||
    1. tadaiva gamako 'syāyam iti nānyasvarūpataḥ |
    2. kathayanti kva cit tāvad boddhavyo 'smād ayaṃ tv iti ||
    1. kva cid vācaka ity evaṃ vācyo 'yam iti cocyate |
    2. kva cid uccaritācchabdād dṛṣṭvārthaviṣayāṃ kriyām ||
    1. keṣāñ cit tatra boddhṛtvam anumānāt pratīyate |
    2. etenāsmād yataḥ śabdād artho 'yam avadhāritaḥ ||
    1. tena nūnam imau siddhau vācyavācakaśaktikau |
    2. itthaṃ vācakatā siddhā saṅkīrṇāpi tataḥ param ||
    1. anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ niṣkṛṣṭe 'rthe niyamyate |
    2. bahujātiguṇadravyakarmabhedāvalamvinaḥ ||
    1. pratyayāt sahasā jātā śrautalākṣaṇikātmakāt |
    2. na lokaḥ kāranābhāvān nirdhārayitum icchati ||
    1. balābalādisiddhyarthaṃ vākyajñāstu viviñcate |
    2. kakṣāntaritasāmānyaviśeṣeṣu hi durbalaḥ ||
    1. sāmānyavacanaḥ śabdo jāyate lakṣaṇābālāt |
    2. tenāvaśyaṃ vivektavyaṃ jāyate lakṣaṇābalāt ||
    1. kiyad vā nityasambandhād abhidheyena lakṣyate |
    2. tatra prayogabāhulyāt tadviśeṣeṣv asatsv api ||
    1. prayogāt parasāmānye sati vācyaprayogataḥ |
    2. sāsnādyekārthasambandhigotvamātrasya vācakaḥ ||
    1. gośabda iti vijñānam anvayavyatirekajam |
    2. tasmād gamakataivādau abhidhāyakatā punaḥ ||
    1. tannimitteti sambandhaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñitvalakṣaṇaḥ |
    2. sambandhaniyamo 'yaṃ tu yā 'vinābhāvitocyate ||
    1. sambandhagrahaṇāt pūrva yasmān na gamayaty ataḥ |
    2. gavāder nābhidhāśaktir devadattapade yathā ||
    1. yathaiva gamakaḥ śabdo vyavahārāt pratīyate |
    2. tathaiva śaktivijñānaṃ tasyopāyo 'vagamyate ||
    1. svarūpagrahaṇaṃ cāsya yathā vyāpriyate phale |
    2. tathā sambandhivijñānaṃ nāśaktis tatkṛtā bhavet ||
    1. yatsādhakatamatvena kasya cit kiñ cid ucyate |
    2. tasyānugrāhakāpekṣā na svaśaktivighātinī ||
    1. na hi tat kāraṇaṃ loke vede vā kiñ cid īdṛśam |
    2. itikartavyatāsādhye yasya nānugrahe 'rthitā ||
    1. pratyātmaniyatatvāc ca yathaiva karaṇaṃ bhavet |
    2. bāhyāntaravibhāgena kva cit syād vā vivakṣayā ||
    1. udvigno hy andhakāreṇa kaś cid evaṃ bravīty api |
    2. kiṃ cakṣuṣā mamaitena dṛṣṭaṃ dīpena yanmayā ||
    1. nityavṛttau tu nāndhānāṃ dṛṣṭir dīpaśatair api |
    2. rūpādidarśane yasmāt tasmāc cakṣuḥ prakāśakam ||
    1. śarīrātmamanoyogād asādhāraṇātābalāt |
    2. vijñānāsattibhāvāc ca cakṣuḥ kāraṇam iṣyate ||
    1. tathaivehāpi sambandhajñānam aṅgaṃ prasiddhitaḥ |
    2. gauravāt karaṇatvena mataṃ cet kena vāryate ||
    1. yathā cakṣur itīdaṃ tu vyabhicāritvam ucyate |
    2. devadatte 'pi cāvyaktāṃ śaktim icchanti yuktitaḥ ||
    1. prakāśe 'vasthite bāhye nāndho rūpaṃ pratīyate |
    2. phalānantaryataś cāpi cakṣuḥ karaṇam iṣyate ||
    1. puruṣādhīnavijñānas tebhyaḥ prāganirūpitaḥ |
    2. yaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhaḥ sa ceṣṭaś ced dhruvaṃ kṛtaḥ ||
    1. bhinnadeśādyadhiṣṭhānād yathā rajjughaṭādiṣu |
    2. samaṃ nāsty anayoḥ kiñ cit tenāsaṅgatatā svataḥ ||

{5,12 sphoṭavāda SPH}

    1. ādhārātmani viñāte sukham ādheyabodhanam |
    2. tasyaiva tāvat prastāvād atha gaur ity ato 'bravīt ||
    1. pratyakṣe 'pi visaṃvādo yeṣāṃ kaḥ svayam uttaram |
    2. tebhyo dadyād iti jñātvā vṛddhānāṃ matam abravīt ||
    1. tatrārthapratyayadvāraṃ kṛtaṃ śabdanirūpaṇam |
    2. yair āsatāṃ tu te tāvat pratyakṣeṇa parīkṣyate ||
    1. pratyakṣaṃ nāsamarthaṃ nastena cārthe 'vadhārite |
    2. na hetur balavān anyaḥ parīkṣyeta yatas tataḥ ||
    1. tasmāc chrotraparicchinno yady arthaṃ gamayen na vā |
    2. sarvathā tasya śabdatvaṃ lokasiddhaṃ na hīyate ||
    1. yadi tv arthagatau śaktir na syād asya tataḥ punaḥ |
    2. vastvantaraṃ prakalpyeta vinā śabdaprasiddhitaḥ ||
    1. agnyādīn gamayanto 'pi śabdā dhūmādayo na hi |
    2. na vā 'pratyāyakatvāt syād ekavarṇeṣv aśabdatā ||
    1. na ca prāgarthavijñānāś chotragrāhye na śabdadhīḥ |
    2. na cārthajñānataḥ paścād aśrautre 'pi ca śabdatā ||
    1. parasparānapekṣāś ca śrotrabuddhyā svarūpataḥ |
    2. varṇā evāvagamyante na pūrvāparavastunī ||
    1. alpīyasāpi yatnena śabdam uccaritaṃ matiḥ |
    2. yadi vā gṛhṇāti varṇaṃ vā sakalaṃ sphuṭam ||
    1. pṛthaṅ na copalabhyante varṇasyāvayavāḥ kva cit |
    2. na ca varṇeṣv anusyūtā dṛśyante tantuvat paṭe ||
    1. teṣām anupalabdheś ca na jñātā liṅgasaṅgatiḥ |
    2. nāgamas tatparaś cāsti nādṛṣṭe copamā kva cit ||
    1. na cāpy anupapattiḥ syād varṇasyāvayavair vinā |
    2. yathānyāvayavānāṃ hi vināpy avayavāntaraiḥ ||
    1. pratyakṣeṇāvabuddhaś ca varṇo 'vayavavarjitaḥ |
    2. kiṃ na syād, vyomavac cātra liṅgaṃ tadrahitā matiḥ ||
    1. tadvac cāsyaikabuddhitvād deśabhede 'py abhinnatā |
    2. nanu bhedamatir na syāt, tavāpy ekatvadhīḥ kutaḥ ||
    1. sāmānyeṣu mamaikā dhīs tadvyaktiṣu ca bhedadhīḥ |
    2. na hīṣṭaṃ bhedamātraṃ hi na syād ekatvadhīr yataḥ ||
    1. vyaktes tāvan na sāmānyaṃ bhinnarūpaṃ pratīyate |
    2. varṇeṣv anyatra śabdatvān nānyac ced varṇa eva saḥ ||
    1. sa eveti matir nāpi sādṛśyam, na ca tat kva cit |
    2. vināvayavasāmānyād varṇeṣv avayavā na ca ||
    1. pratyakṣaviṣayatvāc ca nānyāpoho 'pi yujyate |
    2. vācakaś cātra liṅgaṃ vā na tadānīṃ pratīyate ||
    1. gakārādiṣu sāmānyaṃ śabdatvaṃ kalpyate yathā |
    2. gotvaṃ ca śābaleyādau tathaitat kiṃ na kalpyate ||
    1. śābaleyagakāradīn niṣpannān vyaktirūpataḥ |
    2. sāmānyadhīr na gṛhṇātīty ato jātir apīṣyate ||
    1. na tu drutādibhede 'pi niṣpannā sampratīyate |
    2. gavyaktyantaravyāvṛttā gavyaktir aparā sphuṭā ||
    1. tenaikatvena varṇasya buddhir ekopajāyate |
    2. viśeṣabuddhisadbhāvo bhaved vyañjakabhedataḥ ||
    1. yathaiva tava gatvādi gamyamānaṃ drutādibhiḥ |
    2. viśeṣair api nānekam evaṃ varṇo 'pi no bhavet ||
    1. tvayāpi vyañjakavyaktibhedād bhedo 'bhyupeyate |
    2. mamāpi vyañjakair nādair bhedabuddhir bhaviṣyati ||
    1. tena yat prārthyate jāte tad varṇād eva labhyate |
    2. vyaktilabhyaṃ ca nādebhya iti gatvādidhīr yathā ||
    1. kalpayitvāpi tatpaścād vibhutvaikatvanityatāḥ |
    2. pratyekavṛttitā cāsya bhaveyur mahataḥ śramāt ||
    1. dvayasiddhas tu varṇātmā nityatvādi yathaiva ca |
    2. kalpitasyeṣyate tadvat siddhasyaivābhyupeyatām ||
    1. pratyekasamavāye ca kleśo naiva bhaviṣyati |
    2. vyañjaneṣu ca dhībhedo naiva tādṛk pratīyate ||
    1. dṛśyate 'janurāgeṇa bhedo yo nāma, tatra naḥ |
    2. vivedo 'sty eva na hy eṣa kevalānāṃ pratīyate ||
    1. akṣv apy evaṃ paropādhir drutādipratyayo yathā |
    2. varṇā ''śritatvād varṇatvavyañjanapratyayo yathā ||
    1. gakāro 'tyantaniṣkṛṣṭagatvādhāro na gamyate |
    2. gānyabuddhyanirūpyatvāt paraiḥ kalpitagatvavat ||
    1. avastutvena sādhyatvān niṣedhād dhetusādhyayoḥ |
    2. sapakṣe 'nyatarāsiddhir na doṣāyātra jāyate ||
    1. varṇatvāc cāpi sādhyo 'yaṃ yakārādivad eva ca |
    2. vyatirekasya cādṛṣṭer nātra dṛṣṭaṃ nirvartakam ||
    1. gotvādivāraṇe tv eva dṛṣṭabādhaḥ sphuṭo bhavet |
    2. nānyathā hi matis tatra syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ ||
    1. na cāpy atraikavastutve bhedo vyañjakabhedataḥ |
    2. na piṇḍavyatirekeṇa vyañjako 'tra dhvanir yathā ||
    1. piṇḍavyaṅgyaiva gotvādir jātir nityaṃ pratīyate |
    2. tena bhinneṣu piṇḍeṣu jātir ekā pratīyate ||
    1. nanu yasya dvayaṃ śrotraṃ tasya buddhidvayaṃ bhavet |
    2. bhavato 'tīndriyatvāt tu kathaṃ nādair viśeṣadhīḥ ||
    1. nādena saṃskṛtāc chrotrād yadā śabdaḥ pratīyate |
    2. tadupaśleṣas tat asya bodhaṃ ke cit pracakṣate ||
    1. naiva vā grahaṇaṃ teṣāṃ śabde buddhis tu tadvaśāt |
    2. saṃskārānukṛteḥ so 'pi mahatvādyavabudhyate ||
    1. madhuraṃ tiktarūpeṇa śvetaṃ pītatayā tathā |
    2. gṛhṇanti pittadoṣeṇa viṣayaṃ bhrāntacetasaḥ ||
    1. tathā vegena dhāvanto nāvyārūḍhāś ca gacchataḥ |
    2. parvatādīn vijānanti bhrameṇa bhramataś ca tān ||
    1. maṇḍūkavasayāktākṣā vaṃśānuragabuddhibhiḥ |
    2. vyaktyalpatvamahattvābhyāṃ sāmānyaṃ ca tadāśrtayam ||
    1. gṛhṇanti yadvadetāni nimittagrahaṇād vinā |
    2. vyañjakasthamabudhvaiva vyaṅgye bhrāntir bhaviṣyati ||
    1. varṇāntaratvam evāhuḥ ke cid dīrghapluptādiṣu |
    2. na hi drutādivat tatra prayoho nāntarīyakaḥ ||
    1. tathā ca sati sāmānyaṃ triṣvatvaṃ kaiś cid iṣyate |
    2. sāmānyakalpanā tv anyair na yuktety abhidhīyate ||
    1. atvam ity ucyamānaṃ hi na dīrghaplutayor bhavet |
    2. ātvaṃ na hrasvaplutayos traimātryaṃ na ca pūrvayoḥ ||
    1. sarvasādhāraṇatvena tad vijñātuṃ na śakyate |
    2. pratyekaṃ śābaleyādirūpe gotvaṃ yathā sphuṭam ||
    1. avarṇakulaśabdo 'pi sthānasāmyād vanādivat |
    2. samudāyārthavācīti na jātivacano bhavet ||
    1. svato hrasvādibhedas tu nityavāde virudhyate |
    2. sarvadā yasya sadbhāvaḥ sa kathaṃ mātrikaḥ svayam ||
    1. tasmād uccāraṇaṃ tasya mātrākālaṃ pratīyate |
    2. dvimātraṃ vā trimātraṃ ā na varṇo mātrikaḥ svayam ||
    1. dīrghāder nanv anaṅgatvaṃ vācakādharmato bhavet |
    2. itthaṃ pratīyamānāḥ syur varṇā na pratipādakāḥ ||
    1. yādṛśāt pūrvadṛṣṭo 'sāv artho gamyate tādṛśāt |
    2. bhrāntyā kathaṃ pratītiś cet, nāsāv artham iti prati ||
    1. yathāśvādijavaḥ puṃsāṃ kāryāṅgatvaṃ prakalpayet |
    2. paradharmo 'pi varṇānāṃ dhvanidharmās tathaiva naḥ ||
    1. nanu dīrghādyanityatvād anityo vācako bhavet |
    2. ānupūrvīvad evāsya parihāro bhaviṣyati ||
    1. tathodāttādibhedānāṃ saṃskāravaśagā matiḥ |
    2. teṣāṃ dīrghādivad bhedo na kadā cit pratīyate ||
    1. tatraikavarṇarūpatve bhedo 'pi syād drutādivat |
    2. nātra varṇāntaravyaktir iva dhvanyantarodbhavaḥ ||
    1. ta eva mṛdutīvratvaśīghratvādisamanvitāḥ |
    2. abhede cāpi varṇasya dhvanīnāṃ dviprakāratā ||
    1. ke cit svarūpabodhārthāḥ ke cid bodhānuvartinaḥ |
    2. yugapatkramarūpeṇa saṃskārotpādahetavaḥ ||
    1. tatra dīrghādibodhaḥ syāt pūrveṣāṃ pracayo yadā |
    2. varṇātmaiva hi kālena tāvatā taiḥ pratīyate ||
    1. yugapatpracitais taiś ca syād udāttādikalpanā |
    2. pracaye tv itareṣāṃ syād vatibhedo drutādikaḥ ||
    1. varṇātmanyavabuddhe 'pi tadrūpām eva te matim |
    2. śanair utpādayanti, iti nānyo varṇaḥ pratīyate ||
    1. vyaktyākṛtikṛto bhedo yady apy ekāntato bhavet |
    2. varṇeṣu jaimineḥ pakṣas tathāpi na virudhyate ||
    1. nityatvayatnaḥ sarvo 'pi gatvādiṣu bhaviṣyati |
    2. gakārādivacaś caitat teṣv eva na virotsyate ||
    1. vicchinnayatnavyaṅgyaiś ca nityaiḥ sarvagatair api |
    2. vyatiriktapadārambho varṇair nātropapadyate ||
    1. anārabdhe ca gośabde gośabdatvaṃ kathaṃ bhavet |
    2. varṇasāmānyavac cāpi na tatkalpanam arhati ||
    1. varṇātmanām abhedāc ca siddhā sāmānyadhīr api |
    2. samudāyo 'pi tebhyo 'syo vāraṇīyo 'nayā diśā ||
    1. abhedasamudāyas tu teṣāṃ dharmo na duṣyati |
    2. teṣām asti hi sāmarthyam arthapratyāyanaṃ prati ||
    1. yāvanto yādṛśo ye ca yadarthapratipādane |
    2. varṇāḥ prajñātasāmarthyāste tathivāvabodhakāḥ ||
    1. teṣāṃ tu guṇabhūtānām arthapratyāyanaṃ prati |
    2. sāhityam ekakartrādikramaś cāpi vivakṣitaḥ ||
    1. kartraikatve nimitte ca krame sati niyāmakam |
    2. prayuñjānasya yat pūrvaṃ vṛddhebhyaḥ kramadarśanam ||
    1. yaugapadyaṃ tv aśakyatvān naiva teṣām ihāśritam |
    2. kartṛbhedaś ca tatra syāt, na caivaṃ dṛśyate 'bhidhā ||
    1. yugapad dṛśyasāmarthyā naiva śaktāḥ krame yathā |
    2. bhāvās tathā krame śaktā yaugapadye na śaknuyuḥ ||
    1. dṛṣṭaś ca pūrṇamāsādeḥ kramaḥ saṃhatyakāriṇaḥ |
    2. abhyāsānāṃ ca loke 'pi svādhyāyagrahaṇādiṣu ||
    1. sādhanāditrayāṇāṃ ca vyāpārasyaikakālatā |
    2. sarvatrāstīti neha syād upālambhaḥ kramaṃ prati ||
    1. niṣpannā eva dṛśyante vyāpārāḥ sarva eva hi |
    2. sūkṣmā vyāpārabhedās tu dṛśyate na kadā cana ||
    1. ekasādhanasāṃsthāś ca vyāpārāvayavā yadā |
    2. svarūpato nirīkṣyante yaugapadyam asat tadā ||
    1. kiṃ punar bahavo bhinnā bhinnasādhanasaṃśritāḥ |
    2. bhaveyur yaugapadyena vyāpārāḥ kramavartinaḥ ||
    1. yadā tv ādyaparispandād prabhṛtyā phalalābhataḥ |
    2. kriyā pūrvaparībhūtā lakṣyate varttate tadā ||
    1. tenātrāpi vivakṣātaḥ prabhṛtyā 'rthāvabodhanāt |
    2. sākalyenekṣyamāṇe syād vyāpāre varttamānatā ||
    1. pratyekaṃ ye punas tatra vyāpārās tannirūpaṇam |
    2. phalāniṣpattito na syān nāstitvaṃ na ca tāvatā ||
    1. phalānumeyatāyāṃ ca vyāpārasya phalaṃ prati |
    2. kārakāṇāṃ yathāsthānaṃ vyāpāre vartamānatā ||
    1. avaśyam bhāvinī nityaṃ pratyāsattiś ca kasya cit |
    2. na tāvatā vyapetatvāt itareṣām anaṅgatā ||
    1. dvyantaraikāntaratvena gakārau kārayor dhruvam |
    2. arthaṃ pratyāyane śaktis tatra sthau gamakau yataḥ ||
    1. yathā visarjanīyasya vyavadhāne na śaktatā |
    2. tathaivetarayoḥ śaktir ānantarye na vidyate ||
    1. na ca yatraikaśo 'śaktis tatra sarveṣv aśaktatā |
    2. tathā hy aṅgāni dṛśyante śālyādivahanādiṣu ||
    1. śaktis tatrāsti kā cid dhi vahane sā samṛddhyate |
    2. saṅghātena tu varṇānāṃ pratyekaṃ kā cidīkṣyate ||
    1. na hy arthāvayavaḥ kaś cit pratyekaṃ taiḥ pratīyate |
    2. samastasyātha vā kaś cid bodhaleśo 'tra jāyate ||
    1. rathasyāpi tu yat kāryaṃ śālyādivahanaṃ na tat |
    2. pratyekaṃ dṛśyate kiñ cin manāg api yathehitam ||
    1. atha yatkiñcid ucyeta vahane tad ihāpi naḥ |
    2. svātmapratyayahetutvaṃ varṇeṣv arthe 'pi vā kva cit ||
    1. yasyānavayavaḥ sphoṭo vyajyate varṇabuddhibhiḥ |
    2. so 'pi paryanuyogena vaivaitena vimucyate ||
    1. tatrāpi prativarṇaṃ hi padasphoṭo na gamyate |
    2. na cāvayavaśo vyaktis tadabhāvān na cātra śrīḥ ||
    1. pratyekaṃ cāpy aśaktānāṃ samudāye 'py aśaktayā |
    2. tatra yaḥ parihāras te sa no 'trāpi bhaviṣyati ||
    1. sadbhāvavyatirekau ca tathāvayavavarjanam |
    2. tavādhikaṃ bhavet tasmād yatno 'sāv arthabuddhiṣu ||
    1. nānyathānupapattiś ca bhaved arthamatiṃ prati |
    2. tad evāsyā nimittaṃ syāj jāyate yadanantaram ||
    1. sā ca varṇadvayajñāne 'tīte 'ntyajñānataḥ parā |
    2. bhavatītīdṛg evāsyā nimittam avakalpate ||
    1. vinā saṃskārakalpena tadanantaravṛttitaḥ |
    2. kṛtānugrahasāmarthyo varṇo 'ntyaḥ pratipādakaḥ ||
    1. eṣa eva tu saṃskāra iti ke cit pracakṣate |
    2. adṛṣṭakalpanātītaṃ tāvan mātraṃ hi dṛśyate ||
    1. atha vā vāsanaivāstu saṃskāraḥ, sarva eva hi |
    2. dṛḍhajñānagṛhīte 'rthe saṃskāro 'stīti manvate ||
    1. tasyārthabuddhihetutve visaṃvādo 'sya nirṇaye |
    2. tadbhāvabhāvitāhetur anyatreva pratīyate ||
    1. saṃskāre niṣpramāṇe tu pūrvavṛttattvakalpanam |
    2. niṣpramāṇakam eveti nānugrahaphalaṃ bhavet ||
    1. yady api smṛtihetutvaṃ saṃskārasya vyavasthitam |
    2. kāryāntareṣu sāmarthyaṃ na tasya pratiṣidhyate ||
    1. tena saṃskārasadbhāvo nānenaivaṃ prakalpyate |
    2. tasyārthabuddhihetutvam adṛṣṭaṃ kevalaṃ kṛtam ||
    1. śabdapakṣe 'pi tac caitad adṛṣṭatvān na mucyate |
    2. kāryabodhanaśaktatvaṃ tulyaṃ saṃskāraśabdayoḥ ||
    1. kṣīṇārthāpattir evaṃ ca na sphoṭaṃ parikalpayet |
    2. saṃskārakalpanā pūrvam avaśyam bhāvinī hi te ||
    1. dhvanibhyo 'py aparas tāvan neṣyetārthamatiṃ prati |
    2. te vā yady upalabhyeran varṇāḥ pratyakṣato na ca ||
    1. varṇānāṃ yaugapadyena yadi cāvaśyam arthitā |
    2. nityatvāt sarvadā tat syān na tu kāraṇatā tathā ||
    1. itthaṃ kramagṛhītānāṃ yugapad yātha vā parā |
    2. sthitiḥ sā kāraṇaṃ tu syān nityam arthadhiyaṃ prati ||
    1. yad vā pratyakṣataḥ pūrvaṃ kramajñāneṣu yat param |
    2. samastavarṇavijñānaṃ tadarthajñānakāraṇam ||
    1. tatra jñāne ca varṇānāṃ yaugapadyaṃ pratīyate |
    2. nāvaśyaṃ yaugapadyena pratyakṣasthena tad bhavet ||
    1. citrarūpāṃ cā tāṃ buddhiṃ sadasadvarṇagocarām |
    2. ke cid āhur yathā varṇo gṛhyate 'ntaḥ pade pade ||
    1. antyavarṇe 'pi vijñāte pūrvasaṃskārakāritam |
    2. smaraṇaṃ yaugapadyena sarveṣv anye pracakṣate ||
    1. sarveṣu caivam artheṣu mānasaṃ sarvavādinām |
    2. iṣṭaṃ samuccayajñānaṃ kramajñāneṣu satsv api ||
    1. na cet tadābhyupeyeta kramadṛṣṭeṣu naiva hi |
    2. śatādirūpaṃ jāyeta tatsamuccayadarśanam ||
    1. tena śrotramanobhyāṃ syāt kramād varṇeṣu yady api |
    2. pūrvajñānaṃ parastāt tu yugapat smaraṇaṃ bhavet ||
    1. tadārūḍhās tato varṇā na dūre 'rthāvabodhanāt |
    2. śabdārthamatis tena laukikair abhidhīyate ||
    1. citrabuddhyānayā bhrāntyā varṇebhyo vyatirekataḥ |
    2. paścād gaur iti vijñānaṃ pratyakṣaṃ kaiś cid iṣyate ||
    1. vailakṣaṇyaṃ tu tasyeṣṭam ekaikajñānataḥ sphuṭam |
    2. varṇarūpāvabodhāt tu na tadarthāntaraṃ bhavet ||
    1. yadi cārthāntaratvaṃ syād ekaikasmād trayasya tat |
    2. varṇatrayaparityāge buddhir nānyatra jāyate ||
    1. gaur ity ekamatitvaṃ tu naivāsmābhir nivāryate |
    2. tadgrāhyaikārthatābhyāṃ ca śabde syād ekatāmatiḥ ||
    1. śaidhyād alpāntaratvāc ca gośabde sābhaved api |
    2. devadattādiśabdeṣu sphuṭo bhedaḥ pratīyate ||
    1. na gauṇaḥ śabda ity evaṃ granthasambandhanaṃ bhavet |
    2. asy akṣareṣu hetutvaṃ tatparaṃ vacanaṃ hi tat ||
    1. śabdād iti ca hetutvaṃ pañcamyātrābhidhīyate |
    2. bhavatpakṣe 'pi caikāntāj jñānena vyavadhir bhavet ||
    1. gauṇo 'nyathā prasiddho vā prayujyetānyathā yadi |
    2. na cānyādṛṅnimittatvaṃ kasya cit sampratīyate ||
    1. svavyāpāravyavāyo hi sarvasminn eva kārake |
    2. dṛṣṭo vyāpāra īdṛk tu śabdasyety avyavetatā ||
    1. gakārāder yadā cānyo na loke śabda ucyate |
    2. tadā tasmāt pratīte 'rthe śabdād iti kathaṃ bhavet ||
    1. śabdajñānādisaṃskāravyaktasphoṭakṛte 'tha vā |
    2. pratyaye śabdajanyatvam iti gauṇaṃ prasajyate ||
    1. saṃskārajananārthaṃ ca na śabdoccāraṇaṃ matam |
    2. arthapratītim uddiśya prayuktasya kramādayam ||
    1. tasmāt tādarthyataḥ śabdaḥ phalena vyapadiśyate |
    2. samuccayāvabodhe tu vyavadhānaṃ na kena cit ||
    1. yadi cāpūrvasaṃskāra itikartavyateṣyate |
    2. varṇo 'ntyo gamakas tasya śabdatvān mudhyatā bhavet ||
    1. varṇā vā dhvanayo vāpi sphoṭaṃ na padavākyayoḥ |
    2. vyañjanti vyañjakatvena yathā dīpaprabhādayaḥ ||
    1. sattvād ghaṭādivac ceti sādhanāni yathāruci |
    2. laukikavyatirekeṇa kalpite 'rthe bhavanti hi ||
    1. nārthasya vācakaḥ sphoṭo varṇebhyo vyatirekataḥ |
    2. ghaṭāvivat, na dṛṣṭena virodho dharmasiddhitaḥ ||
    1. pratiṣedhet tu yo varṇān tajjñānānantarodbhavān |
    2. dṛṣṭabādho bhavet tasya śaśicandraniṣedhavat ||
    1. varṇotthā vārthadhīreṣā tajjñānānantarodbhavā |
    2. yedṛśī sā tadutthā hi dhūmāder iva bahnidhīḥ ||
    1. dīpavad vā gakārādir gavādeḥ pratipādakaḥ |
    2. dhruvaṃ pratīyamānatvāt, tatpūrvaṃ pratipādanāt ||
    1. varṇātiriktaḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ padeṣu mandaṃ phalam ādadhāti |
    2. kāryāṇi vākyāvayavāśrayāṇi satyāni katuṃ kṛta eṣa yatnaḥ ||

{5,13 ākṛtivāda AKV}

    1. ākṛtivyatirikte 'rthe sambandho nityatāsya ca |
    2. na sidhyetām iti jñātvā tad vācyatvam ihocyate ||
    1. tatsadbhāvaprasiddhyartham atra tāvat prayatyate |
    2. vācyatve vakṣyate yuktir vyaktyā saha balābale ||
    1. jātim evākṛtiṃ prāhur vyaktir ākriyate yayā |
    2. sāmānyaṃ tac ca piṇḍānām ekabuddhinibandhanam ||
    1. tannimittaṃ ca yatkiñcit sāmānyaṃ śabdagocaram |
    2. sarva evecchatīty evam avirodho 'tra vādinām ||
    1. sarvavastuṣu buddhiś ca vyāvṛttyanugamātmikā |
    2. jāyate dvyātmatvena vinā sā ca na siddhyati ||
    1. viśeṣamātra iṣṭe ca na sāmānyamatir bhavet |
    2. sāmānyamātrabodhe tu nirnimittā viśeṣadhīḥ ||
    1. na cāpy anyatarā bhrāntir upacāreṇa ceṣyate |
    2. dṛḍhatvāt sarvadā buddher bhrāntis tadbhrāntivādinām ||
    1. mukhyayoś cāpy adṛṣṭatvān nopacāreṇa kalpanā |
    2. bāhyārthaviṣayatvaṃ ca buddhīnāṃ pratipāditam ||
    1. anyonyāpekṣitā nityaṃ syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ |
    2. viśeṣāṇāṃ ca sāmānyaṃ te ca tasya bhavanti hi ||
    1. nirviśeṣaṃ na sāmānyaṃ bhavec chaśaviṣāṇavat |
    2. sāmānyarahitatvāc ca viśeṣās tadvad eva hi ||
    1. tadanātmakarūpeṇa hetū vācyāvimau punaḥ |
    2. tena tātyantabhedo 'pi syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ ||
    1. sāmānyabuddhiśaktitvaṃ viśeṣeṣv eva yo vadet |
    2. vinā vastvantarāt, tena vācyā śaktis tu kīdṛśī ||
    1. grāhyā kiṃ vāpy asambodhā bhinnaikā vā tathaiva ca |
    2. gṛhyate yadi saikā ca jātir evānyaśabdikā ||
    1. bhaven nirviṣayā buddhir yadi śaktir na gṛhyate |
    2. na hi sadbhāvamātreṇa viśayaḥ kaś cid iṣyate ||
    1. parasparavibhinnatvād viśeṣā naikabuddhibhiḥ |
    2. gṛhyante viṣayāsattvāc chaktiś caiṣāṃ na vidyate ||
    1. bhinnatve vāpi śaktīnām ekabuddhir na labhyate |
    2. viśeṣaśaktyabhede ca tāvanmātramatir bhavet ||
    1. bhinnā viśeṣaśaktibhyaḥ sarvatrānugatāpi ca |
    2. pratyekaṃ samavetā ca tasmāj jātir apīṣyatām ||
    1. tenātmadharmo bhedānām ekadhīviṣayo 'sti naḥ |
    2. sāmānyam ākṛtir jātiḥ śaktir vā so 'bhidhīyatām ||
    1. nanu bhinne 'pi sattādau sāmānyam iti jāyate |
    2. buddhir vināpi sāmānyād anyasmāt sā kathaṃ bhavet ||
    1. vanopanyāsatulyo 'yam upanyāsaḥ kṛtas tvayā |
    2. bhrāntitvena hi naitasyā bhrāntir gotvādidhīr api ||
    1. śabdāt pūrvaṃ hi sarveṣu gavādāv iva naikadhīḥ |
    2. vastutvaṃ cātra sāmānyaṃ dharmaṃ ke cit pracakṣate ||
    1. evaṃ tu kalpyamāne syāt sāmānyānām anantatā |
    2. punas tena sahānyeṣu sāmānyamatir asti hi ||
    1. viśeṣeṣv api vastutvāt sāmānyam iti dhīr bhavet |
    2. sattādiṣv iva, ttenaitat sāmānyaṃ nopapadyate ||
    1. tasmād ekasya bhinneṣu yā vṛttis tannibandhanaḥ |
    2. sāmānyaśabdaḥ sattādāv ekadhīkaraṇena vā ||
    1. piṇḍeṣv eva ca sāmānyam, nāntarā gṛhyate yataḥ |
    2. na hy ākāśavadicchanti sāmānyaṃ nāma kiñ cana ||
    1. yad vā sarvagatatve 'pi vyaktiḥ śaktyanurodhataḥ |
    2. śaktiḥ kāryānumeyā hi vyaktidarśanahetukā ||
    1. tena yatraiva dṛśyeta vyaktiḥ śaktaṃ tad eva tu |
    2. tenaiva ca na sarvāsu vyaktiṣv etat pratīyate ||
    1. bhinnatve 'pi hi kāsāñ cic chaktiḥ kāś cid aśaktikāḥ |
    2. na ca paryanuyogo 'sti vastuśakteḥ kadā cana ||
    1. vahnir dahati nākāśaṃ ko 'tra paryanuyujyatām |
    2. na cānyā mṛgyate yuktir yathā sandṛśyate tathā ||
    1. na hi yuktyantaraṃ nāstīty etaj jñānam anarthakam |
    2. dharmaś cāvyabhicāryasya na mṛgya upalakṣaṇe ||
    1. nānumānāvagamyaṃ tat, pratyakṣe lakṣaṇena kim |
    2. svābhāvikaś ca sambandho jātivyaktyor na hetumān ||
    1. tenaitasya prasiddhyarthaṃ nānyat sāmānyam iṣyate |
    2. śaktisiddhivadetasya svabhāvo 'tra na vāryate ||
    1. yad vā naimittikatve 'pi tāvanmātrapratīkṣaṇāt |
    2. viśeṣeṣv eva labdheṣu keṣu cin nānyavāñchanam ||
    1. na vyañjantyapare kasmād, yatas teṣu na dṛśyate |
    2. tebhyo 'pi na nivṛttyarthaṃ mṛgyo hetuḥ svabhāvataḥ ||
    1. sāmānyaṃ nānyadiṣṭaṃ cet tasya vṛtter niyāmakam |
    2. gotvenāpi vinā kasmād gobuddhir na niyamyate ||
    1. yathā tulye 'pi bhinnatve keṣu cid vṛttyapekṣitā |
    2. gotvāder animitte 'pi tathā buddhir bhaviṣyati ||
    1. viṣayeṇa hi buddhīnāṃ vinā notpattir iṣyate |
    2. viśeṣād anyad icchanti sāmānyaṃ tena tad dhruvam ||
    1. tā hi tena vinotpannā mithyāḥ syur viṣayād ṛte |
    2. na tv anyena vinā vṛttiḥ sāmānyasyeha duṣyati ||
    1. aniṣyamāṇe sāmānye vṛttiḥ śabdānumānayoḥ |
    2. naiva syāt, na hi sambandho bhedair ānantyato bhavet ||
    1. anubhūtatayā vāsau puruṣasyopayujyate |
    2. jātivyaktyos tu sambandhe nānubhūtyā prayojanam ||
    1. siddhe viṣayarūpe ca gotvādāv indriyaiḥ punaḥ |
    2. arthāpattyupalabdhā syāc chaktir ekā niyāmikā ||
    1. na cātmahetum evāsau siddhaṃ bādhitum arhati |
    2. śaktiś ca naitayā buddhyā, nendriyaiḥ sā hi gṛhyate ||
    1. sāmānyāntarayogānām aniṣṭhā yā ca varṇyate |
    2. tayā sāmānyanāśaḥ syāt sa ca dṛṣṭena bādhyate ||
    1. sambandhas tasya hetur vā tadgrahe na ca kāraṇam |
    2. svarūpato gṛhīte 'rthe paścād etad vikalpyate ||
    1. sāsnādyekārthasambandhi gotvam ity upalakṣaṇam |
    2. na ca svasamavāyy eva kevalaṃ cihnam iṣyate ||
    1. sāsnādibhyas tu piṇḍasya bhedo nātyantato yadā |
    2. sāmānyasya ca piṇḍebhyas tadā syād etad uttaram ||
    1. kasmāt sāsnādimatsv eva gotvaṃ yasmāt tadātmakam |
    2. tādātmyam asya kasmāc cet svabhāvād iti gamyatām ||
    1. upalabdhyanusāreṇa vyavasthāsiddhir īdṛśī |
    2. svato gotvādibhedas tu na tu vyañjakabhedataḥ ||
    1. sā bhūd drutādivanmithyā, nyañjakasya tu kiṃkṛtaḥ |
    2. bhedo hastyādipiṇḍebhyaḥ, svataś cet, iha tatsamam ||
    1. vyaṅgyajātiviśeṣāc cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam |
    2. tasmāt svābhāviko bhedo jātivyaktyoḥ pratīyate ||
    1. anekānanyavṛttittvān na sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ |
    2. ekavastvātmatā yuktā varaṃ tenaupacārikam ||
    1. bhinnebhyaś cāpy abhinnatvād bhedas tat svātmavad bhavet |
    2. ekasmād vāpy abhinnatvād vyaktyekatvaṃ pratīyate ||
    1. ekānekatvam ekasya tathānyānanyatā katham |
    2. tat sāmānyaṃ viśeṣaś cety evamādi ca duṣkaram ||
    1. virodhas tāvad ekāntād vaktum atra na yujyate |
    2. sāmānyānanyavijñāte viśeṣe naikavṛttitā ||
    1. sāmānyānanyavṛttitvaṃ viśeṣātmaikabhāvataḥ |
    2. evañ ca parihartavyā bhinnābhinnatvakalpanā ||
    1. kena cid dhy ātmanaikatvaṃ nānātvaṃ cāsya kena cit |
    2. sāmānyasya tu yo bhedaṃ brūte tasya viśeṣataḥ ||
    1. darśayitvābhyupetavyam, viśeṣaikyaṃ ca jātitaḥ |
    2. yathā kalmāṣavarṇasya yatheṣṭaṃ varṇanigrahaḥ ||
    1. citratvād vastuno 'py evaṃ bhedābhedāvadhāraṇam |
    2. sāmānyāṃśe tu niṣkṛṣya bhedo yena prasādhyate ||
    1. tasya hetor asiddhatvaṃ siddhaś cet siddhasādhanam |
    2. bhedebhyo 'nanyarūpeṇa sāmānyaṃ gṛhyate yadā ||
    1. tadāviśeṣamātreṇa vastu pratyavabhāsate |
    2. tadudbhūtyā ca sāmānyaṃ tadbhāvānuguṇaṃ sthitam ||
    1. sad apy agrāhyarūpatvād asadvat pratibhāti naḥ |
    2. viśeṣān api sāmānyād yadā bhedena buddhyate ||
    1. tadā sāmānyamātratvam evam eva pratīyate |
    2. yadā tu śabalaṃ vastu yugapat pratipadyate ||
    1. tadānyān anyabhedādi sarvam eva pralīyate |
    2. na ca tat tādṛśaṃ kaś cic chabdaḥ śaknoti bhāṣitum ||
    1. sāmānyāṃśān apoddhṛtya padaṃ sarvaṃ pravarttate |
    2. samastavastvapekṣāṃ ca padārthānām apoddhṛtim ||
    1. ke cid āhur asadrūpam, aṃśatvaṃ tu na vāryate |
    2. sārūpyam eva sāmānyaṃ piṇḍānāṃ yena kalpyate ||
    1. tena sārūpyaśabdena kiṃ punaḥ pratipadyate |
    2. samānarūpabhāvaś cej jātiḥ sāsmābhir iṣyate ||
    1. sādṛśyam atha sārūpyaṃ kasya keneti kathyatām |
    2. na tāvacchālaleyena bāhuleyādayaḥ samāḥ ||
    1. viśeṣarūpataḥ, ye 'pi tatsaṃsthānādibhiḥ samāḥ |
    2. śābaleya iveti syāt tatra buddhir na gaur iva ||
    1. śābaleyo 'yam iti vā bhrāntyā gaur iti nāsti dhīḥ |
    2. śābaleyasvarūpaṃ ca na gaur ity avatiṣṭhate ||
    1. tadanyeṣu hi gobuddhir na syāt susadṛśeṣv api |
    2. dṛśyate sā na cānyatra gorūpaṃ tatra vidyate ||
    1. na cānyo gauḥ prasiddho 'sti tatsādṛśyena dhīr bhāvet |
    2. na cāpi sa iti jñānaṃ sadṛśeṣv asti sarvadā ||
    1. sarvapuṃsām ato bhrāntir naiṣā bādhakavarjanāt |
    2. sarvajñānāni mithyā ca prasajyante 'tra kalpane ||
    1. viśeṣagrahaṇābhāvād eva gauḥ kaś ca kathyatām |
    2. babhūva yady asau pūrvam asmadādes tadagrahāt ||
    1. sādṛśyāvadhṛtir nāstīty ato godhīr na labhyate |
    2. na cāvayavasāmānyair vinā sādṛśyakalpanā ||
    1. sāmānyapratyayotpādo na viśeṣeṣu jāyate |
    2. vyaktitaś cātireko 'sya syān na veti vicārite ||
    1. sāmānyam eva sādṛśyaṃ bhaved vā vyaktimātrakam |
    2. tena nātyantabhinno 'rthaḥ sārūpyam iti varṇitam |
    3. granthe vindhyanivāsena bhrānteḥ sādṛśyam ucyate ||

{5,14 apohavāda APV}

    1. agonivṛttiḥ sāmānyaṃ vācyaṃ yaiḥ parikalpitam |
    2. gotvaṃ vastv eva tair uktam ago 'pohagirā sphuṭam ||
    1. bhāvāntaram abhāvo hi purastāt pratipāditaḥ |
    2. tatrāśvādinivṛttyātmā bhāvaḥ ka iti kathyatām ||
    1. neṣṭo 'sādhāraṇas tāvad viṣayo nirvikalpanāt |
    2. tathā ca śābaleyādeḥ, asāmānyaprasaṅgataḥ ||
    1. śābaleyādirūpaṃ hi na sāmānyaṃ parasparam |
    2. na vaikamitareṣāṃ vastatrānantārthatā bhavet ||
    1. na ca sākṣād viśeṣasya te 'pohyā iti yuktimat |
    2. na śābaleyavijñānam agovyāvṛttibandhanam ||
    1. nivṛttyā bāhuleyādes tadvijñānaṃ pravartate |
    2. kuryād agonivṛttiṃ cen nāpohetātmavad dhi tān ||
    1. tenāṃśenānapohaś ca svarūpeṇāpy apohanam |
    2. kalpyate ced virodhaḥ syāt samamākṣepavāraṇe ||
    1. tasmāt prātyātmikai rūpair ago 'poho na yujyate |
    2. samudāye 'pi naiteṣām agovyāvṛttisambhavaḥ ||
    1. sarvopalabdhau tadbuddhir vyāsajyaivaṃ pravartate |
    2. na pratyekaṃ bhaved eṣā, na samasteṣv aśaktitaḥ ||
    1. tasmāt sarveṣu yad rūpaṃ pratyekaṃ pariniṣṭhitam |
    2. gobuddhis tannimittā syād gotvād anyac ca nāsti tat ||
    1. nanu ca prāgabhāvādau sāmānyaṃ vastu neṣyate |
    2. sattaiva hy atra sāmānyam anutpattyādirūṣitā ||
    1. tām utpattyādyanusyūtāṃ satteti pratijānate |
    2. anyāpohānuviddhā tu saivābhāvaḥ pratīyate ||
    1. anityatvaṃ vināśākhyakriyāsāmānyam ucyate |
    2. abrāhmaṇatvaṃ kin tu syād bhinneṣu kṣattriyādiṣu ||
    1. puruṣatvaṃ catuḥsaṃstham, viśeṣeṣu ca nāstidhīḥ |
    2. sāmānyapratyayaś caiṣu pratyekam upajāyate ||
    1. tenātra brāhmaṇābhāvaḥ sāmānyaṃ syād avastu tat |
    2. gotvādāv api tenaiva sāmānyapratyayo bhavet ||
    1. kaiś cit tv atraikaśabdatvam akṣādāv iva kalpitam |
    2. jātitrayasya, naivaṃ tu sambhavatyaghaṭādiṣu ||
    1. nātra hy anantake bhede sādhāraṇyaṃ nirūpyate |
    2. tasmāt kriyāguṇāḥ ke cid dhetavo 'nanyavartinaḥ ||
    1. puruṣatvaṃ nañā caitad brāhmaṇebhyo nivartitam |
    2. cāturvarṇyaprasaktaṃ sad gamyate 'rthādibhir yathā ||
    1. yady apy avāntarā nāsti triṣu jātir vyavasthitā |
    2. nañsāmārthyān naratvaṃ tu tryādhāraṃ sampratīyate ||
    1. śabdasāmarthyabhedena varṇeṣu matibhinnatā |
    2. puṃstve tricaturādhāre paryudāsasvarūpataḥ ||
    1. dūrāntike kṣaṇe śaktir gṛdhravāyasacakṣuṣoḥ |
    2. yathā rūpe tathā puṃstve pumabrāhmaṇaśabdayoḥ ||
    1. brāhmaṇavyatiriktārthavṛtti puṃstvam itīdṛśam |
    2. vākyaṃ yatra pravarteta tatrābrāhmaṇadhīpade ||
    1. pārthivatvādisāmānyam evam evāghaṭādiṣu |
    2. ghaṭatvādivinirmuktaṃ viṣayaḥ sampratīyate ||
    1. asādhāraṇabhāvāc ca nañā śabdo viśeṣitaḥ |
    2. tāvanmātreṇa rahite sāmānye vyavatiṣṭhate ||
    1. viśeṣe pratiṣiddhe hi sāmānyaṃ yadanantaram |
    2. sāmānyākāṅkṣiṇaṃ śabdaṃ niruṇad dhi tadātmani ||
    1. prathamātikrame tasya kāraṇaṃ naiva vidyate |
    2. brāhmaṇatvād ato 'petaṃ naratvam avaśiṣyate ||
    1. vyudasya brāhmaṇatvaṃ ca nañi jāte viśeṣaṇe |
    2. naratvodasanaṃ yat tu kalpetāśrutam eva tat ||
    1. tasmād yasyaiva te bhedā niṣiddhyeraṃs tadarthataḥ |
    2. bhedāntarasthaṃ sāmānyam, loke 'py evaṃ pratīyate ||
    1. prasaṅginyāṃ ca tadbuddhau niṣedho 'rthād apīṣyate |
    2. tanmātrarahite cārthe sādṛśyāt tanmatir bhavet ||
    1. sādṛśyam eva vā vācyam iṣṭam abrāhmaṇādiṣu |
    2. tac cāvayavasāmānyād, vināpy etena lakṣyate ||
    1. kva cid vināpi sādṛśyāt sāhacaryādihetukā |
    2. nañyuktaśabdavṛttiḥ syād yathā vakṣyaty anīkṣaṇe ||
    1. īkṣaṇavyatiriktā hi kriyā tatrāpy apekṣitā |
    2. pratyāsatter na saṅkalpam atikramya pratīyate ||
    1. nāmadhātvarthayogī ca naiva nañ pratiṣedhakaḥ |
    2. vadato 'brāhmaṇādharmāv anyamātravirodhinau ||
    1. yatrāpy ākhyātasambandhāt pratiṣedhaḥ pratīyate |
    2. tatraudāsīnyavastv eva pratipattā 'valambate ||
    1. tasmād vastuny apohāḥ syuḥ, api cāvastukalpane |
    2. prāgntyebhyo viśeṣebhyo na kiñ cid vastu labhyate ||
    1. na cāntyair vyavahāro 'sti, śakyaṃ naiṣāṃ nirūpaṇam |
    2. apohaśabdavācyātha śūnyatānyaprakārikā ||
    1. tasyāṃ cāśvādibuddhīnātmāṃśagrahaṇaṃ bhavet |
    2. tatrānyāpohavācyatvaṃ mudhaivābhyupagamyate ||
    1. sāmānyaṃ vasturūpaṃ hi buddhyākāro bhaviṣyati |
    2. śabdārtho 'rthānapekṣo hi vṛthāpohaḥ prakalpitaḥ ||
    1. vasturūpā ca sā buddhiḥ śabdārtheṣūpajāyate |
    2. tena vastv eva kalpeta vācyaṃ buddhyanapohakam ||
    1. asaty api ca bāhye 'rthe vākyārthapratibhā tathā |
    2. padārthe 'pi tathaiva syāt kim apohaḥ prakalpyate ||
    1. buddhyantarād vyavacchedo na ca buddheḥ pratīyate |
    2. svarūpotpādamātrāc ca nānyam aṃśaṃ bibharti sā ||
    1. bhinnasāmānyavacanā viśeṣavacanāś ca ye |
    2. sarve bhaveyuḥ paryāyā yady apohasya vācyatā ||
    1. nanu bhedād apohānāṃ prasaṅgo 'yaṃ na yujyate |
    2. sāmānyāpohakḷptyā ced vastumātre samaṃ tava ||
    1. bhidyante mama vastutvāt sāmānyāni parasparam |
    2. asaṅkīrṇasvabhāvāni na caikatvaṃ vitanvate ||
    1. saṃsṛṣṭaikatvanānātvavikalparahitātmanām |
    2. avastutvād apohānāṃ tva syād bhinnatā katham ||
    1. yadi vā bhidyamānatvād vastvasādhāraṇāṃśavat |
    2. avastutve tv anānātvāt paryāyatvān na mucyate ||
    1. nanu cāpohyabhedena bhedo 'pohasya setsyati |
    2. na viśeṣaḥ svatas tasya parataś caupacārikaḥ ||
    1. tenaivādhārabhedenāpy asya bhedo na yujyate |
    2. na hi sambandhibhedena bhedo vastuny apīṣyate ||
    1. kim utāvastvasaṃsṛṣṭam anyataś cānivartitam |
    2. anavāptaviśeṣāṃśaṃ yat kim apy anirūpitam ||
    1. tasmād yathaiva bhede 'pi piṇḍānāṃ naiva bhidyate |
    2. tathaivāpohyabhede 'pi nāneko 'yaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
    1. bhede vā pratipiṇḍaṃ syād ago 'pohaḥ, tathā sati |
    2. sāmānyaṃ śābaleyāder iti neṣṭaṃ prasidhyati ||
    1. saṃsargiṇo 'pi cādhārā yaṃ na bhindanti rūpataḥ |
    2. apohyaiḥ sa bahirbhūtair bhidyetety atikalpanā ||
    1. agavyaśvātirekaḥ syād anaśvaś ca gavādhikaḥ |
    2. śeṣaṃ hastyādyapohyaṃ tu dvayor api na bhidyate ||
    1. tatraikabhedād bhedo 'stu bahvabhedād abhinnatā |
    2. bhūyasāṃ syāt sadharmatvam ity abhedaḥ prasajyate ||
    1. gauś ca hastyādyapohena nāśvarūpād viśeṣyate |
    2. karoti tadapohaṃ ced aikarūpyaṃ virudhyate ||
    1. sarvaśabdeṣu caikaikam apohyamatiricyate |
    2. tatrāsādhāraṇatvena tanmātrāpohyatā bhavet ||
    1. tato 'śvāpoharūpatvāt siṃhādiḥ sarva eva te |
    2. tannimittam ago 'pohaṃ bibhrad ucyeta gaur iti ||
    1. sarvāpoho yadīṣyeta, sa vaktavyaḥ kathaṃ punaḥ |
    2. yadi pratyekarūpeṇa nāpohyānantatā bhavet ||
    1. bhinnatvāc cāpy apohyānāṃ bhinno 'pohaḥ prasajyate |
    2. tatraikasmin bhavet piṇḍe 'nantajātisamanvayaḥ ||
    1. tato gaur iti sāmānyaṃ vācyam ekaṃ na sidhyati |
    2. jātyantaramatiś caiṣu bhavej jātyantareṣv iva ||
    1. samudāyātmanā nāpi bhaved eṣām apohyatā |
    2. samudāyo hi naikena vinā dharmeṇa jāyate ||
    1. nāpy ekadeśatā teṣām asti nāpy ekakālatā |
    2. vyatiriktaś ca saṅghātas teṣāṃ kaś cin na vidyate ||
    1. yadi tv avyatiriktaḥ syād ānanyaṃ tadavasthitam |
    2. yadi sāmānyarūpeṇa te 'pohyante, na vastutā ||
    1. kathaṃ vā vastv apohyeta, nābhāvo bhāvamṛcchati |
    2. apohyamāne cābhāve bhāva evāvaśiṣyate ||
    1. apohyabhedakḷptiś ca nābhāvābhedato bhavet |
    2. tadbhedo 'pohabhedāc cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam ||
    1. gosāmānyasya bhinnatvād agaur ity eṣa bhidyate |
    2. agaur ity asya bhedena gosāmānyaṃ ca bhidyate ||
    1. agāvo 'śvādayaś ca syus te 'py abhāvātmakāḥ punaḥ |
    2. karkādyapekṣayā te 'pi tathety evaṃ na gamyate ||
    1. kim apohyam, kva cāpohaḥ, gopiṇḍeṣv evam eva ca |
    2. tatra syād dvayam apy etadantyeṣu paramāṇuṣu ||
    1. na cāntyeṣu dvayor asti vyavahāro bhidāṃ prati |
    2. gavāśvaparamāṇūnāṃ viśeṣaś ca na vidyate ||
    1. svarūpajātisaṃsthānaparimāṇādilakṣaṇaḥ |
    2. kim apohyaṃ kva cāpohas tatrāpi na viśiṣyate ||
    1. na cāprasiddhasārūpyānapohaviṣayātmanā |
    2. śaktaḥ kaś cid api jñātuṃ gavādīnaviśeṣataḥ ||
    1. apohyān api cāśvādīnekadharmānvayād ṛte |
    2. na nirūpayituṃ śaktis tatrāpoho na siddhyati ||
    1. na cānvayavinirmukte pravṛttir liṅgaśabdayoḥ |
    2. tābhyāṃ ca na vināpoho na cāsādhāraṇe 'nvayaḥ ||
    1. apohaś cāpy aniṣpannaḥ sāhacaryaṃ kva dṛśyatām |
    2. tasminn adṛśyamāne ca na tayoḥ syāt pramāṇatā ||
    1. na cādarśanamātreṇa tābhyāṃ pratyāyanaṃ bhavet |
    2. sarvatraiva hy adṛṣṭatvāt pratyāyyaṃ nāvaśiṣyate ||
    1. athāsaty api sārūpye syād apohasya kalpanā |
    2. gavāśvayor ayaṃ kasmād ago 'poho na kalpyate ||
    1. śābaleyāc ca bhinnatvaṃ bāhuleyāśvayoḥ samam |
    2. sāmānyaṃ nānyadiṣṭaṃ cet kvāgo 'pohaḥ pravartatām ||
    1. indriyair nāpy ago 'pohaḥ prathamaṃ vyavasīyate |
    2. nānyatra śabdavṛttiś ca kiṃ dṛṣṭvā sa prayujyatām ||
    1. pūrvoktena prabandhena nānumāpy atra vidyate |
    2. sambandhānubhāvo 'py asya tena naivopapadyate ||
    1. nivṛttivācinaḥ śabdā na prasiddhāś ca yān prati |
    2. teṣām agor asiddhatvān na sāmānyanirākriyā ||
    1. agośabdābhidheyatvaṃ gamyatāṃ ca kathaṃ punaḥ |
    2. na dṛṣṭo yatra gośabdaḥ sambandhānubhavakṣaṇe ||
    1. ekasmāt tarhi gopiṇḍād yadanyat sarvam eva tat |
    2. bhaved apohyam ity evaṃ na sāmānyasya vācyatā ||
    1. siddhaś cāgaur apohyeta goniṣedhātmakaś ca saḥ |
    2. tatra gaur eva vaktavyo nañā yaḥ pratiṣidhyate ||
    1. sa ced agonivṛttyātmā bhaved anyonyasaṃśrayaḥ |
    2. siddhaś ced gaur apohyārthaṃ vṛthāpohaprakalpanā ||
    1. gavyasiddhe tv agaur nāsti tadabhāve ca gauḥ kutaḥ |
    2. nādhārādheyavṛttyādisambandhaś cāpy abhāvayoḥ ||
    1. na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu gamyate 'pohavat tayā |
    2. kathaṃ vā parikalpyeta sambandho vastvavastunoḥ ||
    1. svarūpasattvamātreṇa na ca kiñ cid viśeṣaṇam |
    2. svabuddhyā rajyate yena viśeṣyaṃ tad viśeṣaṇam ||
    1. na cāpy aśvādiśabdebho jāyate 'pohabodhanam |
    2. viśiṣṭabuddhir iṣṭeha na cājñātaviśeṣaṇā ||
    1. na cānyarūpam anyādṛk kuryāj jñānaṃ viśeṣaṇam |
    2. kathaṃ cānyādṛśe jñāte tad ucyeta viśeṣaṇam ||
    1. athānyathā viśeṣye 'pi syād viśeṣaṇakalpanā |
    2. tathā sati hi yatkiñcit prasajyeta viśeṣaṇam ||
    1. abhāvarūpagamye ca na viśeṣye 'sti vastutā |
    2. viśeṣitam apohena vastu vācyaṃ na te 'sty ataḥ ||
    1. yady apy apohanirmukte na vṛttiḥ śabdaliṅgayoḥ |
    2. yuktā tathāpi buddhis tu jñātur vastvavalambate ||
    1. na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu buddhau viparivarttate |
    2. na cāpi nirvikalpatvāt tasya yuktā viśeṣyatā ||
    1. śabdenāgamyamānaṃ ca viśeṣyam iti sāhasam |
    2. tena sāmānyam eṣṭavyaṃ viṣayo buddhiśabdayoḥ ||
    1. yadā cāśabdavācyatvān na vyaktīnām apohyatā |
    2. tadāpohyeta sāmānyaṃ tasyāpohāc ca vastutā ||
    1. nāpohyatvam abhāvānām abhāvābhāvavarjanāt |
    2. vyakto 'pohāntare 'pohas tasmāt sāmānyavastunaḥ ||
    1. abhāvasya ca yo 'bhāvaḥ sa cet tasmād vilakṣaṇaḥ |
    2. bhāva eva bhaven no ced gaur agaus te prasajyate ||
    1. yady apy aneṣu śabdeṣu vastunaḥ syād apohyatā |
    2. sacchabdasya tv abhāvākhyān nāpohyaṃ bhinnam iṣyate ||
    1. tatrāsato 'pi bhāvatvam itikleśo mahān bhavet |
    2. tadasiddhau na sattāsti na cāsattā prasidhyati ||
    1. na cāpi vāsanābhedād bhedaḥ sadrūpatāpi vā |
    2. apohānāṃ prakalpyeta, na hy avastuni vāsanā ||
    1. smṛtiṃ muktvā na cāsty asyāḥ śaktiyogaḥ kriyāntare |
    2. tasmān nānyādṛśe sārthe karoty anyādṛśīṃ matim ||
    1. bhavadbhiḥ śabdabhedo 'pi tannimitto na labhyate |
    2. na hy asādhāraṇaḥ śabdo vācakaḥ prāgadṛṣṭitaḥ ||
    1. bhinnatvāc cāpi naivaikā vāsanā taiḥ prakalpyate |
    2. na cāsti śabdavastv ekaṃ vāsanāṃ yat kariṣyati ||
    1. tatra śabdāntarāpohe sāmānye parikalpite |
    2. tathaivāvasturūpatvāc chabdabhedo na kalpyate ||
    1. vācakānāṃ yathā caivaṃ vācyavācakayor mithaḥ |
    2. na cāpy apohyabhedena bhedo 'stīty upapāditam ||
    1. nāgṛhītaś ca gamakaḥ śabdāpohaḥ kathañ cana |
    2. pratyakṣaṃ na ca tacchaktaṃ na ca sto liṅgavācakau ||
    1. yataḥ syād grahaṇaṃ tasya, liṅgādīnāṃ ca kalpane |
    2. na vyavastheti vācyaivaṃ vinā pratyakṣamūlataḥ ||
    1. na gamyagamakatvaṃ syād avastutvād apohayoḥ |
    2. bhavatpakṣe, yathā loke khapuṣpaśaśaśṛṅgayoḥ ||
    1. vṛṣṭimeghāsator dṛṣṭvā yady anaikāntikaḥ vadet |
    2. vastv evātrāpi matpakṣe bhavatpakṣe 'py adaḥ kutaḥ ||
    1. vidhirūpaś ca śabdārtho yena nābhyupagamyate |
    2. na bhaved vyatireko 'pi tasya tatpūrvako hy asau ||
    1. niṣedhadvayayogitvād asato yāpy abhāvatā |
    2. savastuke bhavet sāpi na tucche buddhyasambhavāt ||
    1. nanu yuktyānayaivāyaṃ vastunāpi na bhidyate |
    2. apohas tena doṣo 'tra pūrvokto na bhaviṣyati ||
    1. siddham evaṃ madiṣṭaṃ syāt, naivānyā gatir asti hi |
    2. abhāve vastubuddhir vā yad vā vastunyabhāvadhīḥ ||
    1. tatrābhāvātmakatve syān nirnimittaiva vastudhīḥ |
    2. vastuny abhāvabodhas tu sidhyaty anyam apekṣya tu ||
    1. apohamātravācyatvaṃ yadi cābhyupagamyate |
    2. nīlotpalādiśabdeṣu śabalārthābhidhāyiṣu ||
    1. viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvasāmānādhikaraṇyayoḥ |
    2. na siddhiḥ, na hy anīlatvavyudāse 'nutpalacyutiḥ ||
    1. nāpi tatretaras tasmān na viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇe |
    2. śabdayor nāpi te syātām abhidheyānapekṣayoḥ ||
    1. sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca na bhinnatvād apohayoḥ |
    2. arthataś caitad iṣyeta kīdṛśyādheyatā tayoḥ ||
    1. na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu gamyate 'nyac ca nāsti te |
    2. agamyamānam aikārthyaṃ śabdayoḥ kvopayujyate ||
    1. athānyāpohavad vastu vācyam ity abhidhīyate |
    2. tatrāpi paratantratvād vyāptiḥ śabdena durbalā ||
    1. khaṇḍe bhinnavyapohyatvād yathaiva madhurādibhiḥ |
    2. śuklādivyāptyabhāvena nākṣepo na viśeṣaṇam ||
    1. tathaivāsadvyudāsāṃśāvacchinnārthāvadhāraṇe |
    2. nāghaṭādinivṛttyaṃśavyāptiḥ śabdāt pratīyate ||
    1. vyāptiś ced artharūpeṇa sattayaivaṃ hi sā bhavet |
    2. na ghaṭatvādimān arthaḥ kaś cin na vyāpyate tayā ||
    1. na ca vastutayā vyāptis tayā śabdasya vāryate |
    2. pratītiṃ prati tulyas tu vyāpāro vastvavastunoḥ ||
    1. nirbhāgo 'pi hi vastvātmā śabdair bhāgena gamyate |
    2. na hi sacchabdavijñānād ghaṭādyarthaḥ pratīyate ||
    1. tenānākṣepadoṣo 'sti, bhāktadoṣaś ca vidyate |
    2. viśeṣaṇatvān mukhyatvam apohasya hi jātivat ||
    1. tasmāt tadvati gauṇatvān nābhidheyatvasambhavaḥ |
    2. avastutvān na mukhyaś cet, na syād evaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||
    1. bhedāś cāpohavantaḥ syus teṣāṃ cāvācyatoditā |
    2. ānantyavyabhicārābhyām, anyo nāsti tv apohavān ||
    1. nāpohavattvam anyad dhi bhedāpohāntare 'sti te |
    2. tac cāpi kalpyamānaṃ syād abhāvo bhāva eva vā ||
    1. vastu cej jātir eva syād avastutve 'pi pūrvavat |
    2. sambandho vaiṣa kalpyeta tasya ceṣṭā na vācyatā ||
    1. na caiko 'pohavān artho vartate 'rthāntare kva cit |
    2. tasmād api na sāmānyaṃ vācyaṃ na ca viśeṣaṇam ||
    1. nātmanyavidyamānatvād viśeṣo 'pohasūcakaḥ |
    2. tasmān na tair viśeṣyatvaṃ prakṛṣṭatvena nīlavat ||
    1. arthākṣepo 'pi nāsty eva sandehāl liṅgaliṅgivat |
    2. na sāmānyātmanāpohas tair vinā na ca siddhyati ||
    1. evam eva tv anākṣepaḥ syād apohena vastunaḥ |
    2. yataḥ śaśaviṣāṇe 'pi tadapohasya sambhavaḥ ||
    1. liṅgasaṃkhyādisambandho na vāpohasya vidyate |
    2. vyakter avyapadeśyatvāt taddvāreṇāpi nāsty asau ||
    1. na hy asādhāraṇatvena sāpohenāpi gamyate |
    2. na cāpy agamyamānasya vastunaḥ syād viśeṣyatā ||
    1. liṅgasaṃkhyādyapohānāṃ nopakāraḥ svarūpataḥ |
    2. vastunaś copakāryatvaṃ kathaṃ śabdaiḥ pratīyate ||
    1. na vinānupalabdhyā ca syād abhāvamatiḥ kva cit |
    2. na cābhāvaprameyatvaṃ gotvāder iha gamyate ||
    1. ākhyāteṣu ca nānyasya nivṛttiḥ sampratīyate |
    2. na paryudāsarūpaṃ hi niṣedhyaṃ tatra vidyate ||
    1. na neti hy ucyamāne 'pi niṣedhasya niṣedhanam |
    2. pacatīty aniṣiddhaṃ tu svarūpeṇāvatiṣṭhate ||
    1. sādhyatvapratyayaś cātra tathābhūtādirūpaṇam |
    2. niṣpannatvād apohasya nirnimittaṃ prasajyate ||
    1. vidhyādāv artharāśau ca nānyāpohanidarśanam |
    2. nañaś cāpi nañā yuktād apohaḥ kīdṛśo bhavet ||
    1. cādīnām api nañyogo naivāstīty anapohanam |
    2. vākyārtho 'nyanivṛttiś ca vyapadeṣṭuṃ na śakyate ||
    1. ananyāpohaśabdādau vācyaṃ na ca nirūpyate |
    2. prameyajñeyaśabdāder apohyaṃ kuta eva tu ||
    1. apohyakalpanāyāṃ tu varaṃ vastv eva kalpitam |
    2. jñānākāraniṣedhāc ca nāntarārthābhidheyatā ||
    1. na cāpy apohyatā, tasmān nāpohas teṣu sidhyati |
    2. evam ityādiśabdānāṃ na vāpohyaṃ nirūpyate ||
    1. virodhitvena bhedānām apoho yadi kalpyate |
    2. virodho 'pohatas tatra virodhāc cāpy apohanam ||
    1. na sāmānyāpahāritvaṃ vidhirūpeṇa tatra te |
    2. palaśādīn apohyāto vṛkṣaṃ harati śiṃśapā ||
    1. sāmānyādyanapohaś ca nāvirodhena kalpyate |
    2. na hi śabdasvarūpāṇāṃ syād viruddhāviruddhatā ||
    1. na ca vastusvarūpeṇa tasya śabdair asaṅgateḥ |
    2. prāk śabdavyāpṛter nāpi sāpohānāṃ pratīyate ||
    1. anyenānavabuddhe 'rthe sadā śabdaḥ pravartate |
    2. sāmānyātmakatā tasya kena rūpeṇa gamyate ||
    1. śabdānurūpataś cet syād anyāpohanirūpaṇam |
    2. bhinnatvād vṛkṣatarvāder apohaḥ kena vāryate ||
    1. śabdaspṛṣṭer vināpoho na ca liṅgena gamyate |
    2. na viruddhāviruddhatvaṃ tasya liṅgāc ca sidhyati ||
    1. adṛṣṭatvād vyudāsas tu purastād eva vāritaḥ |
    2. sāmānyaśabdo bhedena neṣyate vācakātmanā ||
    1. vyudāsas tatra durvāraḥ, kathañ cid dṛṣṭatā punaḥ |
    2. brāhmaṇe kṣattriyasyāpi paryudāsaḥ prasajyate ||
    1. ākāṅkṣaṇādathātyāgas tulyo dravyakriyādiṣu |
    2. vṛkṣeṇāto 'napohaḥ syāt tiṣṭhatyāder asaṃśayam ||
    1. puruṣasya tathā rājño vyudāse na viśeṣyatā |
    2. avyudāsatvapakṣe ca syān nīlotpalatulyatā ||
    1. vṛkṣatvapārthivadravyasajjñeyeṣu yaducyate |
    2. prātilomyānulomyena vidhau sarvārthabodhanam ||
    1. tadayuktam, na sarvo hi śabdaḥ sarvatra dṛśyate |
    2. deśāvibhāgato vṛttir netrasyāpi rasādiṣu ||
    1. grāhakatvena vṛttis tu pratijāti vyavasthitā |
    2. cakṣurādivad evātra saṅkaro na bhaviṣyati ||
    1. nivṛttaceṣṭe śabde ca vyāptyavyāptikṛtaṃ punaḥ |
    2. sattvāder bodhakatvaṃ syād ekanyūnātirekataḥ ||
    1. tavaiva doṣaḥ syād eṣa viśeṣe yasya varttate |
    2. sāmānyaśabdaḥ, vācyānāṃ bhedo nāpy asti vastutaḥ ||
    1. api caikatvanityatvapratyekasamavāyitāḥ |
    2. nirupākhyeṣv apoheṣu kurvato 'sūtrakaḥ paṭaḥ ||
    1. tasmād yeṣv eva śabdeṣu nañyogas teṣu kevalam |
    2. bhaved anyanivṛttyaṃśaḥ svātmaivānyatra gamyate ||
    1. jñeyārthānyānapohatvaṃ pramāṅgatvāt tvagādivat |
    2. yenoktaṃ tasya nañyuktaiḥ śabdaiḥ syād vyabhicāritā ||
    1. pakṣīkuryād yadā sarvāṃs tadāthāvītahetubhiḥ |
    2. anaikānto virodhaś ca sarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ ||
    1. nāpohata itīdaṃ ca kārakatvena ced bhavet |
    2. kevalāpohabuddher vā tataḥ syāt siddhasādhyatā ||
    1. athānyāpohavatyarthe vṛttir nāstīti sādhyate |
    2. tataḥ prāk pakṣabādhaḥ syād gotve 'thāśvādyabhāvataḥ ||
    1. sādhyahīnaś ca dṛṣṭāntaś cakṣurādy api tasya hi |
    2. varttate 'pohavatyeva taṃ yady api na budhyate ||
    1. athānyāpohanirbhāsā na buddhiḥ siddhasādhanam |
    2. apoharūpam apy etad vastv ity eva hi gamyate ||
    1. athāpohanimittāsya vṛttir arthe niṣidhyate |
    2. vyatirekāṅgateṣṭatvāt punaḥ prāk pakṣabādhanam ||
    1. anumāne tathā caitad ity anaikāntiko bhavet |
    2. sandehabādhajātena pratyakṣeṇāpi cetasā ||
    1. viruddhatā ca hetoḥ syāt, śabdaḥ śrotrādivad yataḥ |
    2. ātmāntaḥ karaṇākāśaiḥ svavācitvaṃ jahāti vāḥ ||
    1. vidhirūpapravṛttir vā śabdo 'pohena varttate |
    2. anumānāṅgabhūtatvād yathaiva pratiṣedhakaḥ ||
    1. jātiṃ vā na bravīty eṣa vyaktiṃ vā tadviśeṣitām |
    2. pramāyām aṅgabhūtatvāt tvakśrotrādi yathaiva ca ||
    1. evaṃ sādhanamārgeṇa vācyāvācyanirūpaṇā |
    2. nāvātiṣṭhata ity atra kathyate lokavartmanā ||

{5,15 vanavāda VAV}

    1. sāsnādibhir viśiṣṭatvam ākṛter ucyate katham |
    2. yadāvayavisambandhi gotvaṃ nāvayave sthitam ||
    1. ekāvayavisambandhas teṣāṃ gotvena vidyate |
    2. tenāsādhāraṇatvāt te syur gotvasyopalakṣaṇam ||
    1. piṇḍe sattādijātīnāṃ bahvīnāṃ samavetatā |
    2. tābhyo viśiṣyate gotvaṃ sāsnādibhir asaṃśayam ||
    1. na caite vyañjakās tasya guṇavad vā viśeṣaṇam |
    2. tathā hi nāgṛhīteṣu teṣu syād gotvabodhanam ||
    1. teṣāṃ ca vyañjakaiḥ svaiḥ syāt punargrahaṇakalpanā |
    2. tathā satyanavasthā syāt na syād gotvāvadhāraṇam ||
    1. sarveṣu ca gṛhīteṣu sāsnādiṣu bhavenmatiḥ |
    2. gotve, na caiṣu sarveṣu yugapad buddhisambhavaḥ ||
    1. tasmāt sadbhāvamātreṇa mahattvādau yathaiva dhīḥ |
    2. kriyate 'vayavaiḥ piṇḍe tathā jātiguṇādiṣu ||
    1. yady evam agṛhīteṣu teṣu kiṃ sā na jāyate |
    2. taddeśavyatirekeṇa grāhyaṃ yena na vidyate ||
    1. gṛhyamāṇe tu gotvādau nāntarīyakahetukaḥ |
    2. sāsnādeḥ kasya cid bodhas taddeśatvena jāyate ||
    1. tadanatyantabhedād vā tadviśiṣṭeti kīrtyate |
    2. bādhaḥ parānumānasya na pratyakṣeti bodhyate ||
    1. pareṣāṃ sādhanaṃ hy atra nākṛtiḥ piṇḍataḥ pṛthak |
    2. taddhīhānāv avijñānāt paṅktiyūthavanādivat ||
    1. sarvatra lokasiddhatvān na vācyaṃ sādhanaṃ svayam |
    2. niṣedhatāṃ pareṣāṃ tu virodhaṃ lokato vadet ||
    1. visaṃvādo na dṛśyeta yadi pratyakṣatākṛteḥ |
    2. pramāṇe 'pi visaṃvādāt tārkikeṣu kuto nv iyam ||
    1. rūpādāv api teṣāṃ hi pratyakṣatvena sammate |
    2. vivādaḥ, naiva lokas tu jātau vipratipadyate ||
    1. vyavahārā hi dṛśyante sāmānyārthanibandhanāḥ |
    2. dadhitakrādidānādau kauṇḍinyabrāhmaṇādiṣu ||
    1. ākṛtir jātir evātra saṃsthānaṃ na prakalpyate |
    2. na hi vāyvagniśabdādau kiñ cit saṃsthānam iṣyate ||
    1. anyadanyac ca saṃsthānaṃ pratipiṇḍaṃ pratīyate |
    2. saṃyogātmakatāyāṃ tu vibhāgeṣu vinaśyati ||
    1. atha saṃsthānasāmānyam, aśvādāv api tatsamam |
    2. na gotvena vinā hy etad vyavacchinnaṃ pratīyate ||
    1. sarvapratikṛtīnāṃ ca saṃsthāne saty apīdṛśe |
    2. na gotvādimatir dṛṣṭā, tasmāj jātiḥ pṛthak tataḥ ||
    1. rucakādiṣu sāmānyaṃ rucakatvād yudāhṛtam |
    2. bhinneṣu caiṣu sāmānyaṃ suvarṇatvaṃ pratīyate ||
    1. vardhamānakabhaṅge ca rucakaḥ kriyate yadā |
    2. tadā pūrvārthinaḥ śokaḥ prītiś cāpy uttarārthinaḥ ||
    1. hemārthinas tu mādhyasthaṃ tasmād vastu trayātmakam |
    2. notpādasthitibhaṅgānām abhāve syān matitrayam ||
    1. na nāśena vinā śoko notpādena vinā sukham |
    2. sthityā vinā na mādhyasthyam, tena sāmānyanityatā ||
    1. mudgamāṣatilādau ca yatra bhedo na lakṣyate |
    2. tatraikabuddhinirgrāhyā jātir indriyagocaraḥ ||
    1. ārād dṛṣṭe ca puruṣe sandeho brāhmaṇādiṣu |
    2. na syād yadi na gṛhyeta sāmānyaṃ cakṣurādinā ||
    1. tasyopalakṣaṇaṃ cāpi kva cit kena cid iṣyate |
    2. rūpādīnāṃ viśeṣeṇa deśakālādy apekṣayā ||
    1. suvarṇaṃ bhidyate rūpāt tāmratvāder asaṃśayam |
    2. tailād ghṛtaṃ vilīnaṃ ca gandhena ca rasena ca ||
    1. bhasmapracchādito vahniḥ sparśanenopalabhyate |
    2. aśvatvādau ca dūrasthe niścayo jāyate svanaiḥ ||
    1. saṃsthānena ghaṭatvādi brāhmaṇatvādi yonitaḥ |
    2. kva cid ācārataś cāpi samyag rājānupālitāt ||
    1. pratyekasamavetatvaṃ dṛṣṭatvān na virotsyate |
    2. tathā saty api nānātvaṃ naikabuddher bhaviṣyati ||
    1. na hi sambandhibhedena svarūpaikatvabādhanam |
    2. vibhutvāvayavābhāvau pratipādyau ca śabdavat ||
    1. yathā ca vyatirekaiva dṛśyamānā punaḥ punaḥ |
    2. kālabhede 'py abhinnaiva jātir bhinnāśrayā satī ||
    1. kārtsyāvayavaśo vṛttiḥ praṣṭuṃ jātau na yujyate |
    2. na hi bhedavinirmukte kārtsnyabhāgavikalpanam ||
    1. tasmād vyaktiṣu jātīnāṃ vṛttir astīti gamyate |
    2. viśeṣāvasarābhāvāt tanmātraivāvatiṣṭhate ||
    1. yā cāvayavaśo vṛttiḥ sraksūtrādiṣu dṛśyate |
    2. bhūtakaṇṭhaguṇādeś ca pratipiṇḍaṃ samāptitaḥ ||
    1. tatrāvayavayogitvam avibhutvaṃca kāraṇam |
    2. ākṛtes tadabhāvena na prasaktamado dvayam ||
    1. na ca dvaividhyam eveti vṛtter asti niyāmakam |
    2. trividhāpi hi dṛṣṭatvāt sambhaved dvividhā yathā ||
    1. itaratra na dṛṣṭaṃ cet sragādiṣv api tatsamam |
    2. naiva hy anyonyatulyatvaṃ tayor nāpy anayā saha ||
    1. na hy anyasminn adṛṣṭatvād vahner auṣṇyaṃ praṇaśyati |
    2. na cānumānagamyeyaṃ vāñched yena nidarśanam ||
    1. svarūpataś ca dṛṣṭāyā vṛtter na pararūpataḥ |
    2. nirākriyopapadyeta tadviśeṣam apaśyatām ||
    1. aṅgāṅgāsambhavāc cāpi yā pradhānanirākriyā |
    2. sā 'yuktaiva, anumānena pratyakṣajñānabādhanāt ||
    1. tasmād asambhavo yasya tanmātrasyaiva bādhanam |
    2. yuktaṃ na tāvatānyo 'pi sambhavan bādham arhati ||
    1. tena vaiśeṣikoktāpi jātiḥ sarvagatā satī |
    2. vyajyate yatra piṇḍena varṇavat tatra gṛhyate ||
    1. tasmāt piṇḍeṣu gobuddhir ekagotvanibandhanā |
    2. gavābhāsaikarūpyābhām ekagopiṇḍabuddhivat ||
    1. na śābaleyād gobuddhis tato 'nyālambanāpi vā |
    2. tadabhāve 'pi sadbhāvād ghaṭe pārthivabuddhivat ||
    1. pratyekasamavetārthaviṣayā vāpi gomatiḥ |
    2. pratyekaṃ kṛtsnabuddhitvāt pratyekavyaktibuddhivat ||
